def _ensure(import_name: str, pip_name: Optional[str] = None) -> None:
    try:
        __import__(import_name)
    except ImportError:
        subprocess.check_call([sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", pip_name or import_name, "-q"])

_ensure("telegram", "python-telegram-bot>=20.0")
_ensure("aiohttp")

# ========================= CONFIGURATION =========================
class Config:
    BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
    DOWNLOAD_DIR = BASE_DIR / "downloads"
    OUTPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "generated_code"
    CONFIG_DIR = BASE_DIR / ".bot_config"
    CONFIG_FILE = CONFIG_DIR / "config.json"
    EXPO_DIR = BASE_DIR / "expo-control-panel"
    REPAIR_LOG_DIR = BASE_DIR / ".repair_logs"
    PROGRESSION_DIR = BASE_DIR / ".progression"

    @classmethod
    def setup_directories(cls) -> None:
        for path in [cls.DOWNLOAD_DIR, cls.OUTPUT_DIR, cls.CONFIG_DIR,
                      cls.REPAIR_LOG_DIR, cls.PROGRESSION_DIR]:
            path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    @classmethod
    def load(cls) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        cls.setup_directories()
        if cls.CONFIG_FILE.exists():
            try:
                return json.loads(cls.CONFIG_FILE.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
            except Exception:
                return {}
        return {}

    @classmethod
    def save(cls, config: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        cls.setup_directories()
        cls.CONFIG_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(config, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False), encoding="utf-8")

    @classmethod
    def _get(cls, key: str, default: Any = None) -> Any:
        return cls.load().get(key, default)

    @classmethod
    def _set(cls, key: str, value: Any) -> None:
        config = cls.load()
        config[key] = value
        cls.save(config)

    @classmethod
    def get_telegram_token(cls) -> Optional[str]:
        token = os.environ.get("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN") or cls._get("telegram_token")
        if token and ":" in token and len(token) > 30:
            return token.strip()
        return None

    @classmethod
    def set_telegram_token(cls, token: str) -> None:
        cls._set("telegram_token", token.strip())

    @classmethod
    def get_glm_api_key(cls) -> Optional[str]:
        key = os.environ.get("GLM_API_KEY") or cls._get("glm_api_key")
        return key.strip() if key else None

    @classmethod
    def set_glm_api_key(cls, api_key: str) -> None:
        cls._set("glm_api_key", api_key.strip())

    @classmethod
    def get_glm_model(cls) -> str:
        return cls._get("glm_model", "glm-4.6")

    @classmethod
    def set_glm_model(cls, model: str) -> None:
        cls._set("glm_model", model)

    @classmethod
    def get_glm_endpoint(cls) -> str:
        return cls._get("glm_endpoint", "https://api.z.ai/api/coding/paas/v4/chat/completions")

    @classmethod
    def set_glm_endpoint(cls, endpoint: str) -> None:
        cls._set("glm_endpoint", endpoint)

    @classmethod
    def get_github_repo(cls) -> Optional[str]:
        value = cls._get("github_repo")
        return value.strip() if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip() else None

    @classmethod
    def set_github_repo(cls, repo_url: str) -> None:
        cls._set("github_repo", repo_url.strip())

    @classmethod
    def get_owner_user_id(cls) -> Optional[int]:
        value = cls._get("owner_user_id")
        return int(value) if value not in (None, "") else None

    @classmethod
    def set_owner_user_id(cls, user_id: int) -> None:
        cls._set("owner_user_id", int(user_id))

    @classmethod
    def get_auto_repair_enabled(cls) -> bool:
        return cls._get("auto_repair_enabled", True)

    @classmethod
    def set_auto_repair_enabled(cls, enabled: bool) -> None:
        cls._set("auto_repair_enabled", enabled)

    @classmethod
    def get_max_repair_iterations(cls) -> int:
        return cls._get("max_repair_iterations", 3)

    @classmethod
    def set_max_repair_iterations(cls, max_iter: int) -> None:
        cls._set("max_repair_iterations", max(1, min(10, int(max_iter))))

    @classmethod
    def get_expert_mode(cls) -> bool:
        return cls._get("expert_mode", False)

    @classmethod
    def set_expert_mode(cls, enabled: bool) -> None:
        cls._set("expert_mode", enabled)


# ========================= HELPERS =========================
def mask_secret(value: Optional[str], head: int = 8, tail: int = 4) -> str:
    if not value:
        return "not set"
    if len(value) <= head + tail:
        return "*" * len(value)
    return f"{value[:head]}...{value[-tail:]}"


def truncate(text: str, limit: int) -> str:
    if len(text) <= limit:
        return text
    return text[: limit - 3] + "..."


def safe_ext_from_language(language: str) -> str:
    mapping = {
        "python": "py", "py": "py", "javascript": "js", "js": "js",
        "typescript": "ts", "ts": "ts", "bash": "sh", "shell": "sh",
        "sh": "sh", "json": "json", "html": "html", "css": "css",
        "java": "java", "c": "c", "cpp": "cpp", "csharp": "cs",
        "go": "go", "rust": "rs", "sql": "sql", "xml": "xml",
        "yaml": "yaml", "yml": "yml", "markdown": "md", "md": "md",
        "text": "txt", "txt": "txt", "ruby": "rb", "swift": "swift",
        "kotlin": "kt", "zig": "zig", "lua": "lua",
    }
    return mapping.get(language.lower(), "txt")


def extract_text_preview(file_path: Path, limit: int = 2000) -> Optional[str]:
    suffix = file_path.suffix.lower()
    text_like = {
        ".txt", ".py", ".js", ".ts", ".json", ".md", ".html", ".css", ".csv",
        ".yml", ".yaml", ".xml", ".sql", ".log", ".ini", ".env", ".java", ".c",
        ".cpp", ".cs", ".go", ".rs", ".rb", ".swift", ".kt", ".zig", ".lua",
    }
    if suffix in text_like:
        try:
            return file_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="ignore")[:limit]
        except Exception:
            return None
    if suffix == ".pdf":
        try:
            import pypdf
        except Exception:
            return None
        try:
            reader = pypdf.PdfReader(str(file_path))
            parts: List[str] = []
            for page in reader.pages[:3]:
                extracted = page.extract_text() or ""
                if extracted.strip():
                    parts.append(extracted)
                if sum(len(x) for x in parts) >= limit:
                    break
            return "\n".join(parts)[:limit] if parts else None
        except Exception:
            return None
    return None


async def send_html_chunks(message, title: str, body: str, chunk_size: int = 3800) -> None:
    escaped = html.escape(body)
    full = f"<b>{html.escape(title)}</b>\n\n{escaped}"
    if len(full) <= 4000:
        await message.reply_text(full, parse_mode="HTML")
        return
    chunks: List[str] = []
    current = ""
    for line in full.splitlines(True):
        if len(current) + len(line) > chunk_size:
            chunks.append(current)
            current = line
        else:
            current += line
    if current:
        chunks.append(current)
    for chunk in chunks:
        await message.reply_text(chunk, parse_mode="HTML")

# ========================= 12 LOOP PROBLEMS =========================
LOOP_PROBLEMS = {
    1: """📚 PROBLEMA 1: Numere de la 1 la 10

Cerință: Afișează numerele de la 1 la 10 folosind un for loop.

```python
for i in range(1, 11):
    print(i, end=" ")
print()
```

✅ Explicație: range(1, 11) generează numerele de la 1 la 10 (11 exclus). end=" " păstrează totul pe o linie.""",

    2: """📚 PROBLEMA 2: Adunare până la 'done'

Cerință: Citește numere de la utilizator până scrie 'done', apoi afișează suma.

```python
total = 0
while True:
    user_input = input("Introdu un număr (sau 'done'): ")
    if user_input.lower() == 'done':
        break
    try:
        total += float(user_input)
    except ValueError:
        print("Input invalid. Introdu un număr.")
print(f"Suma: {total}")
```

✅ Explicație: while True cu break - pattern clasic pentru input repetat cu condiție de ieșire.""",

    3: """📚 PROBLEMA 3: Tabla înmulțirii pentru 7

Cerință: Afișează tabla înmulțirii cu 7 (de la 7x1 la 7x10).

```python
num = 7
for i in range(1, 11):
    print(f"{num} x {i} = {num * i}")
```

✅ Explicație: Un singur for loop cu f-string pentru formatare curată.""",

    4: """📚 PROBLEMA 4: Fiecare al doilea element din listă

Cerință: Parcurge lista și afișează elementele de pe pozițiile pare (0, 2, 4...).

```python
my_list = ['apple', 'banana', 'cherry', 'date', 'elderberry']
for i in range(0, len(my_list), 2):
    print(my_list[i])
```

✅ Explicație: range(0, len, 2) - al treilea parametru e pasul (step=2).""",

    5: """📚 PROBLEMA 5: Triunghi cu asteriscuri

Cerință: Afișează un triunghi de înălțime 5 din '*'.

```python
height = 5
for i in range(1, height + 1):
    print('*' * i)
```

✅ Explicație: La fiecare iterație, '*' * i multiplică stringul. Simplu și elegant.""",

    6: """📚 PROBLEMA 6: Numere prime între 2 și 50

Cerință: Găsește toate numerele prime între 2 și 50.

```python
import math
primes = []
for num in range(2, 51):
    is_prime = True
    for divisor in range(2, int(math.sqrt(num)) + 1):
        if num % divisor == 0:
            is_prime = False
            break
    if is_prime:
        primes.append(num)
print(primes)
```

✅ Explicație: Nested loop - verificăm divizori până la sqrt(num). Break oprește la prima găsire.""",

    7: """📚 PROBLEMA 7: Lungime string + uppercase dacă len > 5

Cerință: Pentru fiecare string, afișează lungimea. Dacă > 5 caractere, transformă în uppercase.

```python
strings = ["hello", "python", "code", "programming", "loop", "artificial"]
for s in strings:
    length = len(s)
    if length > 5:
        print(f"{s} ({length}) -> {s.upper()}")
    else:
        print(f"{s} ({length})")
```

✅ Explicație: Loop + condiție în interior - pattern foarte comun în procesare de date.""",

    8: """📚 PROBLEMA 8: Intersecția a două liste fără set

Cerință: Găsește elementele comune între două liste, FĂRĂ a folosi set().

```python
list1 = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7]
list2 = [5, 6, 7, 8, 9]
intersection = []
for item1 in list1:
    for item2 in list2:
        if item1 == item2 and item1 not in intersection:
            intersection.append(item1)
print(intersection)
```

✅ Explicație: Nested loop cu check duplicat - soluția manuală a intersecției.""",

    9: """📚 PROBLEMA 9: Bubble Sort

Cerință: Implementează Bubble Sort cu optimizare (early exit dacă sorted).

```python
def bubble_sort(arr):
    n = len(arr)
    for i in range(n):
        swapped = False
        for j in range(0, n - i - 1):
            if arr[j] > arr[j + 1]:
                arr[j], arr[j + 1] = arr[j + 1], arr[j]
                swapped = True
        if not swapped:
            break
    return arr

numbers = [64, 34, 25, 12, 22, 11, 90]
print(bubble_sort(numbers.copy()))
```

✅ Explicație: Clasicul bubble sort cu swapped flag - O(n) pe array deja sortat.""",

    10: """📚 PROBLEMA 10: Palindrom ignorând semnele și literele mari

Cerință: Verifică dacă un string e palindrom ignorând spații, punctuație și case.

```python
import re

def is_palindrome(s):
    cleaned = re.sub(r'[^a-zA-Z0-9]', '', s).lower()
    left, right = 0, len(cleaned) - 1
    while left < right:
        if cleaned[left] != cleaned[right]:
            return False
        left += 1
        right -= 1
    return True

print(is_palindrome("A man, a plan, a canal: Panama"))
```

✅ Explicație: Two-pointer cu while loop - curățăm stringul apoi verificăm simetria.""",

    11: """📚 PROBLEMA 11: Primele 10 numere Fibonacci

Cerință: Generează și afișează primele 10 numere din șirul lui Fibonacci.

```python
n = 10
a, b = 0, 1
for _ in range(n):
    print(a, end=" ")
    a, b = b, a + b
print()
```

✅ Explicație: Tuple unpacking pentru swap simultan - pattern Pythonic elegant.""",

    12: """📚 PROBLEMA 12: Longest IncrApking Subsequence (LIS)

Cerință: Găsește lungimea celei mai lungi subsecvențe crescătoare.

```python
def longest_incrApking_subsequence(arr):
    if not arr:
        return 0
    dp = [1] * len(arr)
    for i in range(len(arr)):
        for j in range(i):
            if arr[j] < arr[i]:
                dp[i] = max(dp[i], dp[j] + 1)
    return max(dp)

print(longest_incrApking_subsequence([10, 9, 2, 5, 3, 7, 101, 18]))
```

✅ Explicație: Dynamic programming cu nested loop - O(n²). Există și O(n log n) cu binary search.""",
}


# ========================= AUTO-REPAIR ENGINE =========================
class RepairResult:
    def __init__(self, original: str, repaired: str, issues: List[str],
                 iterations: int, success: bool):
        self.original = original
        self.repaired = repaired
        self.issues = issues
        self.iterations = iterations
        self.success = success


class AutoRepairEngine:
    """Self-healing code engine - detects and fixes errors automatically."""

    SYSTEM_PROMPT_DETECT = """You are an expert code reviewer and debugger. Analyze the given code for:
1. SYNTAX ERRORS - missing colons, brackets, parentheses, indentation
2. LOGIC ERRORS - off-by-one, wrong conditions, infinite loops, wrong variable usage
3. IMPORT ERRORS - missing imports, wrong module names
4. TYPE ERRORS - wrong types passed to functions, incompatible operations
5. RUNTIME ERRORS - division by zero, index out of bounds, None dereference
6. SECURITY ISSUES - injection, hardcoded secrets, unsafe operations
7. EDGE CASES - empty input, None values, boundary conditions
8. STYLE/IDIOM ISSUES - non-idiomatic patterns for the language
9. RESOURCE LEAKS - unclosed files, connections, missing cleanup
10. CONCURRENCY ISSUES - race conditions, deadlocks (if applicable)

For EACH issue found, provide:
- SEVERITY: CRITICAL|HIGH|MEDIUM|LOW
- CATEGORY: one of the 10 categories above
- LINE: approximate line number or section
- DESCRIPTION: what's wrong
- FIX: the exact fix needed

Output format - strictly JSON array:
[
  {"severity": "CRITICAL", "category": "SYNTAX ERRORS", "line": 5, "description": "...", "fix": "..."},
  ...
]

If code is perfect, output: []
"""

    SYSTEM_PROMPT_FIX = """You are an expert programmer. Given code with known issues, produce the FIXED version.
Rules:
1. Fix ALL listed issues - do not skip any
2. Do NOT change functionality - only fix bugs
3. Do NOT add unnecessary features
4. Preserve the original structure as much as possible
5. Add minimal comments only where the fix is non-obvious
6. Output ONLY the fixed code, no explanations
7. Keep the same language and style
8. Ensure the fixed code compiles/runs without errors
"""

    SYSTEM_PROMPT_VALIDATE = """You are a strict code validator. Given code, determine if it would compile and run correctly.
Consider:
- Syntax correctness
- Import availability
- Type consistency
- Edge case handling
- Resource management

Output strictly one word: PASS or FAIL
If FAIL, output: FAIL: one sentence rApkon
"""

    def __init__(self, glm_service: Any) -> None:
        self.glm = glm_service

    def _log_repair(self, user_id: int, result: RepairResult) -> None:
        log_dir = Config.REPAIR_LOG_DIR
        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        log_file = log_dir / f"repair_{user_id}_{timestamp}.json"
        log_data = {
            "timestamp": timestamp,
            "user_id": user_id,
            "iterations": result.iterations,
            "success": result.success,
            "issues_count": len(result.issues),
            "issues": result.issues[:20],
            "original_length": len(result.original),
            "repaired_length": len(result.repaired),
        }
        try:
            log_file.write_text(json.dumps(log_data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False), encoding="utf-8")
        except Exception:
            pass

    async def detect_issues(self, code: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        raw = await self.glm.chat(
            f"Analyze this code:\n\n```\n{code}\n```",
            system_prompt=self.SYSTEM_PROMPT_DETECT,
            temperature=0.1,
        )
        try:
            cleaned = raw.strip()
            if cleaned.startswith("```"):
                cleaned = re.sub(r"^```(?:json)?\s*\n?", "", cleaned)
                cleaned = re.sub(r"\n?```\s*$", "", cleaned)
            issues = json.loads(cleaned)
            if isinstance(issues, list):
                return issues
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, AttributeError):
            pass
        # Fallback: parse text for issue indicators
        issues = []
        for line in raw.splitlines():
            if any(s in line.upper() for s in ["CRITICAL", "HIGH", "ERROR", "FAIL", "BUG", "WRONG"]):
                issues.append({
                    "severity": "HIGH",
                    "category": "DETECTED",
                    "line": 0,
                    "description": line.strip(),
                    "fix": "Review manually",
                })
        return issues

    async def fix_code(self, code: str, issues: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:
        issues_text = "\n".join(
            f"- [{i.get('severity','?')}] {i.get('category','?')}: {i.get('description','')} -> Fix: {i.get('fix','')}"
            for i in issues
        )
        prompt = f"Code to fix:\n```\n{code}\n```\n\nIssues found:\n{issues_text}"
        result = await self.glm.chat(prompt, system_prompt=self.SYSTEM_PROMPT_FIX, temperature=0.1)
        # Extract code block
        match = re.search(r"```[a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*\n(.*?)```", result, re.DOTALL)
        if match:
            return match.group(1).strip()
        return result.strip()

    async def validate_code(self, code: str) -> Tuple[bool, str]:
        result = await self.glm.chat(
            f"Validate this code:\n\n```\n{code}\n```",
            system_prompt=self.SYSTEM_PROMPT_VALIDATE,
            temperature=0.0,
        )
        result = result.strip().upper()
        if result.startswith("PASS"):
            return True, "Code validated successfully"
        rApkon = result.replace("FAIL:", "").strip() if "FAIL" in result else "Unknown issue"
        return False, rApkon

    async def repair(self, code: str, user_id: int) -> RepairResult:
        max_iter = Config.get_max_repair_iterations()
        current_code = code
        all_issues: List[str] = []

        for iteration in range(1, max_iter + 1):
            issues = await self.detect_issues(current_code)
            if not issues:
                validated, rApkon = await self.validate_code(current_code)
                if validated:
                    return RepairResult(
                        original=code, repaired=current_code,
                        issues=all_issues, iterations=iteration, success=True,
                    )
                all_issues.append(f"Iter {iteration}: Validation - {rApkon}")
                if iteration == max_iter:
                    break
                continue

            # Filter critical and high issues only for repair focus
            critical = [i for i in issues if i.get("severity", "").upper() in ("CRITICAL", "HIGH")]
            if not critical:
                validated, _ = await self.validate_code(current_code)
                if validated:
                    return RepairResult(
                        original=code, repaired=current_code,
                        issues=all_issues, iterations=iteration, success=True,
                    )
                critical = issues[:3]  # Fix top 3 if no critical

            for i in critical:
                all_issues.append(
                    f"Iter {iteration}: [{i.get('severity','?')}] {i.get('category','?')}: {i.get('description','')}"
                )

            current_code = await self.fix_code(current_code, critical)

        # Final validation attempt
        validated, _ = await self.validate_code(current_code)
        result = RepairResult(
            original=code, repaired=current_code,
            issues=all_issues, iterations=max_iter,
            success=validated,
        )
        self._log_repair(user_id, result)
        return result
