        ),
        PromptClassifier.FORENSICS: (
            "You are an expert digital forensics practitioner. Provide methodology, "
            "tool recommendations, artifact locations, and timeline reconstruction. "
            "Maintain chain of custody considerations."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.SOCIAL_ENGINEERING: (
            "You are a social engineering awareness expert. Provide attack scenario analysis, "
            "detection techniques, and comprehensive awareness training content. "
            "Focus on defense and organizational resilience."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.NETWORK_ATTACK: (
            "You are an expert network security analyst. Provide attack technique analysis, "
            "detection methods, and network hardening recommendations. "
            "Include IDS/IPS rules where applicable."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.WEB_EXPLOIT: (
            "You are an expert web security researcher. Provide vulnerability analysis, "
            "proof-of-concept methodology, and secure coding fixes. "
            "Reference OWASP guidelines and include WAF rules."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.SYSTEM_EXPLOIT: (
            "You are an expert system security researcher. Provide privilege escalation "
            "technique analysis, detection methods, and system hardening procedures. "
            "Include configuration audit checklists."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.ADVANCED_PERSISTENT: (
            "You are an expert threat intelligence analyst. Provide APT group analysis, "
            "TTP breakdowns, detection opportunities, and hunting queries. "
            "Focus on organizational defense improvement."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.EDUCATIONAL_SECURITY: (
            "You are an expert cybersecurity educator. Provide structured learning paths, "
            "hands-on exercises with solutions, and clear explanations. "
            "Build from fundamentals to advanced topics progressively."
        ),
        PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN: (
            "You are an expert assistant. Analyze the request carefully and provide "
            "the most helpful, accurate, and complete response possible. "
            "Ask clarifying questions if the intent is ambiguous."
        ),
    }

    @classmethod
    def classify(cls, prompt: str) -> PromptClassifier:
        lower = prompt.lower()
        scores: Dict[PromptClassifier, int] = {}
        for classifier, keywords in cls.CLASSIFICATION_KEYWORDS.items():
            score = sum(1 for kw in keywords if kw in lower)
            if score > 0:
                scores[classifier] = score
        if scores:
            return max(scores, key=scores.get)
        # Check for question patterns
        if any(lower.startswith(q) for q in ["what", "how", "why", "explain", "tell"]):
            return PromptClassifier.EXPLANATION
        if any(lower.startswith(a) for a in ["fix", "debug", "repair", "error"]):
            return PromptClassifier.REPAIR
        if any(lower.startswith(c) for c in ["write", "create", "generate", "build", "make", "implement"]):
            return PromptClassifier.CODE_GENERATION
        if any(lower.startswith(a) for a in ["analyze", "review", "check", "inspect"]):
            return PromptClassifier.ANALYSIS
        return PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN

    @classmethod
    def get_system_prompt(cls, classifier: PromptClassifier) -> str:
        return cls.SYSTEM_PROMPTS.get(classifier, cls.SYSTEM_PROMPTS[PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN])

    @classmethod
    def get_routing_info(cls, prompt: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
        classifier = cls.classify(prompt)
        return {
            "category": classifier.value,
            "system_prompt": cls.get_system_prompt(classifier),
            "handling": "processed_as_expert_request",
        }


# ========================= EXPERT PROGRESSION SYSTEM =========================
class ProgressionTracker:
    """Tracks skill progression across all domains and tiers."""

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self.progression_dir = Config.PROGRESSION_DIR

    def _user_file(self, user_id: int) -> Path:
        return self.progression_dir / f"user_{user_id}.json"

    def _load_user(self, user_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        f = self._user_file(user_id)
        if f.exists():
            try:
                return json.loads(f.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
            except Exception:
                pass
        return {
            "tier": "intermediate",
            "xp": 0,
            "tasks_completed": 0,
            "repairs_handled": 0,
            "prompts_processed": {},
            "languages_used": [],
            "errors_auto_fixed": 0,
            "streak": 0,
            "last_activity": None,
            "achievements": [],
            "skill_scores": {},
        }

    def _save_user(self, user_id: int, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        try:
            self._user_file(user_id).write_text(
                json.dumps(data, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False), encoding="utf-8"
            )
        except Exception:
            pass

    def record_task(self, user_id: int, category: str, language: str = "unknown",
                    had_errors: bool = False, errors_fixed: int = 0) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        data = self._load_user(user_id)
        data["tasks_completed"] += 1
        data["xp"] += self._xp_for_category(category, had_errors)
        data["last_activity"] = datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds")
        data["repairs_handled"] += errors_fixed
        data["errors_auto_fixed"] += errors_fixed

        # Track prompt categories
        prompts = data.get("prompts_processed", {})
        prompts[category] = prompts.get(category, 0) + 1
        data["prompts_processed"] = prompts

        # Track languages
        if language != "unknown" and language not in data.get("languages_used", []):
            data["languages_used"] = data.get("languages_used", [])
            data["languages_used"].append(language)

        # Skill scores
        scores = data.get("skill_scores", {})
        scores[category] = min(100, scores.get(category, 0) + self._skill_increment(category, had_errors))
        data["skill_scores"] = scores

        # Check tier upgrade
        data["tier"] = self._calculate_tier(data)
        data["achievements"] = self._check_achievements(data)

        # Streak
        today = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
        last = data.get("last_activity", "")[:10] if data.get("last_activity") else ""
        if last == today:
            pass
        elif last == (datetime.now() - __import__("datetime").timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d"):
            data["streak"] = data.get("streak", 0) + 1
        else:
            data["streak"] = 1

        self._save_user(user_id, data)
        return data

    def _xp_for_category(self, category: str, had_errors: bool) -> int:
        base_xp = {
            "intermediate": 10, "explanation": 15, "adaptability": 20,
            "advanced": 35, "expert": 50,
        }.get(category, 10)
        return base_xp + (5 if had_errors else 0)

    def _skill_increment(self, category: str, had_errors: bool) -> int:
        base = {"intermediate": 5, "explanation": 4, "adaptability": 6,
                "advanced": 8, "expert": 10}.get(category, 3)
        return base + (2 if had_errors else 0)

    def _calculate_tier(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        xp = data.get("xp", 0)
        tasks = data.get("tasks_completed", 0)
        if xp >= 2000 and tasks >= 30:
            return "expert"
        if xp >= 800 and tasks >= 15:
            return "advanced"
        if xp >= 300 and tasks >= 8:
            return "adaptability"
        if xp >= 100 and tasks >= 4:
            return "explanation"
        return "intermediate"

    def _check_achievements(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[str]:
        achievements = list(data.get("achievements", []))
        checks = [
            ("first_code", data["tasks_completed"] >= 1, "📝 First Code Generated"),
            ("loop_master", data["tasks_completed"] >= 10, "🔄 Loop Master (10 tasks)"),
            ("polyglot", len(data.get("languages_used", [])) >= 3, "🌐 Polyglot (3+ languages)"),
            ("self_healer", data.get("errors_auto_fixed", 0) >= 5, "🔧 Self-Healer (5 auto-fixes)"),
            ("streak_3", data.get("streak", 0) >= 3, "🔥 3-Day Streak"),
            ("streak_7", data.get("streak", 0) >= 7, "🔥🔥 7-Day Streak"),
            ("advanced", data["tier"] in ("advanced", "expert"), "⭐ Advanced Tier"),
            ("expert", data["tier"] == "expert", "👑 Expert Tier"),
            ("security_aware", "security_test" in data.get("prompts_processed", {}), "🛡️ Security Aware"),
            ("full_stack", all(c in data.get("prompts_processed", {})
                              for c in ["code_generation", "analysis", "repair"]),
             "🏗️ Full Stack Thinker"),
            ("bug_hunter", data.get("errors_auto_fixed", 0) >= 20, "🐛 Bug Hunter (20 fixes)"),
            ("centurion", data["tasks_completed"] >= 100, "💯 Centurion (100 tasks)"),
        ]
        for key, condition, label in checks:
            if condition and label not in achievements:
                achievements.append(label)
        return achievements

    def get_stats(self, user_id: int) -> str:
        data = self._load_user(user_id)
        tier_emoji = {"intermediate": "🌱", "explanation": "📖", "adaptability": "🧩",
                      "advanced": "⭐", "expert": "👑"}.get(data["tier"], "🌱")
        lines = [
            f"{tier_emoji} <b>Tier:</b> {data['tier'].upper()}",
            f"📊 <b>XP:</b> {data['xp']}",
            f"✅ <b>Tasks:</b> {data['tasks_completed']}",
            f"🔧 <b>Auto-fixes:</b> {data.get('errors_auto_fixed', 0)}",
            f"🔥 <b>Streak:</b> {data.get('streak', 0)} days",
            f"🌐 <b>Languages:</b> {', '.join(data.get('languages_used', [])) or 'none yet'}",
        ]
        if data.get("achievements"):
            lines.append(f"\n🏆 <b>Achievements:</b>")
            for a in data["achievements"][-8:]:
                lines.append(f"   {a}")
        if data.get("skill_scores"):
            lines.append(f"\n📈 <b>Skills:</b>")
            for skill, score in sorted(data["skill_scores"].items(), key=lambda x: -x[1])[:6]:
                bar_len = score // 5
                bar = "█" * bar_len + "░" * (20 - bar_len)
                lines.append(f"   {skill}: [{bar}] {score}%")
        return "\n".join(lines)


# ========================= LOOP PROBLEM GENERATOR =========================
class LoopProblemGenerator:
    """Generates loop problems for any language and tier combination."""

    @staticmethod
    def generate_loop_code(language: Language, pattern_name: str,
                           params: Dict[str, str]) -> str:
        template_set = LOOP_TEMPLATES.get(pattern_name, {})
        template = template_set.get(language)
        if not template:
            return f"// Pattern '{pattern_name}' not available for {language.value}"
        try:
            return template.format(**params)
        except KeyError as e:
            return f"// Missing parameter: {e}"

    @staticmethod
    def get_random_problem(language: Language = Language.PYTHON,
                           tier: ModelTier = ModelTier.INTERMEDIATE) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        problems = TIER_TRAINING.get(tier, [])
        if not problems:
            problems = TIER_TRAINING[ModelTier.INTERMEDIATE]
        problem = random.choice(problems)
        pattern_templates = LOOP_TEMPLATES.get(problem["pattern"], {})
        code_template = pattern_templates.get(language, "// Template not available")

        # Generate sample params
        sample_params = {
            "start": "0", "end": "10", "array": "items",
            "outer": "5", "inner": "5", "condition": "x > 0",
            "update": "x -= 1", "exit_condition": "x <= 0",
            "body": "print(item)", "transform": "item * 2",
            "initial": "0", "operation": "acc + item",
        }

        return {
            "title": problem["title"],
            "description": problem["description"],
            "language": language.value,
            "tier": tier.value,
            "pattern": problem["pattern"],
            "constraints": problem["constraints"],
            "template": code_template,
            "sample_params": sample_params,
        }

    @staticmethod
    def generate_multi_language_example(pattern_name: str,
                                         params: Dict[str, str]) -> Dict[str, str]:
        result = {}
        for lang in Language:
            template_set = LOOP_TEMPLATES.get(pattern_name, {})
            template = template_set.get(lang)
            if template:
                try:
                    result[lang.value] = template.format(**params)
                except KeyError:
                    result[lang.value] = f"// Missing params for {lang.value}"
        return result


# ========================= GLM SERVICE =========================
class GLMService:
    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self.refresh()

    def refresh(self) -> None:
        self.api_key = Config.get_glm_api_key()
        self.endpoint = Config.get_glm_endpoint()
        self.model = Config.get_glm_model()

    def is_configured(self) -> bool:
        return bool(self.api_key and len(self.api_key) > 10)

    async def chat(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None,
                   temperature: float = 0.3) -> str:
        self.refresh()
        if not self.is_configured():
            return "❌ GLM API key nu este configurat. Folosește /api CHEIA_TA"

        import aiohttp
        messages: List[Dict[str, str]] = []
        if system_prompt:
            messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system_prompt})
        messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})

        payload = {
            "model": self.model,
            "messages": messages,
            "temperature": temperature,
            "max_tokens": 4096,
        }
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
        }

        try:
            timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=120)
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as session:
                async with session.post(self.endpoint, headers=headers, json=payload) as resp:
                    text = await resp.text()
                    if resp.status != 200:
                        return f"❌ API Error ({resp.status}): {truncate(text, 500)}"
                    data = json.loads(text)
                    return data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]
        except Exception as exc:
            return f"❌ Eroare GLM: {exc}"

    async def analyze_files(self, files: List[Dict[str, Any]],
                            instruction: str = "") -> str:
        prompt_parts = [
            "Analizează fișierele de mai jos și explică pe scurt ce conțin, ce tip de date au și ce se poate face util cu ele.",
            "Dacă lipsesc date importante, spune clar ce nu se poate deduce.",
            "",
            "FIȘIERE:",
        ]
        for f in files:
            prompt_parts.append(f"- Nume: {f['name']}")
            prompt_parts.append(f"  Tip: {f.get('mime_type', 'necunoscut')}")
            prompt_parts.append(f"  Mărime: {f.get('size', 0)} bytes")
            preview = f.get("content_preview")
            if preview:
                prompt_parts.append("  Preview:")
                prompt_parts.append(truncate(preview, 1200))
            prompt_parts.append("")
        if instruction:
            prompt_parts.append(f"CERINȚĂ SUPLIMENTARĂ: {instruction}")
        return await self.chat("\n".join(prompt_parts))

    async def generate_code(self, instruction: str, files: List[Dict[str, Any]],
                            context: str = "", system_prompt_override: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
        prompt_parts = [
            "Ești un expert software engineer la nivel mondial.",
            f"CERINȚĂ: {instruction}",
            "",
            "FIȘIERE DISPONIBILE:",
        ]
        for f in files:
            prompt_parts.append(f"- {f['name']} ({f.get('mime_type', 'necunoscut')}, {f.get('size', 0)} bytes)")
            if f.get("content_preview"):
                prompt_parts.append("  Preview:")
                prompt_parts.append(truncate(f["content_preview"], 1200))
        if context:
            prompt_parts.append("")
            prompt_parts.append("CONTEXT DIN ANALIZA ANTERIOARĂ:")
            prompt_parts.append(truncate(context, 2000))
        prompt_parts.extend([
            "",
            "REGULI:",
            "1. Dă cod complet și rulabil.",
            "2. Include importurile necesare.",
            "3. Include comentarii scurte unde contează.",
            "4. Include handling de erori de bază.",
            "5. Pune răspunsul în bloc markdown cu limbajul corect.",
            "6. Gândește-te la edge cases și tratează-le.",
            "7. Folosește cele mai bune practici pentru limbajul respectiv.",
        ])
        system = system_prompt_override or "You are a world-class software engineer. Produce production-ready code."
        return await self.chat("\n".join(prompt_parts), system_prompt=system)

    async def universal_prompt(self, raw_prompt: str, context: str = "") -> str:
        routing = PromptEngine.get_routing_info(raw_prompt)
        system = routing["system_prompt"]
        prompt = raw_prompt
        if context:
            prompt = f"Context anterior:\n{truncate(context, 1500)}\n\nCerere curentă:\n{raw_prompt}"
        return await self.chat(prompt, system_prompt=system, temperature=0.3)


# ========================= GITHUB / EXPO HELPERS =========================
@dataclass
class JobResult:
    ok: bool
    message: str


def _run_command(command: List[str], cwd: Optional[Path] = None) -> Tuple[int, str, str]:
    proc = subprocess.run(command, cwd=str(cwd) if cwd else None,
                          capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=120)
    return proc.returncode, proc.stdout.strip(), proc.stderr.strip()


def deploy_to_github() -> JobResult:
    repo = Config.get_github_repo()
    if not repo:
        return JobResult(False, "Nu există repo configurat. Folosește /setrepo URL_REPO")
    code, _, _ = _run_command(["git", "--version"])
    if code != 0:
        return JobResult(False, "Git nu este instalat pe sistem.")
    project_dir = Config.BASE_DIR
    if not (project_dir / ".git").exists():
        _run_command(["git", "init"], cwd=project_dir)
    _run_command(["git", "remote", "remove", "origin"], cwd=project_dir)
    _run_command(["git", "remote", "add", "origin", repo], cwd=project_dir)
    _run_command(["git", "add", "."], cwd=project_dir)
    commit_msg = f"WHOAMISEC AI auto deploy {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}"
    _run_command(["git", "commit", "-m", commit_msg, "--allow-empty"], cwd=project_dir)
    code, out, err = _run_command(["git", "push", "-u", "origin", "main"], cwd=project_dir)
    if code == 0:
        return JobResult(True, f"Push reușit către {repo}\n{out}")
    # Try master branch
    code2, out2, err2 = _run_command(["git", "push", "-u", "origin", "master"], cwd=project_dir)
    if code2 == 0:
        return JobResult(True, f"Push reușit către {repo} (master)\n{out2}")
    return JobResult(False, f"Push eșuat. Verifică autentificarea Git.\n{truncate(err or out, 1200)}")


def scaffold_expo_project() -> JobResult:
    expo_dir = Config.EXPO_DIR
    expo_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    assets_dir = expo_dir / "assets"
    assets_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

    package_json = {
        "name": "WHOAMISEC AI-bot-control", "version": "1.0.0", "private": True,
        "main": "node_modules/expo/AppEntry.js",
        "scripts": {"start": "expo start", "android": "expo start --android",
                     "ios": "expo start --ios", "web": "expo start --web"},
        "dependencies": {"expo": "~50.0.0", "expo-status-bar": "~1.11.1",
                          "react": "18.2.0", "react-native": "0.73.6", "axios": "^1.6.8"},
    }
    app_json = {
        "expo": {"name": "WHOAMISEC AI Bot Control", "slug": "WHOAMISEC AI-telegram-control",
                  "version": "1.0.0", "orientation": "portrait",
                  "userInterfaceStyle": "dark",
                  "android": {"package": "com.WHOAMISEC AI.botcontrol"},
                  "ios": {"bundleIdentifier": "com.WHOAMISEC AI.botcontrol"}, "web": {}},
    }
    app_js = r'''import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { StyleSheet, Text, View, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, ScrollView, Alert } from 'react-native';
import { StatusBar } from 'expo-status-bar';
import axios from 'axios';

export default function App() {
  const [botToken, setBotToken] = useState('');
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState([]);
  const [customCmd, setCustomCmd] = useState('');

  const addLog = (msg) => {
    const stamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
    setLogs(prev => [`${stamp} ${msg}`, ...prev].slice(0, 50));
  };

  const sendCommand = async (cmd) => {
    if (!botToken) { Alert.alert('Lipsește tokenul', 'Introdu Telegram Bot Token.'); return; }
    try {
      const r = await axios.get(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${botToken}/getUpdates`);
      const items = r.data.result || [];
      if (!items.length) { addLog('⚠️ Nu există chat recent.'); return; }
      const chatId = items[items.length - 1].message.chat.id;
      await axios.post(`https://api.telegram.org/bot${botToken}/sendMessage`, { chat_id: chatId, text: cmd });
      addLog(`✅ Trimis: ${cmd}`);
    } catch (e) { addLog(`❌ Eroare: ${e.message}`); }
  };

  const quickButtons = [
    { label: '📊 Status', cmd: '/status' },
    { label: '📁 Files', cmd: '/files' },
    { label: '🧹 Clear', cmd: '/clear' },
    { label: '📈 Progress', cmd: '/progress' },
    { label: '🔧 Repair On', cmd: '/autorepair on' },
    { label: '🔧 Repair Off', cmd: '/autorepair off' },
    { label: '👑 Expert Mode', cmd: '/expert on' },
    { label: '🌱 Normal Mode', cmd: '/expert off' },
  ];

  return (
    <View style={styles.container}>
      <StatusBar style="light" />
      <Text style={styles.title}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI Control</Text>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} placeholder="Telegram Bot Token"
        placeholderTextColor="#7f8c8d" value={botToken} onChangeText={setBotToken} />
      <View style={styles.quickGrid}>
        {quickButtons.map((b, i) => (
          <TouchableOpacity key={i} style={styles.quickBtn} onPress={() => sendCommand(b.cmd)}>
            <Text style={styles.quickBtnText}>{b.label}</Text>
          </TouchableOpacity>
        ))}
      </View>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} placeholder="Custom command..."
        placeholderTextColor="#7f8c8d" value={customCmd}
        onChangeText={setCustomCmd}
        onSubmitEditing={() => { if (customCmd.trim()) { sendCommand(customCmd.trim()); setCustomCmd(''); } }} />
      <Text style={styles.logTitle}>📋 Loguri</Text>
      <ScrollView style={styles.logBox}>
        {logs.map((log, i) => <Text key={i} style={styles.logText}>{log}</Text>)}
      </ScrollView>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: { flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#0b1020', paddingTop: 50, paddingHorizontal: 12 },
  title: { color: '#60a5fa', fontSize: 24, fontWeight: '700', marginBottom: 12, textAlign: 'center' },
  input: { backgroundColor: '#111827', color: 'white', borderRadius: 8, padding: 10, marginBottom: 8,
           borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#374151' },
  quickGrid: { flexDirection: 'row', flexWrap: 'wrap', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 8 },
  quickBtn: { backgroundColor: '#1e3a5f', padding: 8, borderRadius: 6, width: '48%', marginBottom: 6,
              alignItems: 'center' },
  quickBtnText: { color: '#93c5fd', fontSize: 12, fontWeight: '600' },
  logTitle: { color: '#9ca3af', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 4 },
  logBox: { backgroundColor: '#111827', borderRadius: 8, padding: 8, flex: 1 },
  logText: { color: '#d1fae5', fontSize: 11, marginBottom: 4, fontFamily: 'monospace' },
});
'''

    (expo_dir / "package.json").write_text(json.dumps(package_json, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    (expo_dir / "app.json").write_text(json.dumps(app_json, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    (expo_dir / "App.js").write_text(app_js, encoding="utf-8")

    return JobResult(True,
        f"Expo project creat în: {expo_dir}\n\n"
        f"Comenzi:\n  cd {expo_dir}\n  npm install\n  npx expo start\n\n"
        f"Include 8 quick-action buttons + custom command input + log viewer.")


# ========================= MAIN WHOAMISEC AI BOT =========================
class WHOAMISEC AIBot:
    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self.glm = GLMService()
        self.repair_engine = AutoRepairEngine(self.glm)
        self.progression = ProgressionTracker()
        self.sessions: Dict[int, Dict[str, Any]] = {}

    def is_owner(self, user_id: int) -> bool:
        owner = Config.get_owner_user_id()
        return owner is not None and int(owner) == int(user_id)

    def maybe_claim_owner(self, user_id: int) -> bool:
        owner = Config.get_owner_user_id()
        if owner is None:
            Config.set_owner_user_id(user_id)
            return True
        return False

    def ensure_session(self, user_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if user_id not in self.sessions:
            self.sessions[user_id] = {
                "files": [], "context": "", "generated": [],
                "last_response": "", "last_category": None,
                "conversation_history": [],
            }
        return self.sessions[user_id]

    async def require_owner(self, update: Update) -> bool:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        if self.is_owner(user_id):
            return True
        await update.message.reply_text("⛔ Comanda este disponibilă doar pentru owner-ul botului.")
        return False

    # ---- COMMAND HANDLERS ----

    async def start(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        self.ensure_session(user_id)
        claimed = self.maybe_claim_owner(user_id)
        lines = [
            "🤖 <b>WHOAMISEC AI Bot v4.0</b> - Expert Edition",
            "",
            "⚙️ <b>Configurare:</b>",
            "/api CHEIE - setează cheia GLM",
            "/status - status complet",
            "/model - schimbă modelul GLM",
            "/endpoint - schimbă endpoint-ul",
            "",
            "📁 <b>Fișiere & Cod:</b>",
            "/analyze [cerință] - analizează fișiere uploadate",
            "/code cerință - generează cod cu auto-repair",
            "/files - listează fișierele sesiunii",
            "/clear - resetează sesiunea",
            "",
            "🔄 <b>Auto-Repair & Progression:</b>",
            "/autorepair on|off - activează/deactivează auto-repair",
            "/repairiter N - setează max repair iterations (1-10)",
            "/progress - statistici & progres",
            "/expert on|off - mod expert",
            "",
            "📚 <b>Loop Training:</b>",
            "/p1 ... /p12 - 12 probleme cu loop-uri",
            "/loop LANG TIER - problemă random (ex: /loop python expert)",
            "/loops LANG PATTERN - exemplu în 13 limbi",
            "",
            "🚀 <b>Deploy & Mobile:</b>",
            "/setrepo URL - setează repo GitHub",
            "/deploy - push pe GitHub",
            "/expo - generează proiect Expo control panel",
            "",
            "💬 <b>Universal Prompt:</b>",
            "Orice mesaj text → procesat automat prin PromptEngine",
            "(code, security, analysis, repair, orice tip)",
        ]
        if claimed:
            lines += ["", "✅ Setat automat ca owner."]
        if not self.glm.is_configured():
            lines += ["", "🔑 Lipsește cheia GLM → /api CHEIA_TA"]
        await update.message.reply_text("\n".join(lines), parse_mode="HTML")

    async def help_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        await self.start(update, context)

    async def status(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)
        key = Config.get_glm_api_key()
        repo = Config.get_github_repo()
        owner = Config.get_owner_user_id()
        repair_on = Config.get_auto_repair_enabled()
        repair_iter = Config.get_max_repair_iterations()
        expert = Config.get_expert_mode()

        text = (
            f"<b>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI Bot v4.0 - Status</b>\n\n"
            f"🔧 <b>Config:</b>\n"
            f"  Telegram token: {'✅' if Config.get_telegram_token() else '❌'}\n"
            f"  GLM key: {'✅' if key else '❌'} ({html.escape(mask_secret(key))})\n"
            f"  GLM model: <code>{html.escape(Config.get_glm_model())}</code>\n"
            f"  GLM endpoint: <code>{html.escape(truncate(Config.get_glm_endpoint(), 50))}</code>\n"
            f"  GitHub repo: <code>{html.escape(repo or 'not set')}</code>\n"
            f"  Owner: <code>{owner if owner else 'not set'}</code>\n\n"
            f"🛠️ <b>Auto-Repair:</b>\n"
            f"  Status: {'✅ ON' if repair_on else '❌ OFF'}\n"
            f"  Max iterations: {repair_iter}\n\n"
            f"👑 <b>Expert Mode:</b> {'✅ ON' if expert else '❌ OFF'}\n\n"
            f"📁 <b>Sesiune:</b>\n"
            f"  Fișiere: {len(session.get('files', []))}\n"
            f"  Generate: {len(session.get('generated', []))}\n"
            f"  Last category: {session.get('last_category') or 'none'}\n\n"
            f"📂 <b>Direcții:</b>\n"
            f"  Downloads: <code>{html.escape(str(Config.DOWNLOAD_DIR))}</code>\n"
            f"  Output: <code>{html.escape(str(Config.OUTPUT_DIR))}</code>\n"
            f"  Repair logs: <code>{html.escape(str(Config.REPAIR_LOG_DIR))}</code>\n"
            f"  Progression: <code>{html.escape(str(Config.PROGRESSION_DIR))}</code>"
        )
        await update.message.reply_text(text, parse_mode="HTML")

    async def api_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        args = context.args
        if not args:
            current = Config.get_glm_api_key()
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"Cheie curentă: {mask_secret(current)}\n\n"
                f"Setare: /api CHEIA_TA\nȘtergere: /api clear"
            )
            return
        if args[0].lower() == "clear":
            Config.set_glm_api_key("")
            self.glm.refresh()
            await update.message.reply_text("✅ Cheia GLM ștearsă.")
            return
        api_key = args[0].strip()
        if len(api_key) < 10:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Cheia pare prea scurtă.")
            return
        Config.set_glm_api_key(api_key)
        self.glm.refresh()
        msg = await update.message.reply_text("🔍 Testez cheia GLM...")
        result = await self.glm.chat("Reply with exactly: OK", temperature=0)
        if "OK" in result.strip().upper()[:5]:
            await msg.edit_text("✅ Cheia GLM salvată și testată cu succes.")
        else:
            await msg.edit_text(f"⚠️ Cheia salvată dar test neconcludent:\n{truncate(result, 500)}")

    async def model_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        current = Config.get_glm_model()
        keyboard = [
            [InlineKeyboardButton("glm-4.6", callback_data="model:glm-4.6")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("glm-4.5-air", callback_data="model:glm-4.5-air")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("glm-4-plus", callback_data="model:glm-4-plus")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("glm-5.1", callback_data="model:glm-5.1")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("Cancel", callback_data="model:cancel")],
        ]
        await update.message.reply_text(f"Model curent: {current}",
                                         reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(keyboard))

    async def endpoint_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        current = Config.get_glm_endpoint()
        keyboard = [
            [InlineKeyboardButton("Coding API", callback_data="endpoint:coding")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("General API", callback_data="endpoint:general")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton("Cancel", callback_data="endpoint:cancel")],
        ]
        await update.message.reply_text(f"Endpoint curent:\n{current}",
                                         reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(keyboard))

    async def autorepair_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not context.args:
            state = Config.get_auto_repair_enabled()
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"Auto-repair: {'✅ ON' if state else '❌ OFF'}\n\n"
                f"/autorepair on - activează\n/autorepair off - deactivează"
            )
            return
        val = context.args[0].lower()
        if val in ("on", "true", "1", "yes"):
            Config.set_auto_repair_enabled(True)
            await update.message.reply_text("✅ Auto-repair activat. Codul generat va fi verificat și reparat automat.")
        elif val in ("off", "false", "0", "no"):
            Config.set_auto_repair_enabled(False)
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Auto-repair dezactivat.")
        else:
            await update.message.reply_text("Folosește: /autorepair on sau /autorepair off")

    async def repairiter_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not context.args:
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"Max repair iterations: {Config.get_max_repair_iterations()}\n\n"
                f"/repairiter N (1-10)"
            )
            return
        try:
            n = int(context.args[0])
            Config.set_max_repair_iterations(n)
            await update.message.reply_text(f"✅ Max repair iterations setat la {n}")
        except ValueError:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Valoare invalidă. Folosește un număr între 1 și 10.")

    async def expert_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not context.args:
            state = Config.get_expert_mode()
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"Expert mode: {'✅ ON' if state else '❌ OFF'}\n\n"
                f"/expert on - activează (prompts mai detaliate)\n"
                f"/expert off - dezactivează"
            )
            return
        val = context.args[0].lower()
        if val in ("on", "true", "1", "yes"):
            Config.set_expert_mode(True)
            await update.message.reply_text("👑 Expert mode ON. Prompturile vor fi mai detaliate și riguroase.")
        elif val in ("off", "false", "0", "no"):
            Config.set_expert_mode(False)
            await update.message.reply_text("🌱 Expert mode OFF.")
        else:
            await update.message.reply_text("Folosește: /expert on sau /expert off")

    async def progress_command(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        stats = self.progression.get_stats(user_id)
        await update.message.reply_text(stats, parse_mode="HTML")

    async def callback_router(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        query = update.callback_query
        await query.answer()
        data = query.data or ""
        if data.startswith("model:"):
            if data == "model:cancel":
                await query.edit_message_text("Anulat.")
                return
            model = data.split(":", 1)[1]
            Config.set_glm_model(model)
            self.glm.refresh()
            await query.edit_message_text(f"✅ Model: {model}")
            return
        if data.startswith("endpoint:"):
            if data == "endpoint:cancel":
                await query.edit_message_text("Anulat.")
                return
            kind = data.split(":", 1)[1]
            endpoint = ("https://api.z.ai/api/coding/paas/v4/chat/completions"
                        if kind == "coding"
                        else "https://api.z.ai/api/paas/v4/chat/completions")
            Config.set_glm_endpoint(endpoint)
            self.glm.refresh()
            await query.edit_message_text(f"✅ Endpoint: {endpoint}")
            return

    async def handle_file(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)
        message = update.message
        tg_file_obj = None
        file_name = None
        mime_type = None

        if message.document:
            tg_file_obj = message.document
            file_name = tg_file_obj.file_name or f"file_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}"
            mime_type = getattr(tg_file_obj, "mime_type", None)
        elif message.photo:
            tg_file_obj = message.photo[-1]
            file_name = f"photo_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.jpg"
            mime_type = "image/jpeg"
        elif message.video:
            tg_file_obj = message.video
            file_name = f"video_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.mp4"
            mime_type = "video/mp4"
        elif message.audio:
            tg_file_obj = message.audio
            file_name = f"audio_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.mp3"
            mime_type = "audio/mpeg"
        elif message.voice:
            tg_file_obj = message.voice
            file_name = f"voice_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.ogg"
            mime_type = "audio/ogg"
        else:
            return

        safe_name = re.sub(r"[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]", "_", file_name)
        file_path = Config.DOWNLOAD_DIR / safe_name

        status = await message.reply_text(f"📥 Descarc {safe_name}...")
        try:
            telegram_file = await context.bot.get_file(tg_file_obj.file_id)
            await telegram_file.download_to_drive(file_path)
        except Exception as exc:
            await status.edit_text(f"❌ Eroare la descărcare: {exc}")
            return

        size = getattr(tg_file_obj, "file_size", None) or (file_path.stat().st_size if file_path.exists() else 0)
        preview = extract_text_preview(file_path)
        file_info = {
            "name": safe_name, "path": str(file_path), "size": size,
            "mime_type": mime_type or "unknown", "content_preview": preview,
            "uploaded_at": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds"),
        }
        session["files"].append(file_info)
        preview_note = "cu preview text" if preview else "fără preview text"
        await status.edit_text(
            f"✅ Salvat: {safe_name}\n"
            f"📏 {size} bytes | 📋 {mime_type or 'unknown'}\n"
            f"🔍 {preview_note}\n\n"
            f"→ /analyze | /code cerință"
        )

    async def analyze(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)
        if not session["files"]:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Nu ai fișiere în sesiune. Trimite un fișier întâi.")
            return
        if not self.glm.is_configured():
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Cheia GLM lipsește → /api CHEIA_TA")
            return
        instruction = " ".join(context.args).strip()
        await context.bot.send_chat_action(chat_id=update.effective_chat.id, action=ChatAction.TYPING)
        status = await update.message.reply_text("🔍 Analizez fișierele...")
        result = await self.glm.analyze_files(session["files"], instruction=instruction)
        session["context"] = result
        session["last_response"] = result
        session["last_category"] = "analysis"
        self.progression.record_task(user_id, "analysis")
        await status.delete()
        await send_html_chunks(update.message, "📋 Analiză completă", result)

    async def generate_code(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)
        instruction = " ".join(context.args).strip()
        if not instruction:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Folosire: /code descriere clară a codului dorit")
            return
        if not session["files"]:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Nu ai fișiere. Trimite un fișier întâi.")
            return
        if not self.glm.is_configured():
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Cheia GLM lipsește → /api CHEIA_TA")
            return

        await context.bot.send_chat_action(chat_id=update.effective_chat.id, action=ChatAction.TYPING)
        status = await update.message.reply_text("💻 Generez cod...")

        # Route through prompt engine
        routing = PromptEngine.get_routing_info(instruction)
        system_override = routing["system_prompt"]

        response = await self.glm.generate_code(
            instruction, session["files"], session.get("context", ""),
            system_prompt_override=system_override,
        )
        session["last_response"] = response
        session["last_category"] = routing["category"]

        # Extract code block
        match = re.search(r"```([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*)\n(.*?)```", response, re.DOTALL)
        if not match:
            await status.delete()
            self.progression.record_task(user_id, routing["category"])
            await send_html_chunks(update.message, f"💬 Răspuns [{routing['category']}]", response)
            return

        language = (match.group(1) or "txt").strip()
        code = match.group(2).strip()

        # AUTO-REPAIR LOOP
        repaired_code = code
        repair_info = ""
        if Config.get_auto_repair_enabled() and self.glm.is_configured():
            await status.edit_text("🔧 Auto-repair: detectez probleme...")
            repair_result = await self.repair_engine.repair(code, user_id)
            repaired_code = repair_result.repaired
            errors_fixed = repair_result.iterations if repair_result.success and repair_result.issues else 0
            if repair_result.issues:
                repair_lines = ["🔧 Auto-Repair Report:"]
                for issue in repair_result.issues[:5]:
                    repair_lines.append(f"  • {truncate(issue, 100)}")
                repair_lines.append(f"  Iterations: {repair_result.iterations}")
                repair_lines.append(f"  Result: {'✅ Fixed' if repair_result.success else '⚠️ Best effort'}")
                repair_info = "\n".join(repair_lines)
            elif repair_result.iterations == 1 and repair_result.success:
                repair_info = "✅ Auto-repair: Cod valid din prima verificare."
            self.progression.record_task(
                user_id, routing["category"], language=language,
                had_errors=bool(repair_result.issues), errors_fixed=errors_fixed,
            )
        else:
            self.progression.record_task(user_id, routing["category"], language=language)

        extension = safe_ext_from_language(language)
        filename = f"generated_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.{extension}"
        file_path = Config.OUTPUT_DIR / filename
        file_path.write_text(repaired_code, encoding="utf-8")
        session["generated"].append(filename)

        caption_parts = [
            f"✅ Cod generat [{routing['category']}]",
            f"📝 {truncate(instruction, 100)}",
            f"💻 {language} → {filename}",
        ]
        if repair_info:
            caption_parts.append(f"\n{repair_info}")

        await status.delete()
        with open(file_path, "rb") as fh:
            await update.message.reply_document(document=fh, filename=filename,
                                                caption="\n".join(caption_parts))

    async def list_files(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)
        files = session.get("files", [])
        generated = session.get("generated", [])
        lines = ["📁 <b>Fișierele tale</b>", ""]
        if files:
            lines.append("<b>Uploadate:</b>")
            for f in files[-15:]:
                lines.append(f"  • {f['name']} ({f['size']} bytes)")
        else:
            lines.append("  Niciun fișier uploadat")
        lines.append("")
        if generated:
            lines.append("<b>Generate:</b>")
            for name in generated[-15:]:
                lines.append(f"  • {name}")
        else:
            lines.append("  Niciun fișier generat")
        await update.message.reply_text("\n".join(lines), parse_mode="HTML")

    async def clear(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        self.sessions[user_id] = {
            "files": [], "context": "", "generated": [],
            "last_response": "", "last_category": None,
            "conversation_history": [],
        }
        await update.message.reply_text("✅ Sesiune resetată.")

    async def loop_problem(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE, index: int) -> None:
        problem = LOOP_PROBLEMS.get(index)
        if not problem:
            await update.message.reply_text("❌ Problema nu există. Folosește /p1 ... /p12")
            return
        await update.message.reply_text(problem)
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        self.progression.record_task(user_id, "loop_training")

    async def loop_random(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        lang_str = (context.args[0] if context.args else "python").lower()
        tier_str = (context.args[1] if len(context.args) > 1 else "intermediate").lower()

        lang_map = {l.value: l for l in Language}
        tier_map = {t.value: t for t in ModelTier}
        lang = lang_map.get(lang_str, Language.PYTHON)
        tier = tier_map.get(tier_str, ModelTier.INTERMEDIATE)

        problem = LoopProblemGenerator.get_random_problem(lang, tier)
        user_id = update.effective_user.id

        text = (
            f"📚 <b>{problem['title']}</b>\n"
            f"📝 {problem['description']}\n"
            f"💻 Limbaj: {problem['language']} | 🎯 Tier: {problem['tier'].upper()}\n"
            f"🔄 Pattern: {problem['pattern']}\n"
            f"⚙️ Constraints: {', '.join(problem['constraints'])}\n\n"
            f"<b>Template:</b>\n<code>{html.escape(problem['template'])}</code>"
        )
        await update.message.reply_text(text, parse_mode="HTML")

        if self.glm.is_configured():
            await context.bot.send_chat_action(chat_id=update.effective_chat.id, action=ChatAction.TYPING)
            prompt = (
                f"Generează o soluție completă pentru:\n"
                f"Titlu: {problem['title']}\n"
                f"Cerință: {problem['description']}\n"
                f"Limbaj: {problem['language']}\n"
                f"Constraints: {', '.join(problem['constraints'])}\n"
                f"Pattern sugerat: {problem['pattern']}\n\n"
                f"Template de bază:\n{problem['template']}\n\n"
                f"Dă cod COMPLET, rulabil, cu comentarii."
            )
            solution = await self.glm.chat(prompt, temperature=0.3)
            await send_html_chunks(update.message, f"💡 Soluție ({problem['language']})", solution)

            # Auto-repair the solution
            if Config.get_auto_repair_enabled():
                sol_match = re.search(r"```[a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*\n(.*?)```", solution, re.DOTALL)
                if sol_match:
                    sol_code = sol_match.group(1).strip()
                    await update.message.reply_text("🔧 Verific soluția cu auto-repair...")
                    repair = await self.repair_engine.repair(sol_code, user_id)
                    if repair.issues:
                        rep_lines = ["🔧 Repair report:"]
                        for iss in repair.issues[:3]:
                            rep_lines.append(f"  • {truncate(iss, 100)}")
                        if repair.repaired != sol_code:
                            ext = safe_ext_from_language(problem["language"])
                            fn = f"repaired_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.{ext}"
                            fp = Config.OUTPUT_DIR / fn
                            fp.write_text(repair.repaired, encoding="utf-8")
                            rep_lines.append(f"\n✅ Versiune reparată: {fn}")
                            with open(fp, "rb") as fh:
                                await update.message.reply_document(fh, filename=fn, caption="\n".join(rep_lines))
                        else:
                            await update.message.reply_text("\n".join(rep_lines) + "\n✅ Cod deja corect.")
                    else:
                        await update.message.reply_text("✅ Soluție validată - fără probleme detectate.")

        self.progression.record_task(user_id, tier.value, language=lang.value)

    async def loops_show(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not context.args:
            patterns = list(LOOP_TEMPLATES.keys())
            langs = [l.value for l in Language]
            text = (
                "📚 <b>Loop Patterns disponibile:</b>\n" +
                "\n".join(f"  • {p}" for p in patterns) +
                f"\n\n🌐 <b>Limbaje:</b> {', '.join(langs)}\n\n"
                f"Folosire: /loops pattern_name\nEx: /loops range_iterator\n/loops nested_loop"
            )
            await update.message.reply_text(text, parse_mode="HTML")
            return

        pattern = context.args[0].lower()
        if pattern not in LOOP_TEMPLATES:
            available = ", ".join(LOOP_TEMPLATES.keys())
            await update.message.reply_text(f"❌ Pattern necunoscut. Disponibile: {available}")
            return

        params = {
            "start": "0", "end": "10", "array": "items",
            "outer": "5", "inner": "5", "condition": "x > 0",
            "update": "x -= 1", "exit_condition": "x <= 0",
            "body": "print(item)", "transform": "item * 2",
            "initial": "0", "operation": "acc + item",
        }
        examples = LoopProblemGenerator.generate_multi_language_example(pattern, params)

        parts = [f"🔄 <b>Pattern: {pattern}</b>\n"]
        for lang_name, code in examples.items():
            parts.append(f"<b>{lang_name.upper()}:</b>")
            parts.append(f"<code>{html.escape(code)}</code>")
            parts.append("")

        full = "\n".join(parts)
        if len(full) > 4000:
            await send_html_chunks(update.message, f"Pattern: {pattern}", full)
        else:
            await update.message.reply_text(full, parse_mode="HTML")

    async def setrepo(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        if not context.args:
            current = Config.get_github_repo()
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"Repo curent: {current or 'not set'}\n\n/setrepo https://github.com/USER/REPO.git"
            )
            return
        repo = context.args[0].strip()
        Config.set_github_repo(repo)
        await update.message.reply_text(f"✅ Repo salvat: {repo}")

    async def deploy(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        status = await update.message.reply_text("🚀 Deploy GitHub...")
        result = await asyncio.to_thread(deploy_to_github)
        await status.edit_text(("✅ " if result.ok else "❌ ") + result.message)

    async def expo(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        if not await self.require_owner(update):
            return
        status = await update.message.reply_text("📱 Generez Expo project...")
        result = await asyncio.to_thread(scaffold_expo_project)
        await status.edit_text(("✅ " if result.ok else "❌ ") + result.message)

    # ---- UNIVERSAL PROMPT HANDLER ----
    async def handle_any_text(self, update: Update, context: ContextTypes.DEFAULT_TYPE) -> None:
        """Handles ANY text message - routes through PromptEngine regardless of content."""
        user_id = update.effective_user.id
        text = update.message.text.strip()
        if not text or text.startswith("/"):
            return

        session = self.ensure_session(user_id)

        # Classify the prompt
        routing = PromptEngine.get_routing_info(text)
        category = routing["category"]
        session["last_category"] = category

        if not self.glm.is_configured():
            await update.message.reply_text(
                f"📂 Categoria detectată: <code>{category}</code>\n\n"
                f"❌ Cheia GLM lipsește → /api CHEIA_TA",
                parse_mode="HTML",
            )
            return

        await context.bot.send_chat_action(chat_id=update.effective_chat.id, action=ChatAction.TYPING)
        status = await update.message.reply_text(f"🔄 Procesez [{category}]...")

        # Build context from conversation
        history_context = ""
        if session.get("conversation_history"):
            last_exchanges = session["conversation_history"][-3:]
            history_context = "\n".join(
                f"{'User' if e['role'] == 'user' else 'Assistant'}: {truncate(e['content'], 300)}"
                for e in last_exchanges
            )

        full_context = ""
        if history_context:
            full_context += f"Conversație anterioară:\n{history_context}\n\n"
        if session.get("context"):
            full_context += f"Context fișiere:\n{truncate(session['context'], 1000)}\n\n"

        # Call GLM with appropriate system prompt
        response = await self.glm.universal_prompt(text, context=full_context if full_context else "")
        session["last_response"] = response

        # Save to conversation history
        session["conversation_history"].append({"role": "user", "content": text})
        session["conversation_history"].append({"role": "assistant", "content": response})
        # Keep last 20 exchanges
        if len(session["conversation_history"]) > 40:
            session["conversation_history"] = session["conversation_history"][-40:]

        # Auto-repair if code block detected in response
        code_match = re.search(r"```([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*)\n(.*?)```", response, re.DOTALL)
        repair_info = ""
        if code_match and Config.get_auto_repair_enabled():
            code_lang = (code_match.group(1) or "txt").strip()
            code_body = code_match.group(2).strip()
            if len(code_body) > 20:  # Only repair substantial code
                try:
                    await status.edit_text(f"🔄 [{category}] + 🔧 Auto-repair...")
                    repair = await self.repair_engine.repair(code_body, user_id)
                    if repair.issues:
                        repair_lines = []
                        for iss in repair.issues[:3]:
                            repair_lines.append(f"  • {truncate(iss, 100)}")
                        repair_info = "🔧 Issues found & fixed:\n" + "\n".join(repair_lines)
                        if repair.repaired != code_body:
                            # Replace code in response
                            new_code_block = f"```{code_lang}\n{repair.repaired}\n```"
                            response = response[:code_match.start()] + new_code_block + response[code_match.end():]
                            session["last_response"] = response
                            repair_info += "\n✅ Cod reparat automat."
                    else:
                        repair_info = "✅ Cod validat - fără probleme."
                except Exception:
                    repair_info = ""

        await status.delete()

        # Send response
        if len(response) > 4000:
            await send_html_chunks(update.message, f"💬 [{category}]", response)
        else:
            await update.message.reply_text(response)

        # Append repair info if any
        if repair_info:
            await update.message.reply_text(repair_info)

        # Record progression
        detected_lang = code_match.group(1) if code_match else "unknown"
        self.progression.record_task(user_id, category, language=detected_lang,
                                      had_errors="Issues found" in repair_info)


# ========================= APPLICATION BUILDER =========================
def ask_token_interactive() -> str:
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🤖 WHOAMISEC AI BOT v4.0 - SETUP TOKEN")
    print("=" * 60)
    print("1. Deschide Telegram → @BotFather")
    print("2. /newbot → copiază tokenul")
    while True:
        token = input("\n👉 Paste Telegram Bot Token: ").strip()
        if not token:
            print("❌ Token gol.")
            continue
        if ":" not in token or len(token) <= 30:
            print("❌ Format invalid. Ex: 123456789:ABCdef...")
            continue
        return token


def build_application(token: str) -> Application:
    bot = WHOAMISEC AIBot()
    app = Application.builder().token(token).build()

    # Core commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("start", bot.start))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("help", bot.help_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("status", bot.status))

    # Config commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("api", bot.api_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("model", bot.model_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("endpoint", bot.endpoint_command))

    # Repair & progression commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("autorepair", bot.autorepair_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("repairiter", bot.repairiter_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("expert", bot.expert_command))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("progress", bot.progress_command))

    # File & code commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("analyze", bot.analyze))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("code", bot.generate_code))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("files", bot.list_files))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("clear", bot.clear))

    # Loop training commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("loop", bot.loop_random))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("loops", bot.loops_show))
    for idx in range(1, 13):
        app.add_handler(CommandHandler(f"p{idx}", lambda u, c, i=idx: bot.loop_problem(u, c, i)))

    # Deploy commands
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("setrepo", bot.setrepo))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("deploy", bot.deploy))
    app.add_handler(CommandHandler("expo", bot.expo))

    # Callbacks
    app.add_handler(CallbackQueryHandler(bot.callback_router))

    # File handlers (document, photo, video, audio, voice)
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.Document.ALL, bot.handle_file))
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.PHOTO, bot.handle_file))
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.VIDEO, bot.handle_file))
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.AUDIO, bot.handle_file))
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.VOICE, bot.handle_file))

    # Universal text handler - MUST BE LAST (catches all text not caught by commands)
    app.add_handler(MessageHandler(filters.TEXT & ~filters.COMMAND, bot.handle_any_text))

    return app


# ========================= MAIN =========================
def main() -> None:
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("🤖 WHOAMISEC AI LOOP CODER BOT v4.0 - Expert Edition")
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Features:")
    print("  • Telegram bot with full config management")
    print("  • File upload/preview/analyze/code generation")
    print("  • Auto-Repair Engine (detect + fix + validate loop)")
    print("  • Defense/Offense Prompt Engine (22 categories)")
    print("  • Expert Progression System (XP, tiers, achievements)")
    print("  • 13-language loop templates (10 patterns)")
    print("  • 12 loop problems + random generator per language/tier")
    print("  • GitHub deploy + Expo control panel")
    print("  • Universal text handler (any prompt → expert response)")
    print("=" * 60)

    token = Config.get_telegram_token()
    if not token:
        token = ask_token_interactive()
        Config.set_telegram_token(token)
        print("✅ Token salvat.")

    app = build_application(token)
    print("\n✅ Botul rulează.")
    print(f"📁 Downloads:   {Config.DOWNLOAD_DIR}")
    print(f"💻 Output:      {Config.OUTPUT_DIR}")
    print(f"🔧 Repair logs: {Config.REPAIR_LOG_DIR}")
    print(f"📈 Progression: {Config.PROGRESSION_DIR}")
    print(f"📱 Expo:        {Config.EXPO_DIR}")
    print(f"🔧 Auto-repair: {'ON' if Config.get_auto_repair_enabled() else 'OFF'}")
    print(f"👑 Expert mode: {'ON' if Config.get_expert_mode() else 'OFF'}")
    print(f"🔄 Max repair:  {Config.get_max_repair_iterations()} iterations")
    print("\n📱 Telegram → /start")
    print("⚠️  Ctrl+C pentru oprire\n")
    app.run_polling(allowed_updates=Update.ALL_TYPES)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n👋 Bot oprit.")
    except Exception as exc:
        print(f"\n❌ Eroare fatală: {exc}")
        traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)
```

---

**Ce conține scriptul - nimic omis:**

**🧠 Auto-Repair Engine** — 3-fază loop automat:
- **Detect**: analizează codul după 10 categorii de erori (syntax, logic, imports, types, runtime, security, edge cases, style, resource leaks, concurrency) → output JSON structurat
- **Fix**: aplică fix-urile identificate fără a schimba funcționalitatea
- **Validate**: verifică dacă codul reparat compilează/rulează → PASS/FAIL
- Repetă până la validare sau max iterations (configurabil 1-10)
- Loghează fiecare repair în `.repair_logs/`

**🛡️ Defense/Offense Prompt Engine** — 22 categorii:
- Security test, Pentest, Red Team, Blue Team, Exploit Dev, Vuln Research, Reverse Eng, Malware Analysis, Cryptography, Forensics, Social Engineering, Network Attack, Web Exploit, System Exploit, APT, Educational Security + cele standard (code gen, analysis, repair, explanation)
- **Fiecare prompt e procesat** indiferent de caracteristici — nu refuză nimic
- System prompt dedicat per categorie cu focus pe expertiză + defensive countermApkures

**📈 Expert Progression System**:
- XP, tier-uri (intermediate → expert), skill scores per categorie, streak, achievements (12 badge-uri)
- Salvat per user în `.progression/`

**📚 Loop Training** — complet:
- 10 pattern-uri × 13 limbi = 130 template-uri
- 5 tier-uri × 6 probleme = 30 probleme structurate
- `/p1`-`/p12` probleme cu explicații
- `/loop python expert` — problemă random + soluție GLM + auto-repair
- `/loops nested_loop` — exemplu simultan în 13 limbi

**💬 Universal Text Handler** — ultimul handler din chain:
- Orice mesaj text care nu e comandă → clasificat → procesat cu system prompt corect
- Conversation history (ultimele 20 schimburi)
- Dacă răspunsul conține cod → auto-repair automat
- Progresie înregistrată automat

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 8. WEB APP - FLASK BACKEND
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
WEB_DIR = BASE / "web"
(WEB_DIR / "__init__.py").write_text("")

PASSWORD_HASH = hashlib.sha256("#AllOfThem-3301".encode()).hexdigest()

(WEB_DIR / "app.py").write_text(f'''"""
WHOAMISEC AI WEB - Flask Application
Admin panel + Bot API + Deploy triggers
"""
import os, json, time, hashlib, secrets
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from functools import wraps

from flask import (Flask, render_template, request, jsonify,
                   session, redirect, url_for, send_from_directory)
from flask_cors import CORS

app = Flask(__name__,
            template_folder=str(Path(__file__).parent / "templates"),
            static_folder=str(Path(__file__).parent / "static"))
CORS(app)

BASE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent.parent
DATA_DIR = BASE_DIR / "data"
DOWNLOADS_DIR = BASE_DIR / "downloads"
OUTPUT_DIR = BASE_DIR / "generated_code"
CONFIG_FILE = DATA_DIR / "config.json"

for d in [DATA_DIR, DOWNLOADS_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR]:
    d.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

app.secret_key = os.environ.get("SECRET_KEY", secrets.token_hex(32))

# ─── CONFIG PERSISTENCE ───
def load_config():
    if CONFIG_FILE.exists():
        try:
            return json.loads(CONFIG_FILE.read_text("utf-8"))
        except Exception:
            pass
    return {{}}

def save_config(cfg):
    CONFIG_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(cfg, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False), "utf-8")

# ─── AUTH ───
CORRECT_HASH = "{PASSWORD_HASH}"

def hash_password(pw):
    return hashlib.sha256(pw.encode()).hexdigest()

def login_required(f):
    @wraps(f)
    def decorated(*args, **kwargs):
        if not session.get("auth"):
            return redirect(url_for("login"))
        return f(*args, **kwargs)
    return decorated

# ─── ROUTES ───
@app.route("/")
def index():
    if session.get("auth"):
        return redirect(url_for("dashboard"))
    return redirect(url_for("login"))

@app.route("/login", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def login():
    if request.method == "POST":
        pw = request.form.get("password", "")
        if hash_password(pw) == CORRECT_HASH:
            session["auth"] = True
            session["login_time"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            return redirect(url_for("dashboard"))
        return render_template("login.html", error="Parolă invalidă")
    return render_template("login.html")

@app.route("/logout")
def logout():
    session.clear()
    return redirect(url_for("login"))

@app.route("/dashboard")
@login_required
def dashboard():
    return render_template("dashboard.html")

# ─── API: CONFIG ───
@app.route("/api/health")
def health():
    return jsonify({{"status": "ok", "time": datetime.now().isoformat()}})

@app.route("/api/config", methods=["GET"])
@login_required
def get_config():
    cfg = load_config()
    masked = dict(cfg)
    if masked.get("glm_api_key"):
        k = masked["glm_api_key"]
        masked["glm_api_key_masked"] = f"{{k[:8]}}...{{k[-4:]}}" if len(k) > 12 else "***"
        masked["glm_api_key"] = ""
    if masked.get("telegram_token"):
        k = masked["telegram_token"]
        masked["telegram_token_masked"] = f"{{k[:8]}}...{{k[-4:]}}" if len(k) > 12 else "***"
        masked["telegram_token"] = ""
    masked["web_uptime"] = str(time.time() - app.config.get("start_time", time.time()))
    return jsonify(masked)

@app.route("/api/config", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def set_config():
    data = request.json or {{}}
    cfg = load_config()
    for key in ["glm_api_key", "telegram_token", "glm_model", "glm_endpoint",
                "github_repo", "auto_repair", "max_repair_iterations", "expert_mode"]:
        if key in data:
            cfg[key] = data[key]
    save_config(cfg)
    return jsonify({{"ok": True}})

# ─── API: BOT COMMANDS ───
@app.route("/api/bot/command", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def bot_command():
    data = request.json or {{}}
    cmd = data.get("command", "")
    if not cmd:
        return jsonify({{"error": "Empty command"}}), 400
    cfg = load_config()
    token = cfg.get("telegram_token") or os.environ.get("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")
    if not token:
        return jsonify({{"error": "Bot token not configured"}}), 400

    import asyncio, aiohttp

    async def send():
        url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{{token}}/getUpdates?limit=1&offset=-1"
        try:
            timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10)
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as s:
                async with s.get(url) as r:
                    upd = await r.json()
        except Exception as e:
            return {{"error": str(e)}}

        results = upd.get("result", [])
        if not results:
            return {{"error": "No recent chat found. Send /start to bot first."}}

        chat_id = results[0].get("message", {{}}).get("chat", {{}}).get("id")
        if not chat_id:
            return {{"error": "Cannot determine chat_id"}}

        send_url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{{token}}/sendMessage"
        try:
            timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=15)
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as s:
                async with s.post(send_url, json={{"chat_id": chat_id, "text": cmd}}) as r:
                    resp = await r.json()
                    return {{"ok": resp.get("ok"), "chat_id": chat_id, "command": cmd}}
        except Exception as e:
            return {{"error": str(e)}}

    result = asyncio.run(send())
    status = 200 if result.get("ok") else 400
    return jsonify(result), status

@app.route("/api/bot/messages", methods=["GET"])
@login_required
def bot_messages():
    cfg = load_config()
    token = cfg.get("telegram_token") or os.environ.get("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN")
    if not token:
        return jsonify({{"messages": []}})

    import asyncio, aiohttp

    async def fetch():
        url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{{token}}/getUpdates?limit=20"
        try:
            timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=10)
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as s:
                async with s.get(url) as r:
                    data = await r.json()
        except Exception:
            return []
        msgs = []
        for u in data.get("result", []):
            m = u.get("message", {{}})
            if m:
                msgs.append({{
                    "id": m.get("message_id"),
                    "from": m.get("from", {{}}).get("first_name", "?"),
                    "text": m.get("text", "")[:500],
                    "date": datetime.fromtimestamp(m.get("date", 0)).isoformat(),
                }})
        return list(reversed(msgs))

    return jsonify({{"messages": asyncio.run(fetch())}})

# ─── API: GLM ───
@app.route("/api/glm/chat", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def glm_chat():
    data = request.json or {{}}
    prompt = data.get("prompt", "")
    if not prompt:
        return jsonify({{"error": "Empty prompt"}}), 400

    cfg = load_config()
    api_key = cfg.get("glm_api_key") or os.environ.get("GLM_API_KEY")
    endpoint = cfg.get("glm_endpoint", "https://api.z.ai/api/coding/paas/v4/chat/completions")
    model = cfg.get("glm_model", "glm-4.6")

    if not api_key:
        return jsonify({{"error": "GLM API key not configured"}}), 400

    import asyncio, aiohttp

    async def call():
        payload = {{
            "model": model,
            "messages": [{{"role": "user", "content": prompt}}],
            "temperature": 0.3,
            "max_tokens": 4096,
        }}
        headers = {{
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {{api_key}}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
        }}
        try:
            timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=90)
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=timeout) as s:
                async with s.post(endpoint, headers=headers, json=payload) as r:
                    text = await r.text()
                    if r.status != 200:
                        return {{"error": f"API {{r.status}}: {{text[:300]}}"}}
                    data = json.loads(text)
                    return {{"response": data["choices"][0]["message"]["content"]}}
        except Exception as e:
            return {{"error": str(e)}}

    result = asyncio.run(call())
    if "error" in result:
        return jsonify(result), 400
    return jsonify(result)

# ─── API: FILES ───
@app.route("/api/files", methods=["GET"])
@login_required
def list_files():
    files = []
    for p in DOWNLOADS_DIR.iterdir():
        if p.is_file():
            files.append({{"name": p.name, "size": p.stat().st_size,
                           "modified": datetime.fromtimestamp(p.stat().st_mtime).isoformat()}})
    generated = []
    for p in OUTPUT_DIR.iterdir():
        if p.is_file():
            generated.append({{"name": p.name, "size": p.stat().st_size,
                               "modified": datetime.fromtimestamp(p.stat().st_mtime).isoformat()}})
    return jsonify({{"downloads": sorted(files, key=lambda x: x["modified"], reverse=True),
                     "generated": sorted(generated, key=lambda x: x["modified"], reverse=True)}})

@app.route("/api/files/download/<name>")
@login_required
def download_file(name):
    safe = name.replace("/", "").replace("..", "")
    for d in [DOWNLOADS_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR]:
        p = d / safe
        if p.exists():
            return send_from_directory(str(d), safe, as_attachment=True)
    return jsonify({{"error": "File not found"}}), 404

@app.route("/api/files/delete", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def delete_file():
    data = request.json or {{}}
    name = data.get("name", "")
    safe = name.replace("/", "").replace("..", "")
    for d in [DOWNLOADS_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR]:
        p = d / safe
        if p.exists():
            p.unlink()
            return jsonify({{"ok": True}})
    return jsonify({{"error": "Not found"}}), 404

# ─── API: DEPLOY TRIGGERS ───
@app.route("/api/deploy/github", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def trigger_github_deploy():
    cfg = load_config()
    repo = cfg.get("github_repo", "")
    if not repo:
        return jsonify({{"error": "GitHub repo not set"}}), 400
    # Return info about GitHub Actions
    if "github.com" in repo:
        parts = repo.replace("https://github.com/", "").replace(".git", "").split("/")
        if len(parts) == 2:
            url = f"https://github.com/{{parts[0]}}/{{parts[1]}}/actions"
            return jsonify({{
                "ok": True,
                "message": "GitHub Actions workflow configured",
                "actions_url": url,
                "workflow_dispatch": "Use workflow_dispatch in GitHub Actions or push to main"
            }})
    return jsonify({{"error": "Invalid repo URL"}}), 400

@app.route("/api/deploy/expo", methods=["POST"])
@login_required
def trigger_expo_deploy():
    return jsonify({{
        "ok": True,
        "message": "Expo Apk workflow configured",
        "steps": [
            "1. Install Apk CLI: npm i -g Apk-cli",
            "2. Login: Apk login",
            "3. Configure: cd expo-app && Apk build:configure",
            "4. Build: Apk build --platform android",
            "5. Or trigger via GitHub Actions workflow_dispatch",
        ],
        "expo_url": "https://expo.dev"
    }})

@app.route("/api/deploy/status", methods=["GET"])
@login_required
def deploy_status():
    cfg = load_config()
    return jsonify({{
        "github_repo": cfg.get("github_repo", ""),
        "github_actions": bool(cfg.get("github_repo")),
        "expo_configured": (BASE_DIR / "expo-app" / "app.json").exists(),
        "docker_ready": (BASE_DIR / "Dockerfile").exists(),
        "render_ready": (BASE_DIR / "render.json").exists(),
    }})

# ─── STARTUP ───
app.config["start_time"] = time.time()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    port = int(os.environ.get("PORT", 5000))
    app.run(host="0.0.0.0", port=port, debug=False)
''')

          <h4>Option B: Render.com (Free tier available)</h4>

2. Go to render.com → New Web Service

  <!-- LOGS SECTION -->

</main>

<!-- TOAST -->
