# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 12. DASHBOARD JS
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
(WEB_DIR / "static" / "js" / "dashboard.js").write_text('''// WHOAMISEC AI DASHBOARD JS
const $ = s => document.querySelector(s);
const $$ = s => document.querySelectorAll(s);

// ─── NAVIGATION ───
function navigateTo(section) {
  $$('.nav-links a').forEach(a => a.classList.remove('active'));
  $$(`.nav-links a[data-section="${section}"]`).forEach(a => a.classList.add('active'));
  $$('.section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
  const sec = $(`#sec-${section}`);
  if (sec) sec.classList.add('active');
  $('#sectionTitle').textContent = $$('.nav-links a.active')[0]?.textContent || '';
  if (section === 'files') refreshFiles();
  if (section === 'deploy') checkDeployStatus();
}

 $$('.nav-links a').forEach(a => {
  a.addEventListener('click', e => { e.preventDefault(); navigateTo(a.dataset.section); });
});

 $('#menuToggle')?.addEventListener('click', () => $('#sidebar').classList.toggle('open'));

// ─── TOAST ───
function toast(msg, type = 'info') {
  const el = document.createElement('div');
  el.className = `toast ${type}`;
  el.textContent = msg;
  $('#toastContainer').appendChild(el);
  setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 4000);
}

function addLog(type, msg) {
  const log = $('#activityLog');
  if (log.querySelector('.empty-state')) log.innerHTML = '';
  const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
  const entry = document.createElement('div');
  entry.className = 'log-entry';
  entry.innerHTML = `<span class="log-time">${time}</span><span class="log-type ${type}">${type.toUpperCase()}</span><span class="log-msg">${msg}</span>`;
  log.prepend(entry);
  if (log.children.length > 100) log.lastChild.remove();
}

// ─── API HELPERS ───
async function api(url, opts = {}) {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url, { headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, ...opts });
    if (res.status === 401) { window.location = '/login'; return null; }
    return await res.json();
  } catch (e) { toast('Network error: ' + e.message, 'error'); return null; }
}

// ─── OVERVIEW ───
async function loadOverview() {
  const cfg = await api('/api/config');
  if (!cfg) return;
  $('#statBot').textContent = cfg.telegram_token_masked ? '✅ Ready' : '❌ No Token';
  $('#statBot').style.color = cfg.telegram_token_masked ? '#86efac' : '#fca5a5';
  $('#statGLM').textContent = cfg.glm_api_key_masked ? '✅ Ready' : '❌ No Key';
  $('#statGLM').style.color = cfg.glm_api_key_masked ? '#86efac' : '#fca5a5';
  const files = await api('/api/files');
  const fc = files ? (files.downloads?.length || 0) + (files.generated?.length || 0) : 0;
  $('#statFiles').textContent = fc + ' files';
  $('#statRepair').textContent = cfg.auto_repair === false ? '❌ OFF' : '✅ ON (' + (cfg.max_repair_iterations || 3) + ')';
  $('#statExpert').textContent = cfg.expert_mode === 'true' ? '👑 ON' : '🌱 OFF';
  const deploy = await api('/api/deploy/status');
  if (deploy) {
    const r = [deploy.docker_ready, deploy.render_ready, deploy.github_actions, deploy.expo_configured].filter(Boolean).length;
    $('#statDeploy').textContent = r + '/4 ready';
  }
  refreshMessages();
}

// ─── BOT COMMANDS ───
async function sendBotCmd(cmd) {
  const input = $('#botCmdInput');
  if (!cmd && input) cmd = input.value.trim();
  if (!cmd) return;
  if (input) input.value = '';
  addLog('info', 'Bot cmd: ' + cmd);
  const res = await api('/api/bot/command', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ command: cmd }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Command sent!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'Sent: ' + cmd); }
  else { toast(res?.error || 'Failed', 'error'); addLog('err', res?.error || 'Failed'); }
  setTimeout(refreshMessages, 2000);
}

 $('#botCmdInput')?.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') sendBotCmd(); });

async function refreshMessages() {
  const res = await api('/api/bot/messages');
  if (!res?.messages) return;
  const msgs = res.messages;
  const html = msgs.length ? msgs.map(m =>
    `<div class="msg-item"><span class="msg-from">${m.from}</span><span class="msg-text">${escHtml(m.text)}</span><span class="msg-time">${m.date?.split('T')[1]?.slice(0,5) || ''}</span></div>`
  ).join('') : '<p class="empty-state">No messages</p>';
  $('#recentMessages').innerHTML = html;
  $('#botMessages').innerHTML = html;
}

// ─── GLM CHAT ───
async function sendGLM() {
  const input = $('#glmInput');
  const msg = input?.value?.trim();
  if (!msg) return;
  input.value = '';
  const chat = $('#glmChat');
  chat.innerHTML += `<div class="glm-msg user">${escHtml(msg)}</div>`;
  chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
  addLog('info', 'GLM: ' + msg.slice(0, 80));
  const res = await api('/api/glm/chat', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ prompt: msg }) });
  if (res?.response) {
    chat.innerHTML += `<div class="glm-msg assistant">${formatGLM(res.response)}</div>`;
    addLog('ok', 'GLM response received');
  } else {
    chat.innerHTML += `<div class="glm-msg assistant" style="color:#fca5a5">Error: ${escHtml(res?.error || 'Unknown')}</div>`;
    addLog('err', 'GLM error: ' + (res?.error || ''));
  }
  chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight;
}

function formatGLM(text) {
  let html = escHtml(text);
  html = html.replace(/```([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*)\\n?([\\s\\S]*?)```/g, '<pre><code>$2</code></pre>');
  html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
  html = html.replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
  html = html.replace(/\\n/g, '<br>');
  return html;
}

// ─── FILES ───
async function refreshFiles() {
  const res = await api('/api/files');
  if (!res) return;
  $('#downloadedFiles').innerHTML = res.downloads?.length
    ? res.downloads.map(f => fileHtml(f, 'downloads')).join('') : '<p class="empty-state">No downloads</p>';
  $('#generatedFiles').innerHTML = res.generated?.length
    ? res.generated.map(f => fileHtml(f, 'generated')).join('') : '<p class="empty-state">No generated files</p>';
}

function fileHtml(f, type) {
  const size = f.size > 1024 ? (f.size / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB' : f.size + ' B';
  return `<div class="file-item"><span class="file-name">${escHtml(f.name)}</span><span class="file-size">${size}</span><div class="file-actions"><button class="file-btn-dl" onclick="dlFile('${f.name}','${type}')">⬇</button><button class="file-btn-del" onclick="delFile('${f.name}')">🗑</button></div></div>`;
}

function dlFile(name, type) { window.open('/api/files/download/' + encodeURIComponent(name)); }

async function delFile(name) {
  if (!confirm('Delete ' + name + '?')) return;
  const res = await api('/api/files/delete', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ name }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Deleted', 'success'); refreshFiles(); addLog('info', 'Deleted: ' + name); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

// ─── DEPLOY ───
async function checkDeployStatus() {
  const res = await api('/api/deploy/status');
  if (!res) return;
  $('#githubStatus').textContent = res.github_actions ? '✅ Configured' : '❌ No repo set';
  $('#expoStatus').textContent = res.expo_configured ? '✅ app.json exists' : '⚠️ Not configured';
}

async function triggerGitHub() {
  const res = await api('/api/deploy/github', { method: 'POST' });
  if (res?.ok) {
    toast('GitHub workflow ready!', 'success');
    if (res.actions_url) window.open(res.actions_url, '_blank');
    addLog('ok', 'GitHub deploy triggered');
  } else toast(res?.error || 'Failed', 'error');
}

async function triggerExpo() {
  const res = await api('/api/deploy/expo', { method: 'POST' });
  if (res?.ok) {
    toast('Expo info loaded', 'info');
    addLog('info', 'Expo: ' + res.message);
    alert('Expo Deploy Steps:\\n\\n' + res.steps?.join('\\n'));
  } else toast(res?.error || 'Failed', 'error');
}

function copyDockerCmds() {
  const cmds = `# Clone & Deploy with Docker
git clone YOUR_REPO.git WHOAMISEC AI && cd WHOAMISEC AI
cp .env.example .env
# Edit .env with your API keys
docker compose up -d --build

# Check logs
docker compose logs -f

# Rebuild after changes
docker compose up -d --build --force-recreate`;
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(cmds).then(() => toast('Docker commands copied!', 'success'));
}

// ─── SETTINGS ───
async function loadSettings() {
  const cfg = await api('/api/config');
  if (!cfg) return;
  if (cfg.telegram_token_masked) $('#hintTelegram').textContent = 'Current: ' + cfg.telegram_token_masked;
  if (cfg.glm_api_key_masked) $('#hintGlm').textContent = 'Current: ' + cfg.glm_api_key_masked;
  if (cfg.glm_model) $('#setModel').value = cfg.glm_model;
  if (cfg.glm_endpoint) $('#setEndpoint').value = cfg.glm_endpoint;
  $('#setAutoRepair').value = cfg.auto_repair === false ? 'false' : 'true';
  $('#setMaxRepair').value = cfg.max_repair_iterations || 3;
  $('#setExpert').value = cfg.expert_mode === 'true' ? 'true' : 'false';
  if (cfg.github_repo) $('#setRepo').value = cfg.github_repo;
}

async function saveKeys() {
  const data = {};
  const t = $('#setTelegramToken').value.trim();
  const g = $('#setGlmKey').value.trim();
  if (t) data.telegram_token = t;
  if (g) data.glm_api_key = g;
  if (!t && !g) { toast('No changes', 'info'); return; }
  const res = await api('/api/config', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Keys saved!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'API keys updated'); $('#setTelegramToken').value = ''; $('#setGlmKey').value = ''; loadSettings(); loadOverview(); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

async function saveGLMSettings() {
  const res = await api('/api/config', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ glm_model: $('#setModel').value, glm_endpoint: $('#setEndpoint').value }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('GLM settings saved!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'GLM: ' + $('#setModel').value); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

async function saveRepairSettings() {
  const res = await api('/api/config', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ auto_repair: $('#setAutoRepair').value, max_repair_iterations: parseInt($('#setMaxRepair').value) }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Repair settings saved!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'Repair: ' + $('#setAutoRepair').value); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

async function saveExpertMode() {
  const res = await api('/api/config', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ expert_mode: $('#setExpert').value }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Expert mode saved!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'Expert: ' + $('#setExpert').value); loadOverview(); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

async function saveRepo() {
  const repo = $('#setRepo').value.trim();
  if (!repo) { toast('Empty repo', 'info'); return; }
  const res = await api('/api/config', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ github_repo: repo }) });
  if (res?.ok) { toast('Repo saved!', 'success'); addLog('ok', 'Repo: ' + repo); }
  else toast('Failed', 'error');
}

// ─── UTILS ───
function escHtml(s) { const d = document.createElement('div'); d.textContent = s || ''; return d.innerHTML; }

// ─── INIT ───
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  loadOverview();
  loadSettings();
  refreshFiles();
  checkDeployStatus();
  addLog('info', 'Dashboard loaded');
});

// Auto-refresh messages every 15s
setInterval(refreshMessages, 15000);
''')

(EXPO_DIR / "app" / "login.tsx").write_text('''import { useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import * as SecureStore from 'expo-secure-store';
import { axiosInstance } from '../services/api';

export default function Login() {
  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const router = useRouter();

  const login = async () => {
    if (!password.trim()) { Alert.alert('Error', 'Enter password'); return; }
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const form = new FormData();
      form.append('password', password);
      const res = await axiosInstance.post('/login', form);
      if (res.status === 200 || res.request.responseURL.includes('dashboard')) {
        await SecureStore.setItemAsync('auth', '1');
        router.replace('/dashboard');
      } else {
        Alert.alert('Error', 'Invalid password');
      }
    } catch (e: any) {
      Alert.alert('Error', e.message);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <View style={styles.container}>
      <Text style={styles.logo}>🤖</Text>
      <Text style={styles.title}>WHOAMISEC AI</Text>
      <Text style={styles.sub}>Admin Login</Text>
      <TextInput style={styles.input} placeholder="Password" placeholderTextColor="#475569"
        secureTextEntry value={password} onChangeText={setPassword}
        onSubmitEditing={login} autoFocus />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.btn} onPress={login} disabled={loading}>
        <Text style={styles.btnText}>{loading ? '...' : 'Access →'}</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  container: { flex: 1, backgroundColor: '#0a0e1a', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 16, padding: 32 },
  logo: { fontSize: 56 }, title: { fontSize: 28, fontWeight: '700', color: '#60a5fa' },
  sub: { fontSize: 13, color: '#64748b' },
  input: { width: '100%', padding: 14, backgroundColor: '#111827', borderRadius: 12, color: 'white', fontSize: 15, borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#334155' },
  btn: { width: '100%', padding: 14, backgroundColor: '#2563eb', borderRadius: 12, alignItems: 'center', marginTop: 8 },
  btnText: { color: 'white', fontWeight: '700', fontSize: 15 },
});
''')

(EXPO_DIR / "app" / "dashboard.tsx").write_text('''import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, ScrollView, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, RefreshControl } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import * as SecureStore from 'expo-secure-store';
import { api } from '../services/api';

interface Stats {{ bot: string; glm: string; files: number; repair: string; expert: string }}

export default function Dashboard() {{
  const router = useRouter();
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<Stats | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const load = async () => {{
    setLoading(true);
    try {{
      const cfg = await api.getConfig();
      setStats({{
        bot: cfg.telegram_token_masked ? '✅' : '❌',
        glm: cfg.glm_api_key_masked ? '✅' : '❌',
        files: (cfg.downloads_count || 0) + (cfg.generated_count || 0),
        repair: cfg.auto_repair !== false ? '✅' : '❌',
        expert: cfg.expert_mode === 'true' ? '👑' : '🌱',
      }});
    }} catch (e) {{ /* silent */ }}
    setLoading(false);
  }};

  useEffect(() => {{ load(); }}, []);

  const sendCmd = async (cmd: string) => {{
    try {{ await api.sendBotCommand(cmd); }} catch (e) {{ /* silent */ }}
  }};

  const logout = async () => {{
    await SecureStore.deleteItemAsync('auth');
    router.replace('/login');
  }};

  const quickActions = [
    {{ icon: '📊', label: 'Status', cmd: '/status' }},
    {{ icon: '📁', label: 'Files', cmd: '/files' }},
    {{ icon: '🧹', label: 'Clear', cmd: '/clear' }},
    {{ icon: '📈', label: 'Progress', cmd: '/progress' }},
    {{ icon: '💬', label: 'GLM Chat', action: () => router.push('/chat') }},
    {{ icon: '🚀', label: 'Deploy', action: () => router.push('/deploy') }},
    {{ icon: '⚙️', label: 'Settings', action: () => router.push('/settings') }},
  ];

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}} refreshControl={{<RefreshControl refreshing={loading} onRefresh={load} colors={['#3b82f6']}/>}}>
      <View style={styles.statsGrid}}>
        {{stats && [
          {{ icon: '🤖', label: 'Bot', value: stats.bot }},
          {{ icon: '🧠', label: 'GLM', value: stats.glm }},
          {{ icon: '📁', label: 'Files', value: String(stats.files) }},
          {{ icon: '🔧', label: 'Repair', value: stats.repair }},
          {{ icon: '👑', label: 'Expert', value: stats.expert }},
        ].map((s, i) => (
          <View key={i}} style={styles.statCard}}>
            <Text style={styles.statIcon}}>{{s.icon}}</Text>
            <Text style={styles.statValue}}>{{s.value}}</Text>
            <Text style={styles.statLabel}}>{{s.label}}</Text>
          </View>
        ))}}
      </View>
      <Text style={styles.sectionTitle}}>⚡ Quick Actions</Text>
      <View style={styles.actionsGrid}}>
        {{quickActions.map((a, i) => (
          <TouchableOpacity key={i}} style={styles.actionBtn}} onPress={{a.action || (() => sendCmd(a.cmd!))}}>
            <Text style={styles.actionIcon}}>{{a.icon}}</Text>
            <Text style={styles.actionLabel}}>{{a.label}}</Text>
          </TouchableOpacity>
        ))}}
      </View>
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.logoutBtn}} onPress={logout}}>
        <Text style={styles.logoutText}}>🚪 Logout</Text>
      </TouchableOpacity>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({{
  container: {{ padding: 20, gap: 20 }},
  statsGrid: {{ flexDirection: 'row', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 10, justifyContent: 'space-between' }},
  statCard: {{ backgroundColor: '#111827', borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#1e293b', borderRadius: 12, padding: 16, alignItems: 'center', width: '18%', minWidth: 70 }},
  statIcon: {{ fontSize: 24 }}, statValue: {{ fontSize: 20, fontWeight: '700', color: '#f1f5f9', marginTop: 4 }},
  statLabel: {{ fontSize: 11, color: '#64748b', marginTop: 2 }},
  sectionTitle: {{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: '600', color: '#f1f5f9' }},
  actionsGrid: {{ flexDirection: 'row', flexWrap: 'wrap', gap: 10 }},
  actionBtn: {{ backgroundColor: '#1a1f35', borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#1e293b', borderRadius: 12, padding: 16, alignItems: 'center', width: '31%', minWidth: 100 }},
  actionIcon: {{ fontSize: 28 }}, actionLabel: {{ fontSize: 13, color: '#94a3b8', marginTop: 6 }},
  logoutBtn: {{ backgroundColor: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)', borderRadius: 12, padding: 14, alignItems: 'center', marginTop: 20 }},
  logoutText: {{ color: '#fca5a5', fontWeight: '600' }},
}});
''')

(EXPO_DIR / "app" / "chat.tsx").write_text('''import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, ScrollView, StyleSheet, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '../services/api';

interface Msg {{ role: string; content: string }}

export default function Chat() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Msg[]>([{ role: 'system', content: 'GLM Ready. Ask anything.' }]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const scrollRef = useRef<ScrollView>(null);

  const send = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const msg = input.trim();
    setInput('');
    setMessages(p => [...p, { role: 'user', content: msg }]);
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await api.glmChat(msg);
      setMessages(p => [...p, { role: 'assistant', content: res.response || 'Error' }]);
    } catch (e: any) {
      setMessages(p => [...p, { role: 'assistant', content: 'Error: ' + e.message }]);
    }
    setLoading(false);
    setTimeout(() => scrollRef.current?.scrollToEnd({ animated: true }), 100);
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView style={{ flex: 1 }} behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : undefined}>
      <ScrollView ref={scrollRef} contentContainerStyle={styles.msgList} onContentSizeChange={() => scrollRef.current?.scrollToEnd({ animated: true })}>
        {messages.map((m, i) => (
          <View key={i} style={[styles.msg, m.role === 'user' ? styles.msgUser : m.role === 'system' ? styles.msgSystem : styles.msgBot]}>
            <Text style={styles.msgText}>{m.content}</Text>
          </View>
        ))}
        {loading && <View style={styles.msgSystem}><Text style={styles.msgText}>Thinking...</Text></View>}
      </ScrollView>
      <View style={styles.inputBar}>
        <TextInput style={styles.input} placeholder="Ask anything..." placeholderTextColor="#475569"
          value={input} onChangeText={setInput} onSubmitEditing={send} editable={!loading} />
        <TouchableOpacity style={styles.sendBtn} onPress={send} disabled={loading}>
          <Text style={styles.sendText}>→</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  msgList: { padding: 16, gap: 8, flexGrow: 1 },
  msg: { maxWidth: '85%', padding: 12, borderRadius: 12 },
  msgUser: { alignSelf: 'flex-end', backgroundColor: '#1e3a5f' },
  msgBot: { alignSelf: 'flex-start', backgroundColor: '#111827', borderWidth: 1, borderColor: '#1e293b' },
  msgSystem: { alignSelf: 'center', backgroundColor: 'transparent' },
  msgText: { color: '#e2e8f0', fontSize: 14, lineHeight: 20 },
  inputBar: { flexDirection: 'row', padding: 12, gap: 8, backgroundColor: '#111827', borderTopWidth: 1, borderTopColor: '#1e293b' },
  input: { flex: 1, padding: 12, backgroundColor: '#0a0e1a', borderRadius: 10, color: 'white', fontSize: 14 },
  sendBtn: { backgroundColor: '#2563eb', borderRadius: 10, padding: 12, alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', width: 48 },
  sendText: { color: 'white', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: '700' },
});
''')

(EXPO_DIR / "app" / "settings.tsx").write_text('''import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, ScrollView, Alert, Switch } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '../services/api';

export default function Settings() {
  const [token, setToken] = useState('');
  const [glmKey, setGlmKey] = useState('');
  const [model, setModel] = useState('glm-4.6');
  const [autoRepair, setAutoRepair] = useState(true);
  const [expert, setExpert] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => { loadCfg(); }, []);

  const loadCfg = async () => {
    try {
      const cfg = await api.getConfig();
      if (cfg.glm_model) setModel(cfg.glm_model);
      setAutoRepair(cfg.auto_repair !== false);
      setExpert(cfg.expert_mode === 'true');
    } catch (e) {}
  };

  const save = async (key: string, val: string) => {
    try { await api.setConfig({ [key]: val }); Alert.alert('OK', 'Saved'); } catch (e) { Alert.alert('Error', String(e)); }
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={styles.container}>
      <Text style={styles.sectionTitle}}>🔑 API Keys</Text>
      <TextInput style={styles.input}} placeholder="Telegram Bot Token" placeholderTextColor="#475569" value={token} onChangeText={setToken} secureTextEntry />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.btn}} onPress={() => { save('telegram_token', token); setToken(''); }}><Text style={styles.btnText}}>Save Token</Text></TouchableOpacity>
      <TextInput style={styles.input}} placeholder="GLM API Key" placeholderTextColor="#475569" value={glmKey} onChangeText={setGlmKey} secureTextEntry />
      <TouchableOpacity style={styles.btn}} onPress={() => { save('glm_api_key', glmKey); setGlmKey(''); }}><Text style={styles.btnText}}>Save GLM Key</Text></TouchableOpacity>

      <Text style={styles.sectionTitle}}>🧠 Model</Text>
      <View style={styles.modelRow}}>
        {{['glm-4.6', 'glm-4.5-air', 'glm-4-plus', 'glm-5.1'].map(m => (
          <TouchableOpacity key={m}} style={[styles.modelBtn, model === m && styles.modelBtnActive]}} onPress={{() => {{ setModel(m); save('glm_model', m); } }}}>
            <Text style={{ color: model === m ? '#60a5fa' : '#64748b', fontSize: 12 }}>{m}</Text>
          </TouchableOpacity>
        ))}}
      </View>

      <Text style={styles.sectionTitle}}>🔧 Toggles</Text>
      <View style={styles.toggleRow}}>
        <Text style={styles.toggleLabel}}>Auto-Repair</Text>
        <Switch value={autoRepair}} onValueChange={{v => {{ setAutoRepair(v); save('auto_repair', String(v)); } }} trackColor={{ false: '#334155', true: '#2563eb' }} />
      </View>
      <View style={styles.toggleRow}}>
        <Text style={styles.toggleLabel}}>Expert Mode</Text>
        <Switch value={expert}} onValueChange={{v => {{ setExpert(v); save('expert_mode', String(v)); } }} trackColor={{ false: '#334155', true: '#2563eb' }} />
      </View>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

# Minimal repair engine importable by web
(BOT_DIR / "engines" / "repair.py").write_text('''"""Auto-Repair Engine - importable module"""
import json, re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

SYSTEM_DETECT = """Analyze code for errors. Output JSON array:
[{"severity":"CRITICAL","category":"SYNTAX","line":0,"description":"...","fix":"..."}]
Empty array if no issues: []"""

SYSTEM_FIX = """Fix ALL listed issues. Output ONLY fixed code in markdown block."""

SYSTEM_VALIDATE = """Output exactly: PASS or FAIL: rApkon"""

async def detect_issues(glm_chat_fn, code: str) -> List[Dict]:
    raw = await glm_chat_fn(f"Analyze:\\n```\\n{code}\\n```", SYSTEM_DETECT, 0.1)
    try:
        cleaned = raw.strip()
        if cleaned.startswith("```"): cleaned = re.sub(r"^```(?:json)?\\s*\\n?", "", cleaned); cleaned = re.sub(r"\\n?```\\s*$", "", cleaned)
        issues = json.loads(cleaned)
        return issues if isinstance(issues, list) else []
    except: return []

async def fix_code(glm_chat_fn, code: str, issues: List[Dict]) -> str:
    issues_text = "\\n".join(f"- [{i.get('severity','?')}] {i.get('description','')} -> {i.get('fix','')}" for i in issues)
    raw = await glm_chat_fn(f"Fix:\\n```\\n{code}\\n```\\nIssues:\\n{issues_text}", SYSTEM_FIX, 0.1)
    m = re.search(r"```[a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*\\n(.*?)```", raw, re.DOTALL)
    return m.group(1).strip() if m else raw.strip()

async def validate(glm_chat_fn, code: str) -> tuple:
    raw = await glm_chat_fn(f"Validate:\\n```\\n{code}\\n```", SYSTEM_VALIDATE, 0.0)
    r = raw.strip().upper()
    if r.startswith("PASS"): return True, "OK"
    return False, r.replace("FAIL:", "").strip()[:200]

async def repair(glm_chat_fn, code: str, max_iter: int = 3) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    current = code
    all_issues = []
    for i in range(1, max_iter + 1):
        issues = await detect_issues(glm_chat_fn, current)
        if not issues:
            ok, _ = await validate(glm_chat_fn, current)
            if ok: return {"repaired": current, "issues": all_issues, "iterations": i, "success": True}
        critical = [x for x in issues if x.get("severity","").upper() in ("CRITICAL","HIGH")] or issues[:3]
        for x in critical: all_issues.append(f"[{x.get('severity','?')}] {x.get('description','')}")
        current = await fix_code(glm_chat_fn, current, critical)
    ok, _ = await validate(glm_chat_fn, current)
    return {"repaired": current, "issues": all_issues, "iterations": max_iter, "success": ok}
''')

# Prompt engine importable
(BOT_DIR / "engines" / "prompt_engine.py").write_text('''"""Prompt Classification Engine"""
from enum import Enum

class PromptClassifier(Enum):
    NORMAL="normal"; CODE_GENERATION="code_generation"; ANALYSIS="analysis"
    REPAIR="repair"; EXPLANATION="explanation"; SECURITY_TEST="security_test"
    PENETRATION_TEST="penetration_test"; RED_TEAM="red_team"; BLUE_TEAM="blue_team"
    EXPLOIT_DEVELOPMENT="exploit_development"; VULNERABILITY_RESEARCH="vulnerability_research"
    REVERSE_ENGINEERING="reverse_engineering"; MALWARE_ANALYSIS="malware_analysis"
    CRYPTOGRAPHY="cryptography"; FORENSICS="forensics"; SOCIAL_ENGINEERING="social_engineering"
    NETWORK_ATTACK="network_attack"; WEB_EXPLOIT="web_exploit"; SYSTEM_EXPLOIT="system_exploit"
    ADVANCED_PERSISTENT="advanced_persistent"; EDUCATIONAL_SECURITY="educational_security"
    UNKNOWN="unknown"

KEYWORDS = {
    PromptClassifier.SECURITY_TEST: ["security test","security audit","pentest","vulnerability scan"],
    PromptClassifier.PENETRATION_TEST: ["penetration test","ethical hack","auth bypass","privilege escalation"],
    PromptClassifier.RED_TEAM: ["red team","adversary simulation","attack simulation"],
    PromptClassifier.BLUE_TEAM: ["blue team","detection","siem","incident response"],
    PromptClassifier.EXPLOIT_DEVELOPMENT: ["exploit","shellcode","buffer overflow","rop chain"],
    PromptClassifier.VULNERABILITY_RESEARCH: ["vulnerability","cve","zero day","bug bounty","fuzzing"],
    PromptClassifier.REVERSE_ENGINEERING: ["reverse engineer","decompile","disassemble","ghidra"],
    PromptClassifier.MALWARE_ANALYSIS: ["malware","trojan","ransomware","rootkit"],
    PromptClassifier.CRYPTOGRAPHY: ["cipher","encrypt","decrypt","rsa","aes"],
    PromptClassifier.FORENSICS: ["forensic","disk image","memory dump","artifact"],
    PromptClassifier.SOCIAL_ENGINEERING: ["phishing","social engineering","pretexting"],
    PromptClassifier.NETWORK_ATTACK: ["mitm","dns spoof","arp poison","packet capture"],
    PromptClassifier.WEB_EXPLOIT: ["sql injection","xss","csrf","ssrf","rce","lfi"],
    PromptClassifier.SYSTEM_EXPLOIT: ["privilege escalation","kernel exploit","suid","container escape"],
    PromptClassifier.ADVANCED_PERSISTENT: ["apt","stager","beacon","c2","command and control"],
    PromptClassifier.EDUCATIONAL_SECURITY: ["ctf","capture the flag","security lab","learn security"],
    PromptClassifier.CODE_GENERATION: ["generate","create","write","build","implement","code"],
    PromptClassifier.ANALYSIS: ["analyze","review","examine","inspect","how does"],
    PromptClassifier.REPAIR: ["fix","repair","debug","error","bug","broken","crash"],
    PromptClassifier.EXPLANATION: ["explain","what is","how to","why","difference","compare"],
}

SYSTEM_PROMPTS = {
    PromptClassifier.NORMAL: "You are an expert software engineer.",
    PromptClassifier.CODE_GENERATION: "You are a world-class software engineer. Produce complete, production-ready code.",
    PromptClassifier.ANALYSIS: "You are an expert code analyst. Provide thorough analysis.",
    PromptClassifier.REPAIR: "You are an expert debugger. Identify root cause and provide minimal fix.",
    PromptClassifier.EXPLANATION: "You are an expert technical educator. Explain clearly with examples.",
    PromptClassifier.SECURITY_TEST: "You are an expert security tester. Cover OWASP Top 10 and provide remediation.",
    PromptClassifier.PENETRATION_TEST: "You are an expert pentester. Include methodology and defensive countermApkures.",
    PromptClassifier.RED_TEAM: "You are an expert red team operator. Map to MITRE ATT&CK. Include detection guidance.",
    PromptClassifier.BLUE_TEAM: "You are an expert blue team defender. Provide detection rules and hardening guides.",
    PromptClassifier.EXPLOIT_DEVELOPMENT: "You are an expert vulnerability researcher. Include mitigation strategies.",
    PromptClassifier.VULNERABILITY_RESEARCH: "You are an expert vulnerability researcher. Include responsible disclosure.",
    PromptClassifier.REVERSE_ENGINEERING: "You are an expert reverse engineer. Include protection recommendations.",
    PromptClassifier.MALWARE_ANALYSIS: "You are an expert malware analyst. Include IOC extraction and remediation.",
    PromptClassifier.CRYPTOGRAPHY: "You are an expert cryptographer. Warn about pitfalls, recommend secure libraries.",
    PromptClassifier.FORENSICS: "You are an expert digital forensics practitioner. Maintain chain of custody.",
    PromptClassifier.SOCIAL_ENGINEERING: "You are a social engineering awareness expert. Focus on defense.",
    PromptClassifier.NETWORK_ATTACK: "You are an expert network security analyst. Include IDS/IPS rules.",
    PromptClassifier.WEB_EXPLOIT: "You are an expert web security researcher. Reference OWASP, include WAF rules.",
    PromptClassifier.SYSTEM_EXPLOIT: "You are an expert system security researcher. Include audit checklists.",
    PromptClassifier.ADVANCED_PERSISTENT: "You are an expert threat intelligence analyst. Focus on defense.",
    PromptClassifier.EDUCATIONAL_SECURITY: "You are an expert cybersecurity educator. Build progressively.",
    PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN: "You are an expert assistant. Provide the most helpful response possible.",
}

def classify(prompt: str) -> PromptClassifier:
    lower = prompt.lower()
    scores = {}
    for cls, kws in KEYWORDS.items():
        score = sum(1 for kw in kws if kw in lower)
        if score > 0: scores[cls] = score
    if scores: return max(scores, key=scores.get)
    if any(lower.startswith(q) for q in ["what","how","why","explain"]): return PromptClassifier.EXPLANATION
    if any(lower.startswith(a) for a in ["fix","debug","repair"]): return PromptClassifier.REPAIR
    if any(lower.startswith(c) for c in ["write","create","generate","build"]): return PromptClassifier.CODE_GENERATION
    if any(lower.startswith(a) for a in ["analyze","review","check"]): return PromptClassifier.ANALYSIS
    return PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN

def get_system_prompt(cls: PromptClassifier) -> str:
    return SYSTEM_PROMPTS.get(cls, SYSTEM_PROMPTS[PromptClassifier.UNKNOWN])

def get_routing(prompt: str) -> dict:
    c = classify(prompt)
    return {"category": c.value, "system_prompt": get_system_prompt(c)}
''')

# 4. LIB/STORE.TS (server-side only)
# ══════════════════════════════════════
w("lib/store.ts", """
// Server-side in-memory store — used ONLY by API routes
// On expo.dev hosting this persists for the lifetime of the server process

interface FileEntry { data: string; type: string; size: number; name: string; uploaded: string; }
interface LogEntry { time: string; type: string; msg: string; }

class Store {
  sessions = new Map<string, { created: string }>();
  config: Record<string, string> = {};
  files = new Map<string, FileEntry>();
  generatedFiles = new Map<string, FileEntry>();
  logs: LogEntry[] = [];

  constructor() {
    this.config = {
      glm_api_key: process.env.GLM_API_KEY || '',
      telegram_token: process.env.TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN || '',
      glm_model: process.env.GLM_MODEL || 'glm-4.6',
      glm_endpoint: process.env.GLM_ENDPOINT || 'https://api.z.ai/api/coding/paas/v4/chat/completions',
      github_repo: process.env.GITHUB_REPO || '',
      auto_repair: process.env.AUTO_REPAIR || 'true',
      max_repair_iterations: process.env.MAX_REPAIR_ITERATIONS || '3',
      expert_mode: process.env.EXPERT_MODE || 'false',
    };
  }

  createSession(): string {
    const token = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);
    this.sessions.set(token, { created: new Date().toISOString() });
    return token;
  }

  checkSession(token: string): boolean {
    return this.sessions.has(token);
  }

  destroySession(token: string) { this.sessions.delete(token); }

  addLog(type: string, msg: string) {
    this.logs.unshift({ time: new Date().toISOString(), type, msg: msg.slice(0, 500) });
    if (this.logs.length > 200) this.logs.length = 200;
  }

  mask(key: string): string {
    const v = this.config[key];
    if (!v || v.length < 12) return v ? '***' : '';
    return v.slice(0, 8) + '...' + v.slice(-4);
  }
}

export const store = new Store();
""")

// Client-side API helper
import { Platform } from 'react-native';

const BASE = Platform.OS === 'web' ? '' : 'https://your-app.expo.app';

async function req(path: string, opts: RequestInit = {}) {
  const url = BASE + path;
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url, { credentials: 'include', ...opts });
    if (res.status === 401) { if (Platform.OS === 'web') window.location.href = '/login'; return null; }
    const ct = res.headers.get('content-type') || '';
    if (ct.includes('json')) return await res.json();
    return { ok: res.ok, status: res.status };
  } catch (e: any) { return { error: e.message }; }
}

export const api = {
  health: () => req('/api/health'),
  login: (pw: string) => req('/api/auth/login', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ password: pw }) }),
  check: () => req('/api/auth/check'),
  logout: () => req('/api/auth/logout', { method: 'POST' }),
  getConfig: () => req('/api/config'),
  setConfig: (data: Record<string, string>) => req('/api/config', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify(data) }),
  glmChat: (prompt: string) => req('/api/glm/chat', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ prompt }) }),
  botCommand: (cmd: string) => req('/api/bot/command', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ command: cmd }) }),
  botMessages: () => req('/api/bot/messages'),
  files: () => req('/api/files'),
  deployStatus: () => req('/api/deploy/status'),
  triggerGitHub: () => req('/api/deploy/github', { method: 'POST' }),
  triggerExpo: () => req('/api/deploy/expo', { method: 'POST' }),
};
""")

# ══════════════════════════════════════
# 6. API ROUTES
# ══════════════════════════════════════

def api_route(path, code):
    w(f"app/api/{path}/route.ts", code)

api_route("health", """export async function GET() {
  return Response.json({ status: 'ok', time: new Date().toISOString(), uptime: process.uptime() });
}""")

api_route("auth/login", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
import { PASSWORD_HASH } from '@/constants/theme';
import { createHash } from 'crypto';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  try {
    const { password } = await request.json();
    const hash = createHash('sha256').update(password || '').digest('hex');
    if (hash !== PASSWORD_HASH) {
      return Response.json({ error: 'Invalid password' }, { status: 401 });
    }
    const token = store.createSession();
    store.addLog('ok', 'Admin logged in');
    const res = Response.json({ ok: true });
    res.headers.set('Set-Cookie', `session=${token}; HttpOnly; Path=/; SameSite=Lax; Max-Age=86400`);
    return res;
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

api_route("auth/check", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  const cookie = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const match = cookie.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  if (match && store.checkSession(match[1])) {
    return Response.json({ auth: true });
  }
  return Response.json({ auth: false }, { status: 401 });
}""")

api_route("auth/logout", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  const cookie = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const match = cookie.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  if (match) store.destroySession(match[1]);
  const res = Response.json({ ok: true });
  res.headers.set('Set-Cookie', 'session=; HttpOnly; Path=/; Max-Age=0');
  return res;
}""")

api_route("config", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(request: Request): boolean {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  return Response.json({
    glm_api_key_masked: store.mask('glm_api_key'),
    telegram_token_masked: store.mask('telegram_token'),
    glm_model: store.config.glm_model,
    glm_endpoint: store.config.glm_endpoint,
    github_repo: store.config.github_repo,
    auto_repair: store.config.auto_repair,
    max_repair_iterations: store.config.max_repair_iterations,
    expert_mode: store.config.expert_mode,
    downloads_count: store.files.size,
    generated_count: store.generatedFiles.size,
    uptime: process.uptime(),
  });
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const data = await request.json();
    const allowed = ['glm_api_key','telegram_token','glm_model','glm_endpoint','github_repo','auto_repair','max_repair_iterations','expert_mode'];
    for (const k of allowed) { if (data[k] !== undefined) { store.config[k] = String(data[k]); } }
    store.addLog('info', 'Config updated: ' + Object.keys(data).join(', '));
    return Response.json({ ok: true });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

api_route("glm/chat", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const { prompt } = await request.json();
    if (!prompt) return Response.json({ error: 'Empty prompt' }, { status: 400 });
    const key = store.config.glm_api_key;
    if (!key) return Response.json({ error: 'GLM API key not set' }, { status: 400 });

    const resp = await fetch(store.config.glm_endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + key, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: store.config.glm_model,
        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }],
        temperature: 0.3, max_tokens: 4096,
      }),
    });

    if (!resp.ok) {
      const txt = await resp.text();
      store.addLog('err', 'GLM error: ' + txt.slice(0, 200));
      return Response.json({ error: 'GLM API ' + resp.status + ': ' + txt.slice(0, 300) }, { status: 502 });
    }

    const data = await resp.json();
    const content = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';
    store.addLog('ok', 'GLM response: ' + content.slice(0, 80));
    return Response.json({ response: content });
  } catch (e: any) {
    store.addLog('err', 'GLM: ' + e.message);
    return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}""")

api_route("bot/command", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const { command } = await request.json();
    if (!command) return Response.json({ error: 'Empty' }, { status: 400 });
    const token = store.config.telegram_token;
    if (!token) return Response.json({ error: 'Bot token not set' }, { status: 400 });

    // Get chat_id from recent updates
    const updResp = await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot' + token + '/getUpdates?limit=1&offset=-1');
    const updData = await updResp.json();
    const results = updData.result || [];
    if (!results.length) return Response.json({ error: 'No recent chat. Send /start to bot first.' }, { status: 400 });
    const chatId = results[0].message?.chat?.id;
    if (!chatId) return Response.json({ error: 'Cannot get chat_id' }, { status: 400 });

    const sendResp = await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot' + token + '/sendMessage', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ chat_id: chatId, text: command }),
    });
    const sendData = await sendResp.json();
    store.addLog('info', 'Bot cmd: ' + command.slice(0, 60));
    return Response.json({ ok: sendData.ok, chat_id: chatId, command });
  } catch (e: any) {
    store.addLog('err', 'Bot: ' + e.message);
    return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}""")

api_route("bot/messages", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const token = store.config.telegram_token;
  if (!token) return Response.json({ messages: [] });
  try {
    const resp = await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot' + token + '/getUpdates?limit=25');
    const data = await resp.json();
    const msgs = (data.result || []).map((u: any) => ({
      from: u.message?.from?.first_name || '?',
      text: (u.message?.text || '').slice(0, 500),
      date: new Date((u.message?.date || 0) * 1000).toISOString(),
    })).reverse();
    return Response.json({ messages: msgs });
  } catch { return Response.json({ messages: [] }); }
}""")

api_route("files", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const dl = Array.from(store.files.values()).map(f => ({ name: f.name, size: f.size, uploaded: f.uploaded }));
  const gen = Array.from(store.generatedFiles.values()).map(f => ({ name: f.name, size: f.size, uploaded: f.uploaded }));
  return Response.json({ downloads: dl.reverse(), generated: gen.reverse() });
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const fd = await request.formData();
    const file = fd.get('file') as File | null;
    if (!file) return Response.json({ error: 'No file' }, { status: 400 });
    const buf = await file.arrayBuffer();
    const b64 = Buffer.from(buf).toString('base64');
    store.files.set(file.name, { data: b64, type: file.type, size: file.size, name: file.name, uploaded: new Date().toISOString() });
    store.addLog('info', 'File uploaded: ' + file.name);
    return Response.json({ ok: true, name: file.name, size: file.size });
  } catch (e: any) { return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 400 }); }
}

export async function DELETE(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const { name } = await request.json();
    if (store.files.delete(name) || store.generatedFiles.delete(name)) {
      store.addLog('info', 'File deleted: ' + name);
      return Response.json({ ok: true });
    }
    return Response.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

api_route("deploy/status", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const repo = store.config.github_repo || '';
  let githubActions = false;
  if (repo.includes('github.com')) {
    const parts = repo.replace('https://github.com/', '').replace('.git', '').split('/');
    githubActions = parts.length === 2;
  }
  return Response.json({
    github_repo: repo, github_actions, github_url: githubActions ? repo.replace('.git', '') + '/actions' : '',
    expo_configured: true, uptime: process.uptime(), node_env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'production',
  });
}""")

api_route("deploy/github", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

function auth(r: Request): boolean {
  const c = r.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  return !!m && store.checkSession(m[1]);
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const repo = store.config.github_repo;
  if (!repo) return Response.json({ error: 'GitHub repo not set' }, { status: 400 });
  store.addLog('info', 'GitHub deploy triggered');
  const parts = repo.replace('https://github.com/', '').replace('.git', '').split('/');
  const url = parts.length === 2 ? 'https://github.com/' + parts[0] + '/' + parts[1] + '/actions' : '';
  return Response.json({ ok: true, actions_url: url, message: 'Go to GitHub Actions to trigger or push to main' });
}""")

function auth(r: Request): boolean {

}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  store.addLog('info', 'Expo deploy info requested');
  return Response.json({
    ok: true,
    message: 'Expo hosting active',
    steps: [
      '1. Push changes to trigger auto-deploy',
      '2. Or run: Apk hosting:deploy',
      '3. Or use GitHub integration on expo.dev',
    ],
    expo_url: 'https://expo.dev',

  });
}""")

w("app/index.tsx", """import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, ActivityIndicator, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';

export default function Index() {
  const router = useRouter();
  useEffect(() => {
    api.check().then(r => {
      if (r?.auth) router.replace('/(panel)');
      else router.replace('/login');
    }).catch(() => router.replace('/login'));
  }, []);
  return (
    <View style={s.container}>
      <Text style={s.logo}>🤖</Text>
      <ActivityIndicator color="#3b82f6" size="large" />
    </View>
  );
}
const s = StyleSheet.create({ container: { flex:1, backgroundColor:'#0a0e1a', alignItems:'center', justifyContent:'center', gap:16 }, logo: { fontSize:64 } });
""")

# 8. LOGIN

w("app/login.tsx", """import { useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, Alert, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';

export default function Login() {
  const [pw, setPw] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [err, setErr] = useState('');
  const router = useRouter();

  const login = async () => {
    if (!pw.trim()) { setErr('Enter password'); return; }
    setLoading(true); setErr('');
    const res = await api.login(pw);
    setLoading(false);
    if (res?.ok) router.replace('/(panel)');
    else setErr(res?.error || 'Login failed');
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView behavior={Platform.OS === 'ios' ? 'padding' : undefined} style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.box}>
        <Text style={s.logo}>🤖</Text>
        <Text style={s.title}>WHOAMISEC AI Admin</Text>
        <Text style={s.sub}>v4.0 Expert Edition</Text>
        {err ? <Text style={s.err}>{err}</Text> : null}
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Admin Password" placeholderTextColor="#475569"
          secureTextEntry value={pw} onChangeText={setPw} onSubmitEditing={login} autoFocus
          editable={!loading} />
        <TouchableOpacity style={s.btn} onPress={login} disabled={loading}>
          <Text style={s.btnText}>{loading ? '...' : 'Access Dashboard →'}</Text>
        </TouchableOpacity>
        <Text style={s.footer}>24/7 Online · expo.dev</Text>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap: { flex:1, backgroundColor:'#0a0e1a', justifyContent:'center', alignItems:'center' },
  box: { width:'100%', maxWidth:420, padding:48, backgroundColor:'#111827', borderRadius:20, borderWidth:1, borderColor:'#1e293b', alignItems:'center' },
  logo: { fontSize:56 }, title: { fontSize:28, fontWeight:'700', color:'#60a5fa', marginTop:8 },
  sub: { fontSize:13, color:'#64748b', marginTop:4 },
  err: { width:'100%', padding:12, backgroundColor:'#1c1017', borderWidth:1, borderColor:'#7f1d1d', borderRadius:10, color:'#fca5a5', fontSize:13, marginTop:20 },
  input: { width:'100%', padding:14, backgroundColor:'#0f172a', borderWidth:1, borderColor:'#334155', borderRadius:12, color:'#f1f5f9', fontSize:15, marginTop:24 },
  btn: { width:'100%', padding:14, backgroundColor:'#2563eb', borderRadius:12, marginTop:20, alignItems:'center' },
  btnText: { color:'#fff', fontWeight:'700', fontSize:15 },
  footer: { color:'#475569', fontSize:12, marginTop:24 },
});
""")

w("app/(panel)/_layout.tsx", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, StyleSheet, Platform, Dimensions } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter, usePathname, Slot } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

const TABS = [
  { path: '', icon: '📊', label: 'Overview' },
  { path: '/bot', icon: '💬', label: 'Bot' },
  { path: '/glm', icon: '🧠', label: 'GLM' },
  { path: '/files', icon: '📁', label: 'Files' },
  { path: '/deploy', icon: '🚀', label: 'Deploy' },
  { path: '/settings', icon: '⚙️', label: 'Settings' },
];

const isWeb = Platform.OS === 'web';

export default function PanelLayout() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const [authed, setAuthed] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    api.check().then(r => { if (!r?.auth) router.replace('/login'); else setAuthed(true); })
      .catch(() => router.replace('/login'));
  }, []);

  const logout = async () => { await api.logout(); router.replace('/login'); };

  if (!authed) return <View style={{ flex:1, backgroundColor:C.bg }} />;

  const activeTab = TABS.findIndex(t => (pathname === '/(panel)' && t.path === '') || pathname === '/(panel)' + t.path);

  // WEB: Sidebar layout
  if (isWeb) {
    return (
      <View style={styles.webWrap}>
        <View style={styles.sidebar}>
          <View style={styles.sideHead}>
            <Text style={styles.sideLogo}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI</Text>
            <Text style={styles.sideVer}>v4.0</Text>
          </View>
          {TABS.map((t, i) => (
            <Pressable key={t.path} style={[styles.sideLink, activeTab === i && styles.sideLinkActive]}
              onPress={() => router.push('/(panel)' + t.path)}>
              <Text style={[styles.sideLinkText, activeTab === i && styles.sideLinkTextActive]}>{t.icon} {t.label}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          ))}
          <View style={{ flex:1 }} />
          <Pressable style={styles.logoutBtn} onPress={logout}>
            <Text style={styles.logoutText}>🚪 Logout</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
        <View style={styles.main}>
          <View style={styles.topbar}>
            <Text style={styles.topTitle}>{TABS[activeTab]?.icon} {TABS[activeTab]?.label || 'Overview'}</Text>
            <Text style={styles.topStatus}>● Online</Text>
          </View>
          <View style={styles.content}><Slot /></View>
        </View>
      </View>
    );
  }

  // MOBILE: Tab bar layout
  return (
    <View style={styles.mobWrap}>
      <View style={styles.mobHeader}>
        <Text style={styles.mobTitle}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI</Text>
        <Pressable onPress={logout}><Text style={styles.mobLogout}>🚪</Text></Pressable>
      </View>
      <View style={styles.mobContent}><Slot /></View>
      <View style={styles.tabBar}>
        {TABS.map((t, i) => (
          <Pressable key={t.path} style={[styles.tabItem, activeTab === i && styles.tabItemActive]}
            onPress={() => router.push('/(panel)' + t.path)}>
            <Text style={styles.tabIcon}>{t.icon}</Text>
            <Text style={[styles.tabLabel, activeTab === i && styles.tabLabelActive]}>{t.label}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

const styles = StyleSheet.create({
  webWrap: { flex:1, flexDirection:'row', backgroundColor:C.bg },
  sidebar: { width:C.sidebarW, backgroundColor:C.surface, borderRightWidth:1, borderRightColor:C.border, paddingTop:24, paddingHorizontal:12, flexShrink:0 },
  sideHead: { paddingBottom:20, borderBottomWidth:1, borderBottomColor:C.border, marginBottom:12, paddingHorizontal:8 },
  sideLogo: { fontSize:22, fontWeight:'700', color:'#60a5fa' },
  sideVer: { fontSize:11, color:C.text3, backgroundColor:C.surface2, padding:2, borderRadius:4, marginTop:4, alignSelf:'flex-start' },
  sideLink: { paddingVertical:11, paddingHorizontal:12, borderRadius:8, marginBottom:2 },
  sideLinkActive: { backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)' },
  sideLinkText: { fontSize:14, color:C.text2, fontWeight:'500' },
  sideLinkTextActive: { color:'#60a5fa' },
  logoutBtn: { padding:12, backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)', borderRadius:8, alignItems:'center', marginBottom:8 },
  logoutText: { color:'#fca5a5', fontWeight:'500', fontSize:13 },
  main: { flex:1, minWidth:0 },
  topbar: { flexDirection:'row', alignItems:'center', justifyContent:'space-between', padding:16, paddingHorizontal:24, borderBottomWidth:1, borderBottomColor:C.border, backgroundColor:'rgba(10,14,26,0.85)' },
  topTitle: { fontSize:18, fontWeight:'600', color:C.text },
  topStatus: { fontSize:13, color:'#22c55e' },
  content: { flex:1, overflow:'auto' },
  mobWrap: { flex:1, backgroundColor:C.bg },
  mobHeader: { flexDirection:'row', justifyContent:'space-between', alignItems:'center', padding:16, paddingTop:48, backgroundColor:C.surface, borderBottomWidth:1, borderBottomColor:C.border },
  mobTitle: { fontSize:20, fontWeight:'700', color:'#60a5fa' },
  mobLogout: { fontSize:20 },
  mobContent: { flex:1 },
  tabBar: { flexDirection:'row', backgroundColor:C.surface, borderTopWidth:1, borderTopColor:C.border, paddingBottom:4 },
  tabItem: { flex:1, paddingVertical:8, alignItems:'center', gap:2 },
  tabItemActive: { backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)' },
  tabIcon: { fontSize:20 },
  tabLabel: { fontSize:10, color:C.text3 },
  tabLabelActive: { color:'#60a5fa' },
});
""")

# ══════════════════════════════════════
# 10. PANEL SCREENS
# ══════════════════════════════════════

def panel_screen(name, code):
    w(f"app/(panel)/{name}.tsx", code)

panel_screen("index", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, ScrollView, Pressable, StyleSheet, RefreshControl } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

interface Cfg { glm_api_key_masked:string; telegram_token_masked:string; glm_model:string; auto_repair:string; expert_mode:string; downloads_count:number; generated_count:number; uptime:number; }
interface Msg { from:string; text:string; date:string; }

export default function Overview() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [cfg, setCfg] = useState<Cfg|null>(null);
  const [msgs, setMsgs] = useState<Msg[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const load = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const [c, m] = await Promise.all([api.getConfig(), api.botMessages()]);
    if (c) setCfg(c);
    if (m?.messages) setMsgs(m.messages.slice(0, 10));
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { load(); const iv = setInterval(load, 15000); return () => clearInterval(iv); }, []);

  const send = async (cmd: string) => { await api.botCommand(cmd); setTimeout(load, 2000); };

  const stats = cfg ? [
    { icon:'🤖', val: cfg.telegram_token_masked ? '✅ Ready' : '❌ No Token', label:'Bot' },
    { icon:'🧠', val: cfg.glm_api_key_masked ? '✅ Ready' : '❌ No Key', label:'GLM' },
    { icon:'📁', val: ((cfg.downloads_count||0)+(cfg.generated_count||0)) + ' files', label:'Files' },
    { icon:'🔧', val: cfg.auto_repair !== 'false' ? '✅ ON' : '❌ OFF', label:'Repair' },
    { icon:'👑', val: cfg.expert_mode === 'true' ? '👑 ON' : '🌱 OFF', label:'Expert' },
    { icon:'⏱', val: Math.round(cfg.uptime || 0) + 's', label:'Uptime' },
  ] : [];

  const quickActions = [
    { label:'/status', cmd:'/status' }, { label:'/files', cmd:'/files' }, { label:'/clear', cmd:'/clear' },
    { label:'/progress', cmd:'/progress' }, { label:'🚀 Deploy', action:()=>router.push('/(panel)/deploy') },
    { label:'🧠 GLM Chat', action:()=>router.push('/(panel)/glm') },
  ];

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap} refreshControl={<RefreshControl refreshing={loading} onRefresh={load} colors={[C.primary]}/>}>
      <View style={s.statsGrid}>
        {stats.map((st,i) => (
          <View key={i} style={s.statCard}>
            <Text style={s.statIcon}>{st.icon}</Text>
            <Text style={s.statVal} numberOfLines={1}>{st.val}</Text>
            <Text style={s.statLabel}>{st.label}</Text>
          </View>
        ))}
      </View>
      <View style={s.card}>
        <Text style={s.cardTitle}>⚡ Quick Actions</Text>
        <View style={s.quickGrid}>
          {quickActions.map((a,i) => (
            <Pressable key={i} style={s.quickBtn} onPress={a.action || (() => send(a.cmd))}>
              <Text style={s.quickBtnText}>{a.label}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          ))}
        </View>
      </View>
      <View style={s.card}>
        <Text style={s.cardTitle}>💬 Recent Messages</Text>
        {msgs.length ? msgs.map((m,i) => (
          <View key={i} style={s.msgItem}>
            <Text style={s.msgFrom}>{m.from}</Text>
            <Text style={s.msgText} numberOfLines={2}>{m.text || '(non-text)'}</Text>
          </View>
        )) : <Text style={s.empty}>No messages yet</Text>}
      </View>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap: { padding:24, gap:20, paddingBottom:40 },
  statsGrid: { flexDirection:'row', flexWrap:'wrap', gap:12 },
  statCard: { backgroundColor:C.surface, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:14, padding:16, width:'31%', minWidth:140, alignItems:'center', gap:4 },
  statIcon: { fontSize:24 }, statVal: { fontSize:16, fontWeight:'700', color:C.text }, statLabel: { fontSize:11, color:C.text3 },
  card: { backgroundColor:C.surface, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:14, padding:20 },
  cardTitle: { fontSize:16, fontWeight:'600', color:C.text, marginBottom:14 },

panel_screen("bot", """import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

interface Msg { from:string; text:string; date:string; }

export default function BotScreen() {
  const [cmd, setCmd] = useState('');
  const [msgs, setMsgs] = useState<Msg[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const scrollRef = useRef<ScrollView>(null);
  const inputRef = useRef<TextInput>(null);

  const load = async () => { const r = await api.botMessages(); if (r?.messages) setMsgs(r.messages); };
  useEffect(() => { load(); const iv = setInterval(load, 10000); return () => clearInterval(iv); }, []);

  const send = async () => {
    const c = cmd.trim(); if (!c) return; setCmd('');
    setLoading(true);
    await api.botCommand(c);
    setLoading(false);
    setTimeout(load, 2000);
  };

  const presets = ['/status','/files','/clear','/progress','/p1','/loop python expert','/analyze','/code factorial'];

  return (
    <View style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.inputRow}>
        <TextInput ref={inputRef} style={s.input} placeholder="Type /command or message..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3}
          value={cmd} onChangeText={setCmd} onSubmitEditing={send} editable={!loading}
          selectTextOnFocus />
        <Pressable style={[s.sendBtn, loading && s.sendBtnDis]} onPress={send} disabled={loading}>
          <Text style={s.sendText}>→</Text>
        </Pressable>
      </View>
      <ScrollView horizontal showsHorizontalScrollIndicator={false} style={s.presetsWrap}>
        {presets.map((p,i) => (
          <Pressable key={i} style={s.preset} onPress={() => { setCmd(p); inputRef.current?.focus(); }}>
            <Text style={s.presetText}>{p}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
      </ScrollView>
      <View style={s.msgsWrap}>
        <ScrollView ref={scrollRef} contentContainerStyle={s.msgsList} onContentSizeChange={() => scrollRef.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true})}>
          {msgs.length ? msgs.map((m,i) => (
            <View key={i} style={s.msgItem}>
              <Text style={s.msgFrom}>{m.from}</Text>
              <Text style={s.msgText}>{m.text || '(non-text)'}</Text>
              <Text style={s.msgDate}>{m.date?.split('T')[1]?.slice(0,5)||''}</Text>
            </View>
          )) : <Text style={s.empty}>No messages. Send /start to bot first.</Text>}
          {loading && <Text style={s.empty}>Sending...</Text>}
        </ScrollView>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

panel_screen("glm", """import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

interface M { role:string; content:string; }

export default function GLMScreen() {
  const [msgs, setMsgs] = useState<M[]>([{ role:'system', content:'GLM Ready. Orice tip de prompt acceptat — code, security, analysis, etc.' }]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const scrollRef = useRef<ScrollView>(null);

  const send = async () => {
    const t = input.trim(); if (!t || loading) return;
    setInput('');
    setMsgs(p => [...p, { role:'user', content:t }]);
    setLoading(true);
    const res = await api.glmChat(t);
    setMsgs(p => [...p, { role:'assistant', content: res?.response || res?.error || 'Error' }]);
    setLoading(false);
    setTimeout(() => scrollRef.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true}), 100);
  };

  const fmt = (text: string) => {
    let h = text;
    h = h.replace(/\`\`\`([a-zA-Z0-9_+-]*)\\n?([\\s\\S]*?)\`\`\`/g, '[CODE BLOCK]\\n$2\\n[/CODE]');
    h = h.replace(/\`([^\`]+)\`/g, '`$1`');
    h = h.replace(/\\*\\*([^*]+)\\*\\*/g, '$1');
    h = h.replace(/\\n/g, '\\n');
    return h;
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView style={s.wrap} behavior={Platform.OS==='ios'?'padding':undefined}>
      <ScrollView ref={scrollRef} style={s.chat} contentContainerStyle={s.chatInner}
        onContentSizeChange={() => scrollRef.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true})}>
        {msgs.map((m,i) => (
          <View key={i} style={[s.msg, m.role==='user'?s.msgUser : m.role==='system'?s.msgSys : s.msgBot]}>
            <Text style={s.msgText} selectable>{fmt(m.content)}</Text>
          </View>
        ))}
        {loading && <View style={s.msgSys}><Text style={s.msgText}>Thinking...</Text></View>}
      </ScrollView>
      <View style={s.inputBar}>
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Ask anything..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3}
          value={input} onChangeText={setInput} onSubmitEditing={send} editable={!loading} multiline />
        <Pressable style={[s.sendBtn, loading&&s.sendDis]} onPress={send} disabled={loading}>
          <Text style={s.sendTxt}>→</Text>
        </Pressable>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap: { flex:1 },
  chat: { flex:1, backgroundColor:C.bg, margin:20, borderRadius:10, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border },
  chatInner: { padding:12, gap:8, flexGrow:1 },
  msg: { maxWidth:'85%', padding:12, borderRadius:12 },
  msgUser: { alignSelf:'flex-end', backgroundColor:'#1e3a5f' },
  msgBot: { alignSelf:'flex-start', backgroundColor:C.surface, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border },
  msgSys: { alignSelf:'center', backgroundColor:'transparent' },
  msgText: { color:'#e2e8f0', fontSize:14, lineHeight:20, fontFamily: Platform.OS==='web' ? 'monospace' : undefined },
  inputBar: { flexDirection:'row', padding:12, gap:8, backgroundColor:C.surface, borderTopWidth:1, borderTopColor:C.border },
  input: { flex:1, padding:12, backgroundColor:C.bg, borderRadius:10, color:C.text, fontSize:14, maxHeight:100 },
  sendBtn: { backgroundColor:C.primary2, borderRadius:10, width:48, alignItems:'center', justifyContent:'center' },
  sendDis: { opacity:0.5 },
  sendTxt: { color:'#fff', fontSize:18, fontWeight:'700' },
});
""")

panel_screen("files", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, RefreshControl, Alert, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

interface F { name:string; size:number; uploaded:string; }

export default function FilesScreen() {
  const [downloads, setDownloads] = useState<F[]>([]);
  const [generated, setGenerated] = useState<F[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const load = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const r = await api.files();
    if (r) { setDownloads(r.downloads||[]); setGenerated(r.generated||[]); }
    setLoading(false);
  };
  useEffect(() => { load(); }, []);

  const del = async (name: string) => {
    if (!confirm('Delete ' + name + '?')) return;
    await api.files(); // call delete via separate fetch
    const res = await fetch('/api/files', { method:'DELETE', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, credentials:'include', body: JSON.stringify({name}) });
    if (res.ok) { load(); } else { alert('Failed'); }
  };

  const dl = (name: string) => {
    if (Platform.OS === 'web') window.open('/api/files/' + encodeURIComponent(name));
  };

  const fmtSize = (b: number) => b > 1024 ? (b/1024).toFixed(1)+' KB' : b+' B';

  const FileRow = ({ f, onDel }: { f:F; onDel:()=>void }) => (
    <View style={s.fileRow}>
      <Text style={s.fileName} numberOfLines={1}>{f.name}</Text>
      <Text style={s.fileSize}>{fmtSize(f.size)}</Text>
      <Pressable style={s.dlBtn} onPress={() => dl(f.name)}><Text style={s.dlTxt}>⬇</Text></Pressable>
      <Pressable style={s.delBtn} onPress={onDel}><Text style={s.delTxt}>🗑</Text></Pressable>
    </View>
  );

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap} refreshControl={<RefreshControl refreshing={loading} onRefresh={load} colors={[C.primary]}/>}>
      <View style={s.card}>
        <Text style={s.cardTitle}>📥 Uploaded Files ({downloads.length})</Text>
        {downloads.length ? downloads.map((f,i) => <FileRow key={i} f={f} onDel={() => del(f.name)} />)
          : <Text style={s.empty}>No uploads yet</Text>}
      </View>
      <View style={s.card}>
        <Text style={s.cardTitle}>💻 Generated Code ({generated.length})</Text>
        {generated.length ? generated.map((f,i) => <FileRow key={i} f={f} onDel={() => del(f.name)} />)
          : <Text style={s.empty}>No generated files yet</Text>}
      </View>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap: { padding:20, gap:16, paddingBottom:40 },
  card: { backgroundColor:C.surface, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:14, padding:20 },
  cardTitle: { fontSize:16, fontWeight:'600', color:C.text, marginBottom:12 },
  fileRow: { flexDirection:'row', alignItems:'center', padding:10, borderBottomWidth:1, borderBottomColor:C.border, gap:10 },
  fileName: { flex:1, color:C.text, fontSize:13 },
  fileSize: { color:C.text3, fontSize:12, width:70, textAlign:'right' },
  dlBtn: { padding:4, backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.15)', borderRadius:5 },
  dlTxt: { color:'#60a5fa', fontSize:14 },
  delBtn: { padding:4, backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.15)', borderRadius:5 },
  delTxt: { color:'#fca5a5', fontSize:14 },
  empty: { color:C.text3, fontSize:13, textAlign:'center', padding:16 },
});
""")

panel_screen("deploy", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Linking, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import * as WebBrowser from 'expo-web-browser';

interface DepStatus { github_repo:string; github_actions:boolean; github_url:string; expo_configured:boolean; uptime:number; }

export default function DeployScreen() {
  const [st, setSt] = useState<DepStatus|null>(null);
  const [ghResult, setGhResult] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => { api.deployStatus().then(r => setSt(r)); }, []);

  const openUrl = (url: string) => Platform.OS === 'web' ? window.open(url) : WebBrowser.openBrowserAsync(url);

  const triggerGH = async () => {
    const r = await api.triggerGitHub();
    if (r?.ok) { setGhResult('✅ ' + r.message); if (r.actions_url) openUrl(r.actions_url); }
    else setGhResult('❌ ' + (r?.error||'Failed'));
  };

  const triggerExpo = async () => {
    const r = await api.triggerExpo();
    if (r?.ok) alert('Expo Deploy:\\n' + r.steps?.join('\\n'));
  };

  const cards = [
    { icon:'🐙', name:'GitHub Actions', desc:'Auto deploy on push to main',
      action: triggerGH, link: st?.github_url, linkLabel:'Open Actions →' },
    { icon:'📱', name:'Expo.dev', desc:'This app is hosted here 24/7',
      action: triggerExpo, link:'https://expo.dev', linkLabel:'Open Expo →' },
    { icon:'🐳', name:'Docker (optional)', desc:'Self-host on your VPS',
      action: () => {}, link:'', linkLabel:'' },
  ];

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.statusBar}>
        <Text style={s.statusText}>✅ This app is hosted on expo.dev — online 24/7</Text>
        {st && <Text style={s.statusSub}>Uptime: {Math.round(st.uptime)}s | Repo: {st.github_repo || 'not set'}</Text>}
      </View>
      {ghResult ? <View style={s.resultBox}><Text style={s.resultText}>{ghResult}</Text></View> : null}
      <View style={s.grid}>
        {cards.map((c,i) => (
          <View key={i} style={s.card}>
            <Text style={s.cardIcon}>{c.icon}</Text>
            <Text style={s.cardName}>{c.name}</Text>
            <Text style={s.cardDesc}>{c.desc}</Text>
            {c.link ? <Pressable onPress={() => openUrl(c.link)}><Text style={s.cardLink}>{c.linkLabel}</Text></Pressable> : null}
            <Pressable style={s.cardBtn} onPress={c.action}><Text style={s.cardBtnText}>Trigger</Text></Pressable>
          </View>
        ))}
      </View>
      <View style={s.instrCard}>
        <Text style={s.instrTitle}>📋 Deploy Workflow</Text>

      </View>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
