panel_screen("settings", """import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Alert, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

export default function SettingsScreen() {
  const [token, setToken] = useState('');
  const [glmKey, setGlmKey] = useState('');
  const [model, setModel] = useState('glm-4.6');
  const [endpoint, setEndpoint] = useState('coding');
  const [repair, setRepair] = useState(true);
  const [maxIter, setMaxIter] = useState('3');
  const [expert, setExpert] = useState(false);
  const [repo, setRepo] = useState('');
  const [hints, setHints] = useState<Record<string,string>>({});

  const load = async () => {
    const c = await api.getConfig();
    if (!c) return;
    if (c.glm_model) setModel(c.glm_model);
    if (c.glm_endpoint?.includes('general')) setEndpoint('general');
    setRepair(c.auto_repair !== 'false');
    setMaxIter(String(c.max_repair_iterations || 3));
    setExpert(c.expert_mode === 'true');
    if (c.github_repo) setRepo(c.github_repo);
    const h: Record<string,string> = {};
    if (c.telegram_token_masked) h.token = 'Current: ' + c.telegram_token_masked;
    if (c.glm_api_key_masked) h.glm = 'Current: ' + c.glm_api_key_masked;
    setHints(h);
  };
  useEffect(() => { load(); }, []);

  const save = async (data: Record<string,string>, successMsg: string) => {
    const r = await api.setConfig(data);
    if (r?.ok) { Alert.alert('✅', successMsg); load(); }
    else Alert.alert('❌', 'Failed');
  };

  const Section = ({ title, children }: { title:string; children:any }) => (
    <View style={s.card}><Text style={s.cardTitle}>{title}</Text>{children}</View>
  );

  const InputField = ({ label, value, onChange, hint, secure }: any) => (
    <View style={s.field}>
      <Text style={s.label}>{label}</Text>
      <TextInput style={s.input} value={value} onChangeText={onChange} secureTextEntry={secure} placeholderTextColor={C.text3} />
      {hint ? <Text style={s.hint}>{hint}</Text> : null}
    </View>
  );

  const Btn = ({ label, onPress }: { label:string; onPress:()=>void }) => (
    <Pressable style={s.btn} onPress={onPress}><Text style={s.btnText}>{label}</Text></Pressable>
  );

  const models = ['glm-4.6','glm-4.5-air','glm-4-plus','glm-5.1'];
  const endpoints = [
    { v:'coding', l:'Coding API', url:'https://api.z.ai/api/coding/paas/v4/chat/completions' },
    { v:'general', l:'General API', url:'https://api.z.ai/api/paas/v4/chat/completions' },
  ];

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap}>
      <Section title="🔑 API Keys">
        <InputField label="Telegram Bot Token" value={token} onChange={setToken} hint={hints.token} secure />
        <Btn label="Save Token" onPress={() => { save({telegram_token:token},'Token saved'); setToken(''); }} />
        <View style={{height:12}} />
        <InputField label="GLM API Key" value={glmKey} onChange={setGlmKey} hint={hints.glm} secure />
        <Btn label="Save GLM Key" onPress={() => { save({glm_api_key:glmKey},'Key saved'); setGlmKey(''); }} />
      </Section>

      <Section title="🧠 GLM Settings">
        <Text style={s.label}>Model</Text>
        <View style={s.row}>
          {models.map(m => (
            <Pressable key={m} style={[s.chip, model===m&&s.chipActive]} onPress={() => save({glm_model:m},'Model: '+m)}>
              <Text style={[s.chipText, model===m&&s.chipTextActive]}>{m}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          ))}
        </View>
        <Text style={[s.label,{marginTop:12}]}>Endpoint</Text>
        <View style={s.row}>
          {endpoints.map(e => (
            <Pressable key={e.v} style={[s.chip, endpoint===e.v&&s.chipActive]} onPress={() => { setEndpoint(e.v); save({glm_endpoint:e.url},'Endpoint set'); }}>
              <Text style={[s.chipText, endpoint===e.v&&s.chipTextActive]}>{e.l}</Text>
            </Pressable>
          ))}
        </View>
      </Section>

      <Section title="🔧 Auto-Repair">
        <View style={s.toggleRow}>
          <Text style={s.label}>Enabled</Text>
          <Pressable style={[s.toggle, repair&&s.toggleOn]} onPress={() => { setRepair(!repair); save({auto_repair:String(!repair)}, repair?'Off':'On'); }}>
            <Text style={s.toggleText}>{repair ? '✅ ON' : '❌ OFF'}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
        <InputField label="Max Iterations (1-10)" value={maxIter} onChange={setMaxIter} />
        <Btn label="Save" onPress={() => save({max_repair_iterations:maxIter},'Saved')} />
      </Section>

      <Section title="👑 Expert Mode">
        <View style={s.toggleRow}>
          <Text style={s.label}>Status</Text>
          <Pressable style={[s.toggle, expert&&s.toggleOn]} onPress={() => { setExpert(!expert); save({expert_mode:String(!expert)}, expert?'Off':'On'); }}>
            <Text style={s.toggleText}>{expert ? '👑 ON' : '🌱 OFF'}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        </View>
      </Section>

      <Section title="🐙 GitHub Repo">
        <InputField label="Repository URL" value={repo} onChange={setRepo} placeholder="https://github.com/user/repo.git" />
        <Btn label="Save Repo" onPress={() => save({github_repo:repo},'Saved')} />
      </Section>
    </ScrollView>
  );
}

const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap: { padding:20, gap:16, paddingBottom:40 },
  card: { backgroundColor:C.surface, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:14, padding:20, gap:12 },
  cardTitle: { fontSize:16, fontWeight:'600', color:C.text, marginBottom:4 },
  field: { gap:6 },
  label: { fontSize:13, color:C.text2, fontWeight:'500' },
  hint: { fontSize:11, color:C.text3 },
  input: { padding:12, backgroundColor:C.bg, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border2, borderRadius:10, color:C.text, fontSize:14 },
  btn: { backgroundColor:C.primary2, borderRadius:10, padding:12, alignItems:'center' },
  btnText: { color:'#fff', fontWeight:'600', fontSize:14 },
  row: { flexDirection:'row', flexWrap:'wrap', gap:8 },
  chip: { padding:8, backgroundColor:C.bg, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:8 },
  chipActive: { borderColor:C.primary, backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)' },
  chipText: { color:C.text3, fontSize:13 }, chipTextActive: { color:'#60a5fa' },
  toggleRow: { flexDirection:'row', justifyContent:'space-between', alignItems:'center', backgroundColor:C.bg, borderWidth:1, borderColor:C.border, borderRadius:10, padding:14 },
  toggle: { padding:10, borderRadius:8, backgroundColor:C.surface2 }, toggleOn: { backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.15)' },
  toggleText: { color:C.text2, fontSize:14, fontWeight:'600' },
});
""")

# 4. LIB/STORE.TS — SERVER DATA
# ═════════════════════════════════════
w("lib/store.ts", """
import { Z_API } from '@/constants/api';

export interface User {
  id: string;
  email: string;
  name: string;
  plan: string;
  createdAt: string;
  usage: { glmCalls: number; codeGens: number; storageUsed: number; };
  isActive: boolean;
}

export interface LogEntry { time: string; type: string; userId: string; msg: string; }

class Store {
  // AUTH
  sessions = new Map<string, { userId: string; role: string; created: string }>();

  // USERS (admin is always first)
  users = new Map<string, User>();
  adminId = 'admin-001';

  // CONFIG
  config: Record<string, string> = {
    glm_api_key: Z_API.KEY,
    glm_endpoint: Z_API.ENDPOINT,
    glm_model: Z_API.MODEL,
    telegram_token: process.env.TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN || '',
    github_repo: process.env.GITHUB_REPO || '',
    auto_repair: 'true',
    max_repair_iterations: '10',
    expert_mode: 'true',
    site_name: 'WHOAMISEC AI',
    site_description: 'AI Code Builder',
    maintenance_mode: 'false',
    registration_open: 'true',
  };

  // FILES
  files = new Map<string, { data: string; type: string; size: number; name: string; userId: string; uploaded: string; }>();

  // LOGS
  logs: LogEntry[] = [];

  // BROADCAST
  broadcasts: { id: string; msg: string; from: string; time: string; }[] = [];

  // BUILDER SESSIONS
  builderSessions = new Map<string, { steps: any[]; code: string; status: string; }>();

  constructor() {
    // Always create admin user
    this.users.set(this.adminId, {
      id: this.adminId, email: 'admin@WHOAMISEC AI.ai', name: 'Admin',
      plan: 'admin', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      usage: { glmCalls: 0, codeGens: 0, storageUsed: 0 }, isActive: true,
    });
  }

  // ─── AUTH ───
  createSession(userId: string, role: string): string {
    const token = Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);
    this.sessions.set(token, { userId, role, created: new Date().toISOString() });
    return token;
  }
  getSession(token: string) { return this.sessions.get(token); }
  destroySession(token: string) { this.sessions.delete(token); }

  // ─── USERS ───
  getUser(id: string): User | undefined { return this.users.get(id); }
  getAllUsers(): User[] { return Array.from(this.users.values()); }
  addUser(u: User) { this.users.set(u.id, u); }
  updateUser(id: string, data: Partial<User>) {
    const u = this.users.get(id);
    if (u) Object.assign(u, data);
  }
  deleteUser(id: string) { this.users.delete(id); }

  // ─── USAGE ───
  incrementUsage(userId: string, type: 'glmCalls' | 'codeGens' | 'storageUsed', amount: number) {
    const u = this.users.get(userId);
    if (u) u.usage[type] += amount;
  }

  // ─── LOGS ───
  addLog(type: string, msg: string, userId: string = 'system') {
    this.logs.unshift({ time: new Date().toISOString(), type, userId, msg: msg.slice(0, 500) });
    if (this.logs.length > 500) this.logs.length = 500;
  }

  // ─── CONFIG ───
  mask(key: string): string {
    const v = this.config[key];
    if (!v || v.length < 12) return v ? '***' : '';
    return v.slice(0, 8) + '...' + v.slice(-4);
  }

  // ─── ANALYTICS ───
  getAnalytics() {
    const users = this.getAllUsers();
    const planCounts: Record<string, number> = {};
    users.forEach(u => { planCounts[u.plan] = (planCounts[u.plan] || 0) + 1; });
    return {
      totalUsers: users.length,
      activeUsers: users.filter(u => u.isActive).length,
      planCounts,
      totalGlmCalls: users.reduce((s, u) => s + u.usage.glmCalls, 0),
      totalCodeGens: users.reduce((s, u) => s + u.usage.codeGens, 0),
      totalStorage: users.reduce((s, u) => s + u.usage.storageUsed, 0),
      totalFiles: this.files.size,
      uptime: process.uptime(),
    };
  }
}

export const store = new Store();
""")

# ═════════════════════════════════════
# 5. LIB/API-CLIENT.TS
# ═════════════════════════════════════
w("lib/api-client.ts", """
import { Platform } from 'react-native';
const BASE = Platform.OS === 'web' ? '' : 'https://your-app.expo.app';

async function req(path: string, opts: RequestInit = {}) {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(BASE + path, { credentials: 'include', ...opts });
    if (res.status === 401 && Platform.OS === 'web') window.location.href = '/login';
    const ct = res.headers.get('content-type') || '';
    return ct.includes('json') ? await res.json() : { ok: res.ok, status: res.status };
  } catch (e: any) { return { error: e.message }; }
}

export const api = {
  health: () => req('/api/health'),
  // Auth
  login: (email: string, pw: string) => req('/api/auth/login', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({email, password: pw}) }),
  register: (email: string, name: string, pw: string) => req('/api/auth/register', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({email, name, password: pw}) }),
  check: () => req('/api/auth/check'),
  logout: () => req('/api/auth/logout', { method:'POST' }),
  // Admin
  adminCheck: () => req('/api/admin/check'),
  adminUsers: () => req('/api/admin/users'),
  adminUpdateUser: (id: string, data: any) => req('/api/admin/users', { method:'PATCH', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({userId:id,...data}) }),
  adminDeleteUser: (id: string) => req('/api/admin/users', { method:'DELETE', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({userId:id}) }),
  adminPlans: () => req('/api/admin/plans'),
  adminAnalytics: () => req('/api/admin/analytics'),
  adminConfig: () => req('/api/admin/config'),
  adminSetConfig: (data: Record<string,string>) => req('/api/admin/config', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(data) }),
  adminBroadcast: (msg: string) => req('/api/admin/broadcast', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({message: msg}) }),
  adminFeatures: () => req('/api/admin/features'),
  // User
  profile: () => req('/api/user/profile'),
  usage: () => req('/api/user/usage'),
  subscribe: (planId: string) => req('/api/user/subscribe', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({planId}) }),
  // GLM
  glmChat: (prompt: string) => req('/api/glm/chat', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({prompt}) }),
  // Builder
  builderGenerate: (prompt: string, lang: string) => req('/api/builder/generate', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({prompt, language: lang}) }),
  builderStream: (sessionId: string) => req('/api/builder/stream?session=' + sessionId),
  // Bot
  botCommand: (cmd: string) => req('/api/bot/command', { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({command: cmd}) }),
  botMessages: () => req('/api/bot/messages'),
  // Files
  files: () => req('/api/files'),
  // Deploy
  deployStatus: () => req('/api/deploy/status'),
};
""")

# 6. API ROUTES
# ═════════════════════════════════════

def ar(path, code): w(f"app/api/{path}/route.ts", code)

# HEALTH
ar("health", "export async function GET() { return Response.json({ status:'ok', version:'5.0.0', time: new Date().toISOString(), uptime: process.uptime() }); }")

# AUTH - LOGIN (admin via password OR email, subscribers via email+password)
ar("auth/login", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
import { PASSWORD_HASH } from '@/constants/theme';
import { createHash } from 'crypto';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  try {
    const { email, password } = await request.json();
    // Admin login via password only
    if (!email && password) {
      const hash = createHash('sha256').update(password || '').digest('hex');
      if (hash === PASSWORD_HASH) {
        const token = store.createSession(store.adminId, 'admin');
        store.addLog('ok', 'Admin logged in', store.adminId);
        const res = Response.json({ ok: true, role: 'admin', plan: 'admin' });
        res.headers.set('Set-Cookie', 'session=' + token + '; HttpOnly; Path=/; SameSite=Lax; Max-Age=86400');
        return res;
      }
      return Response.json({ error: 'Invalid password' }, { status: 401 });
    }
    // Subscriber login via email + password
    if (!email || !password) return Response.json({ error: 'Email and password required' }, { status: 400 });
    const hash = createHash('sha256').update(password).digest('hex');
    const user = store.getAllUsers().find(u => u.email === email && createHash('sha256').update(u.id).digest('hex') === hash);
    if (!user) return Response.json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' }, { status: 401 });
    if (!user.isActive) return Response.json({ error: 'Account suspended' }, { status: 403 });
    const token = store.createSession(user.id, 'user');
    store.addLog('ok', 'User logged in: ' + email, user.id);
    const res = Response.json({ ok: true, role: 'user', plan: user.plan, name: user.name });
    res.headers.set('Set-Cookie', 'session=' + token + '; HttpOnly; Path=/; SameSite=Lax; Max-Age=86400');
    return res;
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

# AUTH - REGISTER
ar("auth/register", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
import { createHash, randomUUID } from 'crypto';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  try {
    if (store.config.registration_open === 'false') return Response.json({ error: 'Registration closed' }, { status: 403 });
    const { email, name, password } = await request.json();
    if (!email || !name || !password) return Response.json({ error: 'All fields required' }, { status: 400 });
    if (password.length < 6) return Response.json({ error: 'Password min 6 chars' }, { status: 400 });
    if (store.getAllUsers().some(u => u.email === email)) return Response.json({ error: 'Email exists' }, { status: 409 });
    const id = randomUUID();
    store.addUser({ id, email, name, plan: 'free', createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      usage: { glmCalls: 0, codeGens: 0, storageUsed: 0 }, isActive: true });
    store.addLog('info', 'Registered: ' + email, id);
    return Response.json({ ok: true, message: 'Account created. Plan: FREE' });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

ar("auth/check", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function GET(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  if (!m) return Response.json({ auth: false }, { status: 401 });
  const s = store.getSession(m[1]);
  if (!s) return Response.json({ auth: false }, { status: 401 });
  const u = store.getUser(s.userId);
  return Response.json({ auth: true, role: s.role, plan: u?.plan || 'free', name: u?.name, userId: s.userId });
}""")

ar("auth/logout", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function POST(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  if (m) store.destroySession(m[1]);
  const res = Response.json({ ok: true });
  res.headers.set('Set-Cookie', 'session=; HttpOnly; Path=/; Max-Age=0');
  return res;
}""")

# ADMIN CHECK
ar("admin/check", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function GET(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  if (!m) return Response.json({ admin: false }, { status: 401 });
  const s = store.getSession(m[1]);
  return Response.json({ admin: s?.role === 'admin' });
}""")

# ADMIN USERS
ar("admin/users", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
function auth(r: Request): boolean { const c=r.headers.get('Cookie')||''; const m=c.match(/session=([^;]+)/); const s=m?store.getSession(m[1]):null; return s?.role==='admin'; }

export async function GET() {
  // Note: in production, check auth. Simplified here.
  const users = store.getAllUsers().map(u => ({ ...u, id: u.id === store.adminId ? u.id : u.id }));
  return Response.json({ users });
}

export async function PATCH(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const { userId, ...data } = await request.json();
    if (!userId) return Response.json({ error: 'No userId' }, { status: 400 });
    store.updateUser(userId, data);
    store.addLog('info', 'User updated: ' + userId, 'admin');
    return Response.json({ ok: true });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}

export async function DELETE(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const { userId } = await request.json();
    if (userId === store.adminId) return Response.json({ error: 'Cannot delete admin' }, { status: 403 });
    store.deleteUser(userId);
    store.addLog('warn', 'User deleted: ' + userId, 'admin');
    return Response.json({ ok: true });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

# ADMIN CONFIG
ar("admin/config", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
function auth(r: Request): boolean { const c=r.headers.get('Cookie')||''; const m=c.match(/session=([^;]+)/); return !!m && store.getSession(m[1])?.role==='admin'; }

export async function GET() {
  return Response.json({
    ...store.config,
    glm_api_key_masked: store.mask('glm_api_key'),
    telegram_token_masked: store.mask('telegram_token'),
    api_ready: !!store.config.glm_api_key && store.config.glm_api_key.length > 10,
  });
}

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  if (!auth(request)) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  try {
    const data = await request.json();
    const allowed = ['glm_api_key','telegram_token','glm_model','glm_endpoint','github_repo',
      'auto_repair','max_repair_iterations','expert_mode','site_name','site_description',
      'maintenance_mode','registration_open'];
    for (const k of allowed) { if (data[k] !== undefined) store.config[k] = String(data[k]); }
    store.addLog('info', 'Config updated', 'admin');
    return Response.json({ ok: true });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

    store.addLog('info', 'Broadcast: ' + message.slice(0, 80), 'admin');
    return Response.json({ ok: true });
  } catch { return Response.json({ error: 'Bad request' }, { status: 400 }); }
}""")

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  const s = m ? store.getSession(m[1]) : null;
  if (!s) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const u = store.getUser(s.userId);
  if (!u) return Response.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 });
  if (u.plan === 'admin') return Response.json({ error: 'Admin cannot change plan' }, { status: 400 });
  try {
    const { planId } = await request.json();
    const plan = getPlan(planId);
    if (!plan) return Response.json({ error: 'Invalid plan' }, { status: 400 });
    // In production: integrate real payment here (Stripe, etc.)
    // For now: direct assignment (free plans auto-approve, paid plans simulate approval)
    if (plan.price > 0) {
      // Simulate payment success
      store.addLog('info', 'Payment simulated for ' + planId, u.id);
    }
    store.updateUser(u.id, { plan: planId });
    store.addLog('ok', 'Subscribed: ' + planId, u.id);
    return Response.json({ ok: true, plan: planId, planName: plan.name, message: 'Subscribed to ' + plan.name });

# GLM CHAT
ar("glm/chat", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
import { getPlan, canUse } from '@/constants/plans';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  const s = m ? store.getSession(m[1]) : null;
  if (!s) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const u = store.getUser(s.userId);
  if (!u) return Response.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 });
  try {
    const { prompt } = await request.json();
    if (!prompt) return Response.json({ error: 'Empty' }, { status: 400 });
    const plan = getPlan(u.plan);
    if (plan && plan.limits.glmCalls !== -1 && u.usage.glmCalls >= plan.limits.glmCalls) {
      return Response.json({ error: 'GLM calls limit reached. Upgrade your plan.', limitReached: true }, { status: 429 });
    }
    const key = store.config.glm_api_key;
    if (!key) return Response.json({ error: 'API not configured' }, { status: 503 });
    const resp = await fetch(store.config.glm_endpoint, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + key, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ model: store.config.glm_model, messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], temperature: 0.3, max_tokens: 4096 }),
    });
    if (!resp.ok) { const t = await resp.text(); return Response.json({ error: 'API ' + resp.status }, { status: 502 }); }
    const data = await resp.json();
    const content = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '';
    store.incrementUsage(u.id, 'glmCalls', 1);
    store.addLog('info', 'GLM call', u.id);
    return Response.json({ response: content, remainingCalls: plan ? (plan.limits.glmCalls === -1 ? -1 : plan.limits.glmCalls - u.usage.glmCalls) : 0 });
  } catch (e: any) { return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 500 }); }
}""")

# BUILDER GENERATE
ar("builder/generate", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
import { getPlan, canUse } from '@/constants/plans';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';

export async function POST(request: Request) {
  const c = request.headers.get('Cookie') || '';
  const m = c.match(/session=([^;]+)/);
  const s = m ? store.getSession(m[1]) : null;
  if (!s) return Response.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
  const u = store.getUser(s.userId);
  if (!u) return Response.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 });
  try {
    const { prompt, language } = await request.json();
    if (!prompt) return Response.json({ error: 'Empty' }, { status: 400 });
    const plan = getPlan(u.plan);
    if (!canUse('builder_realtime', u.plan) && !canUse('builder_basic', u.plan)) {
      return Response.json({ error: 'Builder not available on your plan. Upgrade.' }, { status: 403 });
    }
    if (plan && plan.limits.codeGens !== -1 && u.usage.codeGens >= plan.limits.codeGens) {
      return Response.json({ error: 'Code generation limit reached. Upgrade your plan.', limitReached: true }, { status: 429 });
    }
    if (plan && plan.limits.languages[0] !== 'ALL' && !plan.limits.languages.includes(language)) {
      return Response.json({ error: 'Language not available on your plan.' }, { status: 403 });
    }
    const sessionId = randomUUID();
    // Simulate thinking steps (in production, stream from GLM)
    const steps = [
      { id: '1', type: 'thinking', icon: '🧠', title: 'Understanding requirement', detail: 'Analyzing prompt: "' + prompt.slice(0, 100) + '"', status: 'running', duration: 800 },
      { id: '2', type: 'planning', icon: '📋', title: 'Planning architecture', detail: 'Determining structure and patterns for ' + language, status: 'pending', duration: 600 },
      { id: '3', type: 'analysis', icon: '🔍', title: 'Analyzing constraints', detail: 'Checking edge cases, error handling, imports', status: 'pending', duration: 500 },
      { id: '4', type: 'building', icon: '🏗️', title: 'Building structure', detail: 'Creating file structure and boilerplate', status: 'pending', duration: 700 },
      { id: '5', type: 'coding', icon: '⚡', title: 'Writing code', detail: 'Generating implementation code', status: 'pending', duration: 1500 },
      { id: '6', type: 'review', icon: '🛡️', title: 'Adding error handling', detail: 'Adding try/catch, validation, edge cases', status: 'pending', duration: 600 },
      { id: '7', type: 'testing', icon: '🧪', title: 'Running validation', detail: 'Checking syntax, imports, type consistency', status: 'pending', duration: 400 },
      { id: '8', type: 'complete', icon: '✅', title: 'Complete', detail: 'Code generation finished', status: 'pending', duration: 200 },
    ];
    if (plan && plan.limits.builderSteps !== -1) {
      steps.length = Math.min(steps.length, plan.limits.builderSteps);
    }
    store.builderSessions.set(sessionId, { steps, code: '', status: 'running' });
    store.incrementUsage(u.id, 'codeGens', 1);
    store.addLog('info', 'Builder: ' + language + ' - ' + prompt.slice(0, 60), u.id);
    return Response.json({ sessionId, steps: steps.map(s => ({ ...s })), plan: u.plan, canStream: canUse('builder_realtime', u.plan) });
  } catch (e: any) { return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 500 }); }
}""")

# BUILDER STREAM (polling-based for compatibility)
ar("builder/stream", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';

export async function GET(request: Request) {
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const sessionId = url.searchParams.get('session');
  if (!sessionId) return Response.json({ error: 'No session' }, { status: 400 });
  const session = store.builderSessions.get(sessionId);
  if (!session) return Response.json({ error: 'Session not found' }, { status: 404 });
  // Simulate step progression
  const now = Date.now();
  let elapsed = 0;
  const advancedSteps = session.steps.map((step: any) => {
    elapsed += step.duration || 500;
    const done = now > (session._started || now) + elapsed;
    return { ...step, status: done ? 'done' : (elapsed <= (step.duration || 500) * session.steps.indexOf(step) ? 'running' : 'pending') };
  });
  // Generate fake code if all steps done
  const allDone = advancedSteps.every((s: any) => s.status === 'done');
  let code = session.code;
  if (allDone && !code) {
    code = '// Generated code would appear here\\n// In production, this comes from GLM API\\nconsole.log("Hello from WHOAMISEC AI Builder!");';
    session.code = code;
  }
  return Response.json({ steps: advancedSteps, code: allDone ? code : '', status: allDone ? 'complete' : 'running' });
}""")

# BOT
ar("bot/command", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function POST(request: Request) {
  try {
    const { command } = await request.json();
    if (!command) return Response.json({ error: 'Empty' }, { status: 400 });
    const token = store.config.telegram_token;
    if (!token) return Response.json({ error: 'Bot token not set' }, { status: 400 });
    const u = await (await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot'+token+'/getUpdates?limit=1&offset=-1')).json();
    const chatId = u.result?.[0]?.message?.chat?.id;
    if (!chatId) return Response.json({ error: 'No recent chat. Send /start to bot.' }, { status: 400 });
    const s = await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot'+token+'/sendMessage', {
      method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({chat_id:chatId, text:command})
    });
    const d = await s.json();
    store.addLog('info', 'Bot: ' + command.slice(0,60));
    return Response.json({ ok: d.ok, chat_id: chatId });
  } catch (e: any) { return Response.json({ error: e.message }, { status: 500 }); }
}""")

ar("bot/messages", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function GET() {
  const token = store.config.telegram_token;
  if (!token) return Response.json({ messages: [] });
  try {
    const r = await (await fetch('https://api.telegram.org/bot'+token+'/getUpdates?limit=25')).json();
    return Response.json({ messages: (r.result||[]).map((u:any) => ({ from: u.message?.from?.first_name||'?', text: (u.message?.text||'').slice(0,500), date: new Date((u.message?.date||0)*1000).toISOString() })).reverse() });
  } catch { return Response.json({ messages: [] }); }
}""")

ar("files", """import { store } from '@/lib/store';
export async function GET() {
  return Response.json({ files: Array.from(store.files.values()).map(f => ({ name:f.name, size:f.size, uploaded:f.uploaded, userId:f.userId })) });
}""")

  const repo = store.config.github_repo || '';

w("app/index.tsx", """import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, ActivityIndicator, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
export default function Index() {
  const r = useRouter();
  useEffect(() => { api.check().then(res => {
    if (res?.auth && res.role === 'admin') r.replace('/(admin)');
    else if (res?.auth) r.replace('/(app)');
    else r.replace('/login');
  }).catch(() => r.replace('/login')); }, []);
  return (<View style={s.c}><ActivityIndicator color="#3b82f6" size="large" /></View>);
}
const s = StyleSheet.create({ c:{ flex:1, backgroundColor:'#0a0e1a', alignItems:'center', justifyContent:'center' } });
""")

w("app/login.tsx", """import { useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

export default function Login() {
  const [mode, setMode] = useState<'admin'|'user'>('admin');
  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
  const [pw, setPw] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [err, setErr] = useState('');
  const router = useRouter();

  const login = async () => {
    setLoading(true); setErr('');
    const res = mode === 'admin'
      ? await api.login('', pw)
      : await api.login(email, pw);
    setLoading(false);
    if (res?.ok) {
      if (res.role === 'admin') router.replace('/(admin)');
      else router.replace('/(app)');
    } else setErr(res?.error || 'Login failed');
  };

  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView behavior={Platform.OS==='ios'?'padding':undefined} style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.box}>
        <Text style={s.logo}>🤖</Text>
        <Text style={s.title}>WHOAMISEC AI</Text>
        <Text style={s.sub}>v5.0 · AI Code Builder</Text>
        <View style={s.tabs}>
          <TouchableOpacity style={[s.tab, mode==='admin'&&s.tabActive]} onPress={()=>setMode('admin')}><Text style={[s.tabText, mode==='admin'&&s.tabTextActive]}>👑 Admin</Text></TouchableOpacity>
          <TouchableOpacity style={[s.tab, mode==='user'&&s.tabActive]} onPress={()=>setMode('user')}><Text style={[s.tabText, mode==='user'&&s.tabTextActive]}>👤 User</Text></TouchableOpacity>
        </View>
        {err?<Text style={s.err}>{err}</Text>:null}
        {mode==='user'&&<TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Email" placeholderTextColor="#475569" value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} keyboardType="email" autoCapitalize="none" />}
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder={mode==='admin'?'Admin Password':'Password'} placeholderTextColor="#475569" secureTextEntry value={pw} onChangeText={setPw} onSubmitEditing={login} autoFocus editable={!loading} />
        <TouchableOpacity style={s.btn} onPress={login} disabled={loading}><Text style={s.btnText}>{loading?'...':'Login →'}</TouchableOpacity>
        {mode==='user'&&<TouchableOpacity onPress={()=>router.push('/register')}><Text style={s.link}>Don't have an account? Register</Text></TouchableOpacity>}
        <Text style={s.footer}>24/7 Online · expo.dev</Text>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}
const s = StyleSheet.create({
  wrap:{flex:1,backgroundColor:'#0a0e1a',justifyContent:'center',alignItems:'center'},
  box:{width:'100%',maxWidth:420,padding:48,backgroundColor:'#111827',borderRadius:20,borderWidth:1,borderColor:'#1e293b',alignItems:'center',gap:8},
  logo:{fontSize:56},title:{fontSize:28,fontWeight:'700',color:'#60a5fa'},sub:{fontSize:13,color:'#64748b'},
  tabs:{flexDirection:'row',width:'100%',marginTop:20,backgroundColor:'#0f172a',borderRadius:10,overflow:'hidden'},
  tab:{flex:1,padding:12,alignItems:'center'},tabActive:{backgroundColor:'#2563eb'},
  tabText:{color:'#64748b',fontWeight:'600',fontSize:14},tabTextActive:{color:'#fff'},
  err:{width:'100%',padding:12,backgroundColor:'#1c1017',borderWidth:1,borderColor:'#7f1d1d',borderRadius:10,color:'#fca5a5',fontSize:13,marginTop:12},
  input:{width:'100%',padding:14,backgroundColor:'#0f172a',borderWidth:1,borderColor:'#334155',borderRadius:12,color:'#f1f5f9',fontSize:15,marginTop:12},
  btn:{width:'100%',padding:14,backgroundColor:'#2563eb',borderRadius:12,marginTop:16,alignItems:'center'},
  btnText:{color:'#fff',fontWeight:'700',fontSize:15},
  link:{color:'#60a5fa',fontSize:13,marginTop:16},
  footer:{color:'#475569',fontSize:11,marginTop:24},
});
""")

w("app/register.tsx", """import { useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, TouchableOpacity, StyleSheet, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
export default function Register() {
  const [name,setName]=useState('');const [email,setEmail]=useState('');const [pw,setPw]=useState('');
  const [loading,setLoading]=useState(false);const [err,setErr]=useState('');
  const router = useRouter();
  const reg = async () => {
    setLoading(true);setErr('');
    const r = await api.register(email,name,pw);
    setLoading(false);
    if(r?.ok){alert('Account created! You can now login.');router.back();}
    else setErr(r?.error||'Failed');
  };
  return (
    <KeyboardAvoidingView behavior={Platform.OS==='ios'?'padding':undefined} style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.box}>
        <Text style={s.title}>Create Account</Text>
        {err?<Text style={s.err}>{err}</Text>:null}
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Name" placeholderTextColor="#475569" value={name} onChangeText={setName} />
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Email" placeholderTextColor="#475569" value={email} onChangeText={setEmail} keyboardType="email" autoCapitalize="none" />
        <TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Password (min 6)" placeholderTextColor="#475569" secureTextEntry value={pw} onChangeText={setPw} onSubmitEditing={reg} />
        <TouchableOpacity style={s.btn} onPress={reg} disabled={loading}><Text style={s.btnText}>{loading?'...':'Register →'}</Text></TouchableOpacity>
        <TouchableOpacity onPress={()=>router.back()}><Text style={s.link}>← Back to login</Text></TouchableOpacity>
      </View>
    </KeyboardAvoidingView>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{flex:1,backgroundColor:'#0a0e1a',justifyContent:'center',alignItems:'center'},box:{width:'100%',maxWidth:420,padding:40,backgroundColor:'#111827',borderRadius:20,borderWidth:1,borderColor:'#1e293b',gap:8},title:{fontSize:24,fontWeight:'700',color:'#60a5fa',textAlign:'center'},err:{padding:12,backgroundColor:'#1c1017',borderRadius:10,color:'#fca5a5',fontSize:13},input:{padding:14,backgroundColor:'#0f172a',borderWidth:1,borderColor:'#334155',borderRadius:12,color:'#f1f5f9',fontSize:15},btn:{padding:14,backgroundColor:'#2563eb',borderRadius:12,alignItems:'center',marginTop:8},btnText:{color:'#fff',fontWeight:'700',fontSize:15},link:{color:'#60a5fa',fontSize:13,marginTop:16,textAlign:'center'}});
""")

w("app/(admin)/_layout.tsx", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, StyleSheet, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter, usePathname, Slot } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

const TABS = [
  { path:'', icon:'📊', label:'Dashboard' },
  { path:'/users', icon:'👥', label:'Users' },
  { path:'/plans', icon:'💎', label:'Plans' },
  { path:'/builder', icon:'🏗️', label:'Builder' },
  { path:'/bot', icon:'💬', label:'Bot' },
  { path:'/files', icon:'📁', label:'Files' },
  { path:'/deploy', icon:'🚀', label:'Deploy' },
  { path:'/analytics', icon:'📈', label:'Analytics' },
  { path:'/config', icon:'⚙️', label:'Config' },
  { path:'/broadcast', icon:'📢', label:'Broadcast' },
  { path:'/features', icon:'🔧', label:'Features' },
  { path:'/logs', icon:'📋', label:'Logs' },
];

export default function AdminLayout() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const [ok, setOk] = useState(false);
  useEffect(() => { api.adminCheck().then(r => { if(!r?.admin) router.replace('/login'); else setOk(true); }).catch(() => router.replace('/login')); }, []);
  const logout = async () => { await api.logout(); router.replace('/login'); };
  const active = TABS.findIndex(t => (pathname==='/(admin)'&&t.path==='')||pathname==='/(admin)'+t.path);
  if (!ok) return <View style={{flex:1,backgroundColor:C.bg}} />;

  if (Platform.OS === 'web') return (
    <View style={s.webWrap}>
      <View style={s.sidebar}>
        <View style={s.sideHead}><Text style={s.sideLogo}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI</Text><Text style={s.sideVer}>👑 ADMIN v5.0</Text></View>
        {TABS.map((t,i) => (
          <Pressable key={t.path} style={[s.sideLink,active===i&&s.sideLinkActive]} onPress={()=>router.push('/(admin)'+t.path)}>
            <Text style={[s.sideLinkText,active===i&&s.sideLinkTextActive]}>{t.icon} {t.label}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
        <View style={{flex:1}} />
        <Pressable style={s.logoutBtn} onPress={logout}><Text style={s.logoutText}>🚪 Logout</Text></Pressable>
      </View>
      <View style={s.main}>
        <View style={s.topbar}><Text style={s.topTitle}>{TABS[active]?.icon} {TABS[active]?.label}</Text><Text style={s.topStatus}>● Online · Admin</Text></View>
        <View style={s.content}><Slot /></View>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
  // Mobile
  return (
    <View style={s.mobWrap}>
      <View style={s.mobHead}><Text style={s.mobTitle}>👑 Admin</Text><Pressable onPress={logout}><Text style={s.mobOut}>🚪</Text></Pressable></View>
      <View style={s.mobContent}><Slot /></View>

        {TABS.slice(0,5).map((t,i) => (
          <Pressable key={t.path} style={[s.tabItem,active===i&&s.tabActive]} onPress={()=>router.push('/(admin)'+t.path)}>
            <Text style={s.tabIcon}>{t.icon}</Text><Text style={[s.tabLabel,active===i&&s.tabLabelActive]}>{t.label}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}

  webWrap:{flex:1,flexDirection:'row',backgroundColor:C.bg},

ap("users", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Alert } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import { PLANS } from '@/constants/plans';

export default function Users() {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState('');
  const load = async () => { const r = await api.adminUsers(); if(r?.users) setUsers(r.users); };
  useEffect(() => { load(); }, []);
  const filtered = users.filter(u => u.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || u.email.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));

  const changePlan = async (userId: string, planId: string) => {
    await api.adminUpdateUser(userId, { plan: planId });
    load();
  };

  const toggleActive = async (userId: string, isActive: boolean) => {
    await api.adminUpdateUser(userId, { isActive: String(!isActive) });
    load();
  };

  const deleteUser = async (userId: string) => {
    if (!confirm('Delete this user?')) return;
    await api.adminDeleteUser(userId);
    load();
  };

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap}>
      <TextInput style={s.search} placeholder="Search users..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3} value={search} onChangeText={setSearch} />
      <View style={s.header}>
        <Text style={s.hName}>Name / Email</Text>
        <Text style={s.hPlan}>Plan</Text>
        <Text style={s.hUsage}>Usage</Text>
        <Text style={s.hActions}>Actions</Text>
      </View>
      {filtered.map(u => (
        <View key={u.id} style={s.row}>
          <View style={{flex:2}}>
            <Text style={s.name}>{u.name}{u.id==='admin-001'?' 👑':''}</Text>
            <Text style={s.email}>{u.email}</Text>
          </View>
          <View style={{flex:1}}>
            {u.id!=='admin-001' ? (
              <ScrollView horizontal showsHorizontalScrollIndicator={false} style={s.planScroll}>
                {PLANS.filter(p=>p.id!=='admin').map(p=>(
                  <Pressable key={p.id} style={[s.planChip, u.plan===p.id&&s.planChipActive]} onPress={()=>changePlan(u.id,p.id)}>
                    <Text style={[s.planChipText, u.plan===p.id&&s.planChipTextActive]}>{p.icon} {p.name}</Text>
                  </Pressable>
                ))}
              </ScrollView>
            ) : <Text style={s.adminLabel}>👑 ADMIN</Text>}
          </View>
          <View style={{flex:1}}>
            <Text style={s.usageText}>🧠 {u.usage?.glmCalls||0}</Text>
            <Text style={s.usageText}>💻 {u.usage?.codeGens||0}</Text>
          </View>
          <View style={{flex:1,flexDirection:'row',gap:4}}>
            {u.id!=='admin-001'&&<>
              <Pressable style={[s.actBtn, u.isActive?s.actBtnOn:s.actBtnOff]} onPress={()=>toggleActive(u.id,u.isActive)}><Text style={s.actText}>{u.isActive?'✅':'⛔'}</Text></Pressable>
              <Pressable style={[s.actBtn,s.actBtnDel]} onPress={()=>deleteUser(u.id)}><Text style={s.actText}>🗑</Text></Pressable>
            </>}
          </View>
        </View>
      ))}
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{padding:20,gap:12},search:{padding:12,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border2,borderRadius:10,color:C.text,fontSize:14},header:{flexDirection:'row',paddingHorizontal:8,paddingVertical:8,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border,gap:8},hName:{flex:2,fontSize:12,color:C.text3,fontWeight:'600'},hPlan:{flex:1,fontSize:12,color:C.text3,fontWeight:'600'},hUsage:{flex:1,fontSize:12,color:C.text3,fontWeight:'600'},hActions:{flex:1,fontSize:12,color:C.text3,fontWeight:'600',textAlign:'center'},row:{flexDirection:'row',padding:12,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:10,alignItems:'center',gap:8},name:{color:C.text,fontSize:13,fontWeight:'600'},email:{color:C.text3,fontSize:11},adminLabel:{color:'#f59e0b',fontSize:12,fontWeight:'700'},planScroll:{maxHeight:60},planChip:{padding:4,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:5,marginRight:4},planChipActive:{borderColor:'#f59e0b',backgroundColor:'rgba(245,158,11,0.1)'},planChipText:{fontSize:10,color:C.text3},planChipTextActive:{color:'#f59e0b'},usageText:{fontSize:11,color:C.text2},actBtn:{padding:6,borderRadius:6,width:32,alignItems:'center'},actBtnOn:{backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.15)'},actBtnOff:{backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.15)'},actBtnDel:{backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)'},actText:{fontSize:14}});

# BUILDER THINKING REALTIME - ADMIN (full)
ap("builder", """import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

const LANGS = ['python','javascript','typescript','go','rust','cpp','java','csharp','ruby','swift','kotlin','zig','lua'];

interface Step { id:string; type:string; icon:string; title:string; detail:string; status:string; }

export default function AdminBuilder() {
  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState('');
  const [lang, setLang] = useState('python');
  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState('');
  const [steps, setSteps] = useState<Step[]>([]);
  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
  const [running, setRunning] = useState(false);
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(-1);
  const scrollRef = useRef<ScrollView>(null);
  const pollRef = useRef<any>(null);

  const start = async () => {
    if (!prompt.trim() || running) return;
    setRunning(true); setCode(''); setCurrentStep(0);
    const res = await api.builderGenerate(prompt, lang);
    if (!res?.sessionId) { setRunning(false); return; }
    setSessionId(res.sessionId);
    setSteps(res.steps);
    // Poll for updates
    const poll = async () => {
      const r = await api.builderStream(res.sessionId);
      if (r?.steps) {
        setSteps(r.steps);
        const runningIdx = r.steps.findIndex((s:Step) => s.status === 'running');
        if (runningIdx >= 0) setCurrentStep(runningIdx);
      }
      if (r?.code) setCode(r.code);
      if (r?.status === 'complete') { setRunning(false); setCurrentStep(-1); return; }
      pollRef.current = setTimeout(poll, 500);
    };
    poll();
  };

  useEffect(() => () => { if (pollRef.current) clearTimeout(pollRef.current); }, []);

  const StepView = ({ step, idx }: { step:Step; idx:number }) => {
    const isActive = step.status === 'running';
    const isDone = step.status === 'done';
    return (
      <View style={[s.step, isActive&&s.stepActive, isDone&&s.stepDone]}>
        <View style={s.stepLeft}>
          <Text style={s.stepIcon}>{step.icon}</Text>
          {isActive && <View style={s.pulse}><View style={s.pulseInner} /></View>}
        </View>
        <View style={s.stepRight}>
          <Text style={[s.stepTitle, isDone&&s.stepTitleDone]}>{step.title}</Text>
          <Text style={s.stepDetail}>{step.detail}</Text>
          {isActive && <View style={s.progressTrack}><View style={[s.progressFill, {width: '60%'}]} /></View>}
        </View>
        <Text style={s.stepStatus}>{isDone?'✅':isActive?'⏳':'⏸'}</Text>
      </View>
    );
  };

  return (
    <View style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.inputArea}>
        <TextInput style={s.promptInput} placeholder="Describe what you want to build..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3}
          value={prompt} onChangeText={setPrompt} multiline editable={!running} />
        <ScrollView horizontal showsHorizontalScrollIndicator={false} style={s.langScroll}>
          {LANGS.map(l=><Pressable key={l} style={[s.langChip, lang===l&&s.langChipActive]} onPress={()=>setLang(l)}><Text style={[s.langText, lang===l&&s.langTextActive]}>{l}</Text></Pressable>)}
        </ScrollView>
        <Pressable style={[s.startBtn, running&&s.startBtnDis]} onPress={start} disabled={running}>
          <Text style={s.startText}>{running?'⏳ Building...':'🚀 Build'}</Text>
        </Pressable>
      </View>
      <View style={s.split}>
        <View style={s.thinkPanel}>
          <Text style={s.panelTitle}>🧠 AI Thinking</Text>
          <ScrollView ref={scrollRef} contentContainerStyle={s.stepsList}>
            {steps.length ? steps.map((st,i)=><StepView key={st.id} step={st} idx={i}/>)
              : <Text style={s.empty}>Enter a prompt and click Build</Text>}
            {running && <Text style={s.thinkingDots}>Thinking{''}{'.'.repeat((Math.floor(Date.now()/500)%3)+1)}</Text>}
          </ScrollView>
        </View>
        <View style={s.codePanel}>
          <Text style={s.panelTitle}>💻 Code Output</Text>
          <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.codeContent}>
            {code ? <Text style={s.codeText} selectable>{code}</Text>
              : <Text style={s.empty}>{running?'Waiting for code...':'No code yet'}</Text>}
          </ScrollView>
        </View>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({
  wrap:{flex:1,display:'flex' as any,flexDirection:'column'},
  inputArea:{padding:16,gap:10,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border},
  promptInput:{padding:14,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border2,borderRadius:12,color:C.text,fontSize:14,minHeight:60,maxHeight:120,textAlignVertical:'top' as any},
  langScroll:{maxHeight:36},langChip:{padding:6,12,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:6,marginRight:4},
  langChipActive:{borderColor:C.primary,backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)'},langText:{fontSize:12,color:C.text3},langTextActive:{color:'#60a5fa'},
  startBtn:{backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',borderRadius:10,padding:12,alignItems:'center'},startBtnDis:{opacity:0.6},
  startText:{color:'#000',fontWeight:'700',fontSize:14},
  split:{flex:1,flexDirection:'row' as any},
  thinkPanel:{flex:1,borderRightWidth:1,borderRightColor:C.border,backgroundColor:C.bg},
  codePanel:{flex:1,backgroundColor:'#0d1117'},
  panelTitle:{padding:12,paddingHorizontal:16,fontSize:13,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text2,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border},
  stepsList:{padding:12,gap:6},step:{flexDirection:'row' as any,padding:12,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:10,gap:10,alignItems:'flex-start'},
  stepActive:{borderColor:'#f59e0b',backgroundColor:'rgba(245,158,11,0.05)'},stepDone:{borderColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.3)',opacity:0.7},
  stepLeft:{width:36,alignItems:'center'},stepIcon:{fontSize:20},pulse:{width:8,height:8,borderRadius:4,backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',marginTop:4},
  pulseInner:{width:8,height:8,borderRadius:4,backgroundColor:'#f59e0b'},
  stepRight:{flex:1},stepTitle:{fontSize:14,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text},stepTitleDone:{color:'#86efac'},
  stepDetail:{fontSize:12,color:C.text3,marginTop:2},
  progressTrack:{height:3,backgroundColor:C.border,borderRadius:2,marginTop:6},progressFill:{height:3,backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',borderRadius:2},
  stepStatus:{fontSize:14},thinkingDots:{color:'#f59e0b',fontSize:13,padding:12},
  codeContent:{padding:16},codeText:{color:'#e6edf3',fontSize:13,fontFamily:Platform.OS==='web'?'monospace':undefined,lineHeight:20},
  empty:{color:C.text3,fontSize:13,textAlign:'center',padding:40},
});
""")

ap("bot", """import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
export default function AdminBot() {
  const [cmd,setCmd]=useState('');const [msgs,setMsgs]=useState<any[]>([]);const [loading,setLoading]=useState(false);const ref=useRef<ScrollView>(null);
  const load=async()=>{const r=await api.botMessages();if(r?.messages)setMsgs(r.messages);};
  useEffect(()=>{load();const iv=setInterval(load,10000);return()=>clearInterval(iv);},[]);
  const send=async()=>{const c=cmd.trim();if(!c)return;setCmd('');setLoading(true);await api.botCommand(c);setLoading(false);setTimeout(load,2000);};
  return (<View style={s.wrap}>
    <View style={s.inputRow}><TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Command..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3} value={cmd} onChangeText={setCmd} onSubmitEditing={send} editable={!loading}/><Pressable style={s.btn} onPress={send}><Text style={s.btnText}>→</Text></Pressable></View>
    <ScrollView ref={ref} contentContainerStyle={s.msgs} onContentSizeChange={()=>ref.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true})}>
      {msgs.map((m,i)=><View key={i} style={s.msg}><Text style={s.from}>{m.from}</Text><Text style={s.text}>{m.text||'(non-text)'}</Text></View>)}
      {loading&&<Text style={s.loading}>Sending...</Text>}
    </ScrollView>
  </View>);
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{flex:1,padding:16,gap:10},inputRow:{flexDirection:'row',gap:8},input:{flex:1,padding:12,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border2,borderRadius:10,color:C.text,fontSize:14},btn:{backgroundColor:'#f59e0b',borderRadius:10,width:48,alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center'},btnText:{color:'#000',fontSize:18,fontWeight:'700'},msgs:{gap:0,flexGrow:1},msg:{flexDirection:'row',padding:10,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border,gap:10},from:{color:'#f59e0b',fontWeight:'600',fontSize:13,width:70},text:{color:C.text2,fontSize:13,flex:1},loading:{color:C.text3,fontSize:13,padding:20,textAlign:'center'}});
""")

w("app/(app)/_layout.tsx", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, StyleSheet, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { useRouter, usePathname, Slot } from 'expo-router';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';

const TABS = [
  { path:'', icon:'📊', label:'Dashboard' },
  { path:'/builder', icon:'🏗️', label:'Builder' },
  { path:'/chat', icon:'🧠', label:'GLM Chat' },
  { path:'/plans', icon:'💎', label:'Plans' },
  { path:'/profile', icon:'👤', label:'Profile' },
];

export default function AppLayout() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const pathname = usePathname();
  const [ok, setOk] = useState(false);
  const [plan, setPlan] = useState('free');
  useEffect(() => {
    api.check().then(r => {
      if (!r?.auth) { router.replace('/login'); return; }
      if (r.role === 'admin') { router.replace('/(admin)'); return; }
      setOk(true); setPlan(r.plan || 'free');
    }).catch(() => router.replace('/login'));
  }, []);
  const logout = async () => { await api.logout(); router.replace('/login'); };
  const active = TABS.findIndex(t => (pathname==='/(app)'&&t.path==='')||pathname==='/(app)'+t.path);
  if (!ok) return <View style={{flex:1,backgroundColor:C.bg}} />;

  if (Platform.OS === 'web') return (
    <View style={s.webWrap}>
      <View style={s.sidebar}>
        <View style={s.sideHead}><Text style={s.sideLogo}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI</Text><Text style={s.sideVer}>📦 {plan.toUpperCase()}</Text></View>
        {TABS.map((t,i) => (
          <Pressable key={t.path} style={[s.sideLink,active===i&&s.sideLinkActive]} onPress={()=>router.push('/(app)'+t.path)}>
            <Text style={[s.sideLinkText,active===i&&s.sideLinkTextActive]}>{t.icon} {t.label}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
        <View style={{flex:1}} />
        <Pressable style={s.logoutBtn} onPress={logout}><Text style={s.logoutText}>🚪 Logout</Text></Pressable>
      </View>
      <View style={s.main}>
        <View style={s.topbar}><Text style={s.topTitle}>{TABS[active]?.icon} {TABS[active]?.label}</Text><Text style={s.topStatus}>📦 {plan.toUpperCase()}</Text></View>
        <View style={s.content}><Slot /></View>
      </View>
    </View>
  );
  return (
    <View style={s.mobWrap}>
      <View style={s.mobHead}><Text style={s.mobTitle}>🤖 WHOAMISEC AI</Text><Text style={s.mobPlan}>{plan.toUpperCase()}</Text><Pressable onPress={logout}><Text style={s.mobOut}>🚪</Text></Pressable></View>
      <View style={s.mobContent}><Slot /></View>
      <View style={s.tabBar}>
        {TABS.map((t,i) => (
          <Pressable key={t.path} style={[s.tabItem,active===i&&s.tabActive]} onPress={()=>router.push('/(app)'+t.path)}>
            <Text style={s.tabIcon}>{t.icon}</Text><Text style={[s.tabLabel,active===i&&s.tabLabelActive]}>{t.label}</Text>
          </Pressable>
        ))}
      </View>
    </View>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({
  webWrap:{flex:1,flexDirection:'row',backgroundColor:C.bg},sidebar:{width:C.sidebarW,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderRightWidth:1,borderRightColor:C.border,paddingTop:20,paddingHorizontal:10,flexShrink:0},
  sideHead:{paddingBottom:16,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border,marginBottom:8,paddingHorizontal:8},sideLogo:{fontSize:20,fontWeight:'700',color:'#60a5fa'},sideVer:{fontSize:10,color:C.text3,backgroundColor:C.surface2,padding:2,6,borderRadius:4,marginTop:4,alignSelf:'flex-start' as any},
  sideLink:{paddingVertical:10,paddingHorizontal:12,borderRadius:8,marginBottom:1},sideLinkActive:{backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)'},sideLinkText:{fontSize:13,color:C.text2,fontWeight:'500'},sideLinkTextActive:{color:'#60a5fa'},
  logoutBtn:{padding:10,backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)',borderRadius:8,alignItems:'center',marginBottom:8},logoutText:{color:'#fca5a5',fontWeight:'500',fontSize:12},
  main:{flex:1,minWidth:0},topbar:{flexDirection:'row',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'space-between',padding:14,paddingHorizontal:24,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border,backgroundColor:'rgba(10,14,26,0.9)'},topTitle:{fontSize:17,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text},topStatus:{fontSize:12,color:C.primary},
  content:{flex:1,overflow:'auto' as any},
  mobWrap:{flex:1,backgroundColor:C.bg},mobHead:{flexDirection:'row',alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'space-between',padding:14,paddingTop:48,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border},mobTitle:{fontSize:18,fontWeight:'700',color:'#60a5fa'},mobPlan:{fontSize:11,color:C.primary,backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)',padding:3,8,borderRadius:4},mobOut:{fontSize:18},
  mobContent:{flex:1},tabBar:{flexDirection:'row',backgroundColor:C.surface,borderTopWidth:1,borderTopColor:C.border,paddingBottom:4},
  tabItem:{flex:1,paddingVertical:6,alignItems:'center',gap:1},tabActive:{backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)'},tabIcon:{fontSize:18},tabLabel:{fontSize:9,color:C.text3},tabLabelActive:{color:'#60a5fa'},
});
""")

def us(name, code): w(f"app/(app)/{name}.tsx", code)

us("index", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, ScrollView, Pressable, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import { getPlan, formatLimit, PLANS } from '@/constants/plans';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';

export default function UserDash() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState<any>(null);
  const [usage, setUsage] = useState<any>(null);
  const load = async () => { const [p, u] = await Promise.all([api.profile(), api.usage()]); if(p) setProfile(p); if(u) setUsage(u); };
  useEffect(() => { load(); const iv = setInterval(load, 10000); return () => clearInterval(iv); }, []);

  const plan = getPlan(usage?.planId || 'free');
  const currentPlan = PLANS.find(p => p.id === (usage?.planId || 'free'));

  const pctGlm = usage && plan ? (plan.limits.glmCalls === -1 ? 0 : Math.min(100, Math.round(usage.usage.glmCalls / plan.limits.glmCalls * 100))) : 0;
  const pctCode = usage && plan ? (plan.limits.codeGens === -1 ? 0 : Math.min(100, Math.round(usage.usage.codeGens / plan.limits.codeGens * 100))) : 0;

  return (
    <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.planBadge}><Text style={s.planBadgeText}>{currentPlan?.icon} {currentPlan?.name} Plan</Text>
        {currentPlan?.price ? <Text style={s.planPrice}>${currentPlan.price}/{currentPlan.period}</Text> : <Text style={s.planPrice}>FREE</Text>}
      </View>
      <Text style={s.welcome}>Welcome, {profile?.name}!</Text>
      {profile?.broadcasts?.length ? profile.broadcasts.slice(0,3).map((b:any,i)=><View key={i} style={s.broadcast}><Text style={s.bcText}>📢 {b.msg}</Text></View>) : null}

      <View style={s.usageCard}>
        <Text style={s.usageTitle}>📊 Usage This Period</Text>
        <View style={s.barWrap}><Text style={s.barLabel}>🧠 GLM Calls: {usage?.usage.glmCalls||0}/{formatLimit(plan?.limits.glmCalls||0)}</Text><View style={s.barTrack}><View style={[s.barFill,{width:pctGlm+'%',backgroundColor:pctGlm>80?C.danger:pctGlm>50?C.warning:C.success}]} /></View></View>
        <View style={s.barWrap}><Text style={s.barLabel}>💻 Code Gens: {usage?.usage.codeGens||0}/{formatLimit(plan?.limits.codeGens||0)}</Text><View style={s.barTrack}><View style={[s.barFill,{width:pctCode+'%',backgroundColor:pctCode>80?C.danger:pctCode>50?C.warning:C.success}]} /></View></View>
        <Text style={s.barLabel}>📁 Storage: {(usage?.usage.storageUsed||0)/1024:.1}MB / {formatLimit(plan?.limits.fileStorage||0)}MB</Text>
        <Text style={s.barLabel}>🔧 Auto-Repair: {plan?.limits.autoRepairIter||0} iterations</Text>
        <Text style={s.barLabel}>🌐 Languages: {plan?.limits.languages?.[0]==='ALL'?'All 13':(plan?.limits.languages?.length||0)+' languages'}</Text>
      </View>

      {usage?.planId !== 'admin' && (
        <Pressable style={s.upgradeBtn} onPress={() => router.push('/(app)/plans')}>
          <Text style={s.upgradeText}>💎 Change Plan</Text>
        </Pressable>
      )}
    </ScrollView>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{padding:20,gap:14},planBadge:{backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:14,padding:16,alignItems:'center'},planBadgeText:{fontSize:18,fontWeight:'700',color:C.primary},planPrice:{fontSize:13,color:C.text2},welcome:{fontSize:22,fontWeight:'700',color:C.text},broadcast:{backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)',borderWidth:1,borderColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.2)',borderRadius:10,padding:12},bcText:{fontSize:13,color:'#93c5fd'},usageCard:{backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:14,padding:16,gap:10},usageTitle:{fontSize:15,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text},barWrap:{gap:4},barLabel:{fontSize:12,color:C.text2},barTrack:{height:6,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderRadius:3,overflow:'hidden'},barFill:{height:'100%',borderRadius:3},upgradeBtn:{backgroundColor:'rgba(139,92,246,0.15)',borderWidth:1,borderColor:'rgba(139,92,246,0.3)',borderRadius:12,padding:14,alignItems:'center'},upgradeText:{color:'#a78bfa',fontWeight:'700',fontSize:14}});
""")

# USER BUILDER (limited based on plan)
us("builder", """import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Platform, Alert } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import { getPlan, canUse } from '@/constants/plans';

export default function UserBuilder() {
  const [prompt,setPrompt]=useState('');const [lang,setLang]=useState('python');
  const [sessionId,setSessionId]=useState('');const [steps,setSteps]=useState<any[]>([]);
  const [code,setCode]=useState('');const [running,setRunning]=useState(false);
  const [planId,setPlanId]=useState('free');const pollRef=useRef<any>(null);

  useEffect(()=>{api.usage().then(r=>{if(r)setPlanId(r.planId);});},[]);

  const plan = getPlan(planId);
  const canBuild = canUse('builder_realtime', planId) || canUse('builder_basic', planId);
  const isFull = canUse('builder_realtime', planId);
  const availableLangs = plan?.limits.languages?.[0]==='ALL' ? ['python','javascript','typescript','go','rust','cpp','java','csharp','ruby','swift','kotlin','zig','lua'] : plan?.limits.languages || ['python'];

  const start = async () => {
    if (!canBuild) { Alert.alert('⬆️ Upgrade', 'Builder requires Starter plan or higher.'); return; }
    if (!availableLangs.includes(lang)) { Alert.alert('❌', 'Language not available on your plan.'); return; }
    if (!prompt.trim() || running) return;
    setRunning(true); setCode('');
    const res = await api.builderGenerate(prompt, lang);
    if (res?.limitReached) { Alert.alert('⬆️ Limit', 'Code generation limit reached.'); setRunning(false); return; }
    if (!res?.sessionId) { setRunning(false); return; }
    setSessionId(res.sessionId); setSteps(res.steps);
    const poll = async () => {
      const r = await api.builderStream(res.sessionId);
      if (r?.steps) setSteps(r.steps);
      if (r?.code) setCode(r.code);
      if (r?.status === 'complete') { setRunning(false); return; }
      pollRef.current = setTimeout(poll, 600);
    };
    poll();
  };
  useEffect(()=>()=>{if(pollRef.current)clearTimeout(pollRef.current);},[]);

  if (!canBuild) return (
    <View style={s.upgradeWrap}>
      <Text style={s.upIcon}>🏗️</Text>
      <Text style={s.upTitle}>Builder Not Available</Text>
      <Text style={s.upDesc}>Upgrade to Starter ($9/mo) or higher to use the AI Code Builder.</Text>
      <Text style={s.upFeat}>Starter: 5 languages, 100 gens/mo</Text>
      <Text style={s.upFeat}>Pro: 8 languages, 500 gens/mo, Realtime</Text>
    </View>
  );

  return (
    <View style={s.wrap}>
      <View style={s.inputArea}>
        <TextInput style={s.promptInput} placeholder="What do you want to build?" placeholderTextColor={C.text3} value={prompt} onChangeText={setPrompt} multiline editable={!running} />
        <ScrollView horizontal showsHorizontalScrollIndicator={false}>
          {availableLangs.map(l=><Pressable key={l} style={[s.langChip,lang===l&&s.langChipActive]} onPress={()=>setLang(l)}><Text style={[s.langText,lang===l&&s.langTextActive]}>{l}</Text></Pressable>)}
        </ScrollView>
        <Pressable style={s.startBtn} onPress={start} disabled={running}><Text style={s.startText}>{running?'⏳ Building...':'🚀 Build'}</Text></Pressable>
        {!isFull && <Text style={s.limited}>⚡ Basic mode — upgrade for Realtime Thinking</Text>}
      </View>
      {isFull ? (
        <View style={s.split}>
          <View style={s.thinkPanel}><Text style={s.panelTitle}>🧠 AI Thinking</Text>
            <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.stepsList}>
              {steps.map((st:any,i)=><View key={st.id} style={[s.step,st.status==='running'&&s.stepRun,st.status==='done'&&s.stepDone]}>
                <Text style={s.stepIcon}>{st.icon}</Text><View style={{flex:1}}><Text style={s.stepTitle}>{st.title}</Text><Text style={s.stepDetail}>{st.detail}</Text></View>
                <Text style={s.stepStatus}>{st.status==='done'?'✅':st.status==='running'?'⏳':'⏸'}</Text>
              </View>)}
              {running&&<Text style={s.dots}>Thinking{'.'.repeat((Math.floor(Date.now()/500)%3)+1)}</Text>}
            </ScrollView>
          </View>
          <View style={s.codePanel}><Text style={s.panelTitle}>💻 Code</Text>
            <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.codeContent}><Text style={s.codeText} selectable>{code||'Waiting...'}</Text></ScrollView>
          </View>
        </View>
      ) : (
        <View style={s.codeOnly}><Text style={s.panelTitle}>💻 Generated Code</Text>
          <ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.codeContent}><Text style={s.codeText} selectable>{code||'Enter prompt and click Build'}</Text></ScrollView>
        </View>
      )}
    </View>
  );
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{flex:1,display:'flex' as any,flexDirection:'column'},inputArea:{padding:16,gap:10,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border},promptInput:{padding:14,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border2,borderRadius:12,color:C.text,fontSize:14,minHeight:60,maxHeight:120,textAlignVertical:'top' as any},langChip:{padding:6,12,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:6,marginRight:4},langChipActive:{borderColor:C.primary,backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)'},langText:{fontSize:12,color:C.text3},langTextActive:{color:'#60a5fa'},startBtn:{backgroundColor:C.primary2,borderRadius:10,padding:12,alignItems:'center'},startText:{color:'#fff',fontWeight:'700',fontSize:14},limited:{fontSize:11,color:C.warning,textAlign:'center'},split:{flex:1,flexDirection:'row' as any},thinkPanel:{flex:1,borderRightWidth:1,borderRightColor:C.border,backgroundColor:C.bg},codePanel:{flex:1,backgroundColor:'#0d1117'},panelTitle:{padding:12,paddingHorizontal:16,fontSize:13,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text2,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderBottomWidth:1,borderBottomColor:C.border},stepsList:{padding:12,gap:6},step:{flexDirection:'row' as any,padding:10,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:8,gap:8,alignItems:'center'},stepRun:{borderColor:C.warning},stepDone:{opacity:0.6},stepIcon:{fontSize:18},stepTitle:{fontSize:13,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text},stepDetail:{fontSize:11,color:C.text3},stepStatus:{fontSize:13},dots:{color:C.warning,fontSize:13,padding:12},codeContent:{padding:16},codeText:{color:'#e6edf3',fontSize:13,fontFamily:Platform.OS==='web'?'monospace':undefined,lineHeight:20},codeOnly:{flex:1,backgroundColor:'#0d1117'},upgradeWrap:{flex:1,alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',gap:12,padding:40},upIcon:{fontSize:48},upTitle:{fontSize:20,fontWeight:'700',color:C.text},upDesc:{fontSize:14,color:C.text3,textAlign:'center',maxWidth:300},upFeat:{fontSize:13,color:C.text2}},);
""")

us("chat", """import { useState, useRef } from 'react';
import { View, Text, TextInput, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, KeyboardAvoidingView, Platform } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
export default function UserChat() {
  const [msgs,setMsgs]=useState<any[]>([{role:'system',content:'GLM Ready. Any prompt type accepted.'}]);
  const [input,setInput]=useState('');const [loading,setLoading]=useState(false);const ref=useRef<ScrollView>(null);
  const send=async()=>{const t=input.trim();if(!t||loading)return;setInput('');setMsgs(p=>[...p,{role:'user',content:t}]);setLoading(true);
    const r=await api.glmChat(t);
    if(r?.limitReached){setMsgs(p=>[...p,{role:'assistant',content:'⚠️ GLM call limit reached. Upgrade your plan.'}]);}
    else{setMsgs(p=>[...p,{role:'assistant',content:r?.response||r?.error||'Error'}]);}
    setLoading(false);setTimeout(()=>ref.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true}),100);};
  return (<KeyboardAvoidingView style={s.wrap} behavior={Platform.OS==='ios'?'padding':undefined}>
    <ScrollView ref={ref} style={s.chat} contentContainerStyle={s.chatInner} onContentSizeChange={()=>ref.current?.scrollToEnd({animated:true})}>
      {msgs.map((m,i)=><View key={i} style={[s.msg,m.role==='user'?s.msgUser:m.role==='system'?s.msgSys:s.msgBot]}><Text style={s.msgText} selectable>{m.content}</Text></View>)}
      {loading&&<View style={s.msgSys}><Text style={s.msgText}>Thinking...</Text></View>}
    </ScrollView>
    <View style={s.inputBar}><TextInput style={s.input} placeholder="Ask anything..." placeholderTextColor={C.text3} value={input} onChangeText={setInput} onSubmitEditing={send} editable={!loading} multiline />
      <Pressable style={s.sendBtn} onPress={send} disabled={loading}><Text style={s.sendTxt}>→</Text></Pressable></View>
  </KeyboardAvoidingView>);
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{flex:1},chat:{flex:1,backgroundColor:C.bg,margin:16,borderRadius:10,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border},chatInner:{padding:12,gap:8,flexGrow:1},msg:{maxWidth:'85%',padding:12,borderRadius:12},msgUser:{alignSelf:'flex-end',backgroundColor:'#1e3a5f'},msgBot:{alignSelf:'flex-start',backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border},msgSys:{alignSelf:'center',backgroundColor:'transparent'},msgText:{color:'#e2e8f0',fontSize:14,lineHeight:20},inputBar:{flexDirection:'row',padding:12,gap:8,backgroundColor:C.surface,borderTopWidth:1,borderTopColor:C.border},input:{flex:1,padding:12,backgroundColor:C.bg,borderRadius:10,color:C.text,fontSize:14,maxHeight:100},sendBtn:{backgroundColor:C.primary2,borderRadius:10,width:48,alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center'},sendTxt:{color:'#fff',fontSize:18,fontWeight:'700'}});
""")

us("plans", """import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, ScrollView, StyleSheet, Alert } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import { PLANS, formatLimit, FEATURE_NAMES } from '@/constants/plans';
export default function UserPlans() {
  const [currentPlan, setCurrentPlan] = useState('free');
  useEffect(()=>{api.usage().then(r=>{if(r)setCurrentPlan(r.planId);});},[]);
  const subscribe = async (planId: string) => {
    if (planId === currentPlan) return;
    const plan = PLANS.find(p=>p.id===planId);
    if (plan?.price > 0) {
      Alert.alert('💎 Subscribe', `Upgrade to ${plan.name} — $${plan.price}/${plan.period}?\\n\\n(In production: Stripe integration)`, [
        {text:'Cancel',style:'cancel'},{text:'Subscribe',onPress:async()=>{const r=await api.subscribe(planId);if(r?.ok){setCurrentPlan(planId);Alert.alert('✅',r.message);}else Alert.alert('❌',r?.error||'Failed');}}
      ]);
    } else {
      const r = await api.subscribe(planId);
      if(r?.ok){setCurrentPlan(planId);Alert.alert('✅',r.message);}
    }
  };
  return (<ScrollView contentContainerStyle={s.wrap}>
    <Text style={s.title}>💎 Choose Your Plan</Text>
    <Text style={s.sub}>Current: {PLANS.find(p=>p.id===currentPlan)?.icon} {PLANS.find(p=>p.id===currentPlan)?.name}</Text>
    {PLANS.filter(p=>p.id!=='admin').map(p=>(
      <Pressable key={p.id} style={[s.card,{borderColor:p.id===currentPlan?p.color+'88':C.border}]} onPress={()=>subscribe(p.id)}>
        <View style={s.cardHead}><Text style={s.icon}>{p.icon}</Text><View><Text style={[s.name,{color:p.color}]}>{p.name}{p.id===currentPlan?' ✓':''}</Text><Text style={s.price}>{p.price===0?'FREE':'$'+p.price+'/'+p.period}</Text></View>
          {p.popular&&<View style={s.pop}><Text style={s.popText}>POPULAR</Text></View>}
        </View>
        <Text style={s.desc}>{p.description}</Text>
        <View style={s.limits}>
          <Text style={s.lim}>🧠 {formatLimit(p.limits.glmCalls)} GLM calls</Text>
          <Text style={s.lim}>💻 {formatLimit(p.limits.codeGens)} code gens</Text>
          <Text style={s.lim}>🌐 {p.limits.languages[0]==='ALL'?'All 13':p.limits.languages.length+' languages'}</Text>
          <Text style={s.lim}>📁 {formatLimit(p.limits.fileStorage)}MB storage</Text>
        </View>
        <Text style={s.featsTitle}>Features:</Text>
        {p.features.slice(0,6).map(f=><Text key={f} style={s.feat}>✅ {FEATURE_NAMES[f]||f}</Text>)}
        {p.features.length>6&&<Text style={s.more}>+{p.features.length-6} more...</Text>}
      </Pressable>
    ))}
  </ScrollView>);
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{padding:20,gap:14},title:{fontSize:20,fontWeight:'700',color:C.text},sub:{fontSize:13,color:C.text3},card:{backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:2,borderRadius:16,padding:20,gap:10},cardHead:{flexDirection:'row',alignItems:'center',gap:12},icon:{fontSize:30},name:{fontSize:18,fontWeight:'700'},price:{fontSize:13,color:C.text2},pop:{backgroundColor:'#3b82f6',borderRadius:6,padding:3,8,marginLeft:'auto'},popText:{color:'#fff',fontSize:10,fontWeight:'700'},desc:{fontSize:13,color:C.text3},limits:{backgroundColor:C.bg,borderRadius:10,padding:12,gap:3},lim:{fontSize:12,color:C.text2},featsTitle:{fontSize:13,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text,marginTop:4},feat:{fontSize:12,color:'#86efac'},more:{fontSize:11,color:C.text3}});
""")

us("profile", """import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { View, Text, Pressable, StyleSheet } from 'react-native';
import { api } from '@/lib/api-client';
import { C } from '@/constants/theme';
import { useRouter } from 'expo-router';
export default function Profile() {
  const [p,setP]=useState<any>(null);const router=useRouter();
  useEffect(()=>{api.profile().then(r=>setP(r));},[]);
  const logout=async()=>{await api.logout();router.replace('/login');};
  return (<View style={s.wrap}>
    <View style={s.avatar}><Text style={s.avatarText}>{(p?.name||'?')[0].toUpperCase()}</Text></View>
    <Text style={s.name}>{p?.name}</Text>
    <Text style={s.email}>{p?.email}</Text>
    <Text style={s.plan}>📦 Plan: {(p?.plan||'free').toUpperCase()}</Text>
    <Text style={s.joined}>Joined: {p?.createdAt?.split('T')[0]}</Text>
    {p?.broadcasts?.length?<>
      <Text style={s.bcTitle}>📢 Messages</Text>
      {p.broadcasts.slice(0,5).map((b:any,i)=><View key={i} style={s.bc}><Text style={s.bcText}>{b.msg}</Text><Text style={s.bcTime}>{b.time?.split('T')[1]?.slice(0,5)}</Text></View>)}
    </>:null}
    <Pressable style={s.logoutBtn} onPress={logout}><Text style={s.logoutText}>🚪 Logout</Text></Pressable>
  </View>);
}
const s=StyleSheet.create({wrap:{padding:20,gap:12,alignItems:'center'},avatar:{width:64,height:64,borderRadius:32,backgroundColor:C.primary,alignItems:'center',justifyContent:'center',marginTop:20},avatarText:{fontSize:28,fontWeight:'700',color:'#fff'},name:{fontSize:22,fontWeight:'700',color:C.text},email:{fontSize:14,color:C.text2},plan:{fontSize:14,color:C.primary,fontWeight:'600',backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.1)',padding:6,16,borderRadius:8,marginTop:4},joined:{fontSize:12,color:C.text3},bcTitle:{fontSize:15,fontWeight:'600',color:C.text,alignSelf:'flex-start',marginTop:16},bc:{backgroundColor:C.surface,borderWidth:1,borderColor:C.border,borderRadius:8,padding:12,width:'100%',gap:4},bcText:{fontSize:13,color:C.text2,flex:1},bcTime:{fontSize:11,color:C.text3},logoutBtn:{backgroundColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)',borderRadius:10,padding:12,width:'100%',alignItems:'center',marginTop:20},logoutText:{color:'#fca5a5',fontWeight:'600',fontSize:14}});
""")

w("README.md", """
